> **REPO & VERSION CONTEXT (read first):** You audit **CRM2 (v2)** ‚Äî a GREENFIELD rebuild living in `crm2/`, which has its **OWN git repo** (`github.com/acsdeveloper2025/acs-crm-2`) even though it sits INSIDE the v1 monorepo directory `CRM-APP-MONOREPO-PROD/` (v1 git-ignores it). **THREE separate git repos share that one folder:**
> 1. **v1 (legacy, in prod)** ‚Äî repo `acsdeveloper2025/CRM-APP-MONOREPO-PROD`; the live app = `CRM-BACKEND/` + `CRM-FRONTEND/`. ‚öÝÔ∏è `acs_db_final_version.sql` at the v1 root is the **v1** schema ‚Äî NEVER audit v2 against it; the v2 schema is `crm2/db/v2/migrations/` (+ the live test/dev DBs).
> 2. **v2 (this, greenfield build)** ‚Äî repo `acsdeveloper2025/acs-crm-2`; everything you review is here under `crm2/`.
> 3. **mobile (field-executive app)** ‚Äî `crm-mobile-native/`, repo `acsdeveloper2025/crm-mobile-native`, React-Native, **ALREADY DEVELOPED & currently CONNECTED TO v1** (`https://crm.allcheckservices.com/api/mobile`). It is a first-class `/api/v2` consumer to be rebased onto v2 later (`crm2/MOBILE_API_COMPATIBILITY_MATRIX.md`) ‚Äî **never break the mobile contract** (ADR-0012).

# Ledger ‚Äî Security Auditor

Charter: AGENT_ORG.md row 4. RBAC default-deny + server-side scope ¬∑ IDOR/ownership ¬∑ injection ¬∑
authn/JWT ¬∑ secrets ¬∑ PII/DPDP. SoT: SECURITY_STANDARDS ¬∑ SECURITY_GUIDE ¬∑ ADR-0014 (auth) ¬∑
project_rbac_hierarchy_model (6 roles) ¬∑ gitleaks.

## Standing invariants
- **Default-deny RBAC**, 6 roles; perms granted explicitly (Object.values auto-includes SUPER_ADMIN).
  Server is the real gate (FE role checks are cosmetic).
- **No raw user text in SQL.** Parameterize values; column/identifier names that can't be bound
  (`ORDER BY`) MUST come from a server-side whitelist.
- JWT: stateless access (15m) + refresh denylist/rotation; `JWT_SECRET` has a dev default only.
- Secrets never committed (gitleaks gate). PII columns flagged `pii_sensitive`; consent/retention day-1.

## Key controls (verify not weakened)
- **üîí Sort-injection control (added DataGrid slice):** `platform/pagination.ts resolvePage` maps `sortBy`
  ‚Üí `spec.sortMap[...]` (whitelist) and falls back to `defaultSort` for unknown input; `sortOrder` pinned
  asc/desc. So `ORDER BY ${sortColumn} ${sortOrder}` is injection-safe. **DON'T-REGRESS:** any new list's
  `PageSpec.sortMap` must contain ONLY real column names; never interpolate a raw `sortBy` into SQL.
- `validateTaskRecordAccess` on task read routes (VT‚Üíuuid; IDOR-safe) ‚Äî operations concern.

## Log
- **2026-06-06 ¬∑ DataGrid + pagination (`4e7a8fd`)** ‚Äî sort-injection control CONFIRMED safe (unit +
  integration tests cover `sortBy='name; DROP TABLE‚Ä¶'` ‚Üí falls back to default). No secrets. RBAC unchanged
  (list endpoints keep their existing `masterdata.view` perms). OPEN: re-verify the whitelist on every
  rolled-out list's PageSpec; check filter params are also whitelisted/parameterized.
- **2026-06-06 ¬∑ DataGrid server-pagination Slice 1 ‚Äî `users`/`verification_units`/`report_templates` lists ‚Üí paginated envelope** ‚Äî **VERDICT: PASS.**
  - (a) **Sort-injection ‚Äî SAFE.** All three services define a `PageSpec.sortMap` of apiField‚Üíreal-column only (service.ts:`USER_PAGE_SPEC`/`VU_PAGE_SPEC`/`TEMPLATE_PAGE_SPEC`); `resolvePage` (pagination.ts:50-55) whitelists `sortBy` via `hasOwnProperty(sortMap)` else falls back to `defaultSort`, and `sortColumn` is `sortMap[sortBy]` (never raw input). `sortOrder` pinned to `'asc'|'desc'` (pagination.ts:57-59). The `ORDER BY ${o.sortColumn} ${o.sortOrder}` interpolations (users repo:459, vu repo:721, templates repo:214) therefore receive only trusted strings ‚Äî the secondary `id`/`u.id` tiebreaker is a literal. Tests assert `sortBy=name;DROP TABLE‚Ä¶` ‚Üí 200 + default sort (users.api.test.ts:351, vu:618, templates:108). `search` parameterized via `ILIKE $n` with `%‚Ä¶%` bound as a value (users repo:439, vu repo:707, templates repo:201) ‚Äî not interpolated. `limit>500`‚Üí400 `LIMIT_TOO_LARGE`, `limit<1`‚Üí400 `INVALID_LIMIT` (pagination.ts:41-42); tested.
  - (b) **RBAC unchanged.** routes.ts untouched (git diff name-only: no route/router files): GET `/` still `authorize(USER_VIEW)` / `MASTERDATA_VIEW` / `TEMPLATE_VIEW`; writes still `*_MANAGE`. Default-deny intact (controllers only moved query-parsing into the service; no auth path touched).
  - (c) **IDOR/scope ‚Äî n/a, no regression.** Admin master-data, SUPER_ADMIN-perm-scoped reads; no per-tenant/per-owner row exists to leak. No new cross-entity join added (users LEFT JOINs `users m` for reports_to_name ‚Äî pre-existing).
  - (d) **No new PII exposure.** users SELECT column list unchanged from prior (id/username/name/email/role/reports_to/‚Ä¶ + reports_to_name); no new sensitive column. `filters` echo in `buildPage` only reflects server-PARSED values (role validated vs USER_ROLES, active coerced bool, search=trimmed string), not arbitrary raw query keys.
  - (e) **`req.query as Record<string,unknown>` cast ‚Äî safe.** Every consumer path is typed/validated: `resolvePage` (whitelist+clamp), explicit `parseType`/USER_ROLES membership check, `active==='true'|'false'` coercion, `kind`/`category` `typeof==='string'` guard. Nothing from the cast reaches SQL un-whitelisted or un-parameterized. No `console.*`/secrets in diff (scanned).
  - SHOULD-FIX (none blocking): `kind`/`category` filters (vu service:771-774) pass any string straight to a parameterized `= $n` ‚Äî value-bound so injection-safe, but unlike `role`/`templateType` they're not enum-validated, so a bogus value just returns 0 rows (cosmetic, not a security issue). Note for FE caps: CpvPage/RateManagementPage now request `limit=200` then `.then(r=>r.items)` ‚Äî within the 500 cap, fine.
  - OPEN (carried): re-verify `sortMap` contains ONLY real columns on every future list rollout; never interpolate raw `sortBy`. Watch that `filters` echo never starts reflecting unparsed raw query keys.
- **2026-06-06 ¬∑ DataGrid server-pagination Slice 3 ‚Äî `cases` list ‚Üí paginated envelope** ‚Äî **VERDICT: PASS.**
  - (a) **Sort-injection ‚Äî SAFE.** `CASE_PAGE_SPEC.sortMap` (service.ts:14-26) maps apiField‚Üíserver-defined literal SQL columns only (`caseNumber‚Üícs.case_number`, `clientName‚Üícl.name` (JOIN alias), `productName‚Üíp.name`, `primaryName‚Üípa.name`, etc.) ‚Äî all are trusted literals, none derived from user input. `resolvePage` (pagination.ts:50-55) whitelists `sortBy` via `hasOwnProperty(sortMap)` else falls back to `defaultSort='createdAt'`; `sortColumn = sortMap[sortBy]` (never raw). `sortOrder` pinned to `'asc'|'desc'` (pagination.ts:57-59). The interpolation `ORDER BY ${o.sortColumn} ${o.sortOrder}, cs.id ${o.sortOrder}` (repo:233) receives only trusted strings; the `cs.id` tiebreaker is a literal. Injection test PRESENT and asserts default fallback: `sortBy=case_number;DROP TABLE cases` ‚Üí 200 + `sort.sortBy==='createdAt'` (cases.api.test.ts:296-302). `search` parameterized via `ILIKE $n` with `%‚Ä¶%` bound as a VALUE in both the data query and the COUNT query (repo:217-220) ‚Äî never interpolated. `status` validated against `CASE_STATUSES` membership (service.ts:67-70) before being bound as `$n` (repo:208-210). `clientId` coerced via `Number.isInteger && >0` else dropped (service.ts:72-73), bound as `$n` (repo:212-214). `limit>500`‚Üí400 `LIMIT_TOO_LARGE` (pagination.ts:42; tested cases.api.test.ts:289-293), `limit<1`‚Üí400 `INVALID_LIMIT`.
  - (b) **RBAC unchanged.** routes.ts NOT in diff (verified): GET `/api/v2/cases` still `authorize(CASE_VIEW)`; writes `POST /` `CASE_CREATE`, `POST /:id/tasks` `CASE_CREATE`, assign/unassign `CASE_ASSIGN`. Controller only stopped pre-parsing and now forwards `req.query` to the service (controller.ts:62) which does the validation/whitelisting ‚Äî no auth path touched. Default-deny intact.
  - (c) **Scope/IDOR ‚Äî PRE-EXISTING gap, NOT a regression of this slice.** The cases LIST returns ALL cases to any `case.view` holder ‚Äî there is NO per-user/territory/portfolio row scoping on the list. CONFIRMED pre-existing: the prior bare-array `repo.list` (old code: `ORDER BY cs.created_at DESC LIMIT 200`, no scope WHERE) also returned all cases; this slice only adds pagination/sort/count over the same unscoped query. Recorded as an OPEN operational item (row-level case scope deferred ‚Äî same class as the assignment territory gap B-20), **not a blocker for this slice.**
  - (d) **No new PII exposure.** `CASE_VIEW_SELECT` UNCHANGED (not in diff) ‚Äî still exposes pre-existing `primary_name`/`primary_mobile`/`primary_pan`; no new sensitive column added. The new COUNT query (repo:222-227) joins only `cases`+`case_applicants` and selects `count(*)::int` (no PII columns). `filters` echo (service.ts:84-88) reflects only server-PARSED values (status validated, clientId coerced int, search trimmed) ‚Äî never raw query keys. No `console.*`/secrets/`SELECT *` in diff (scanned).
  - (e) **COUNT-query join correctness (security-adjacent).** COUNT uses `LEFT JOIN case_applicants pa ‚Ä¶ AND pa.is_primary`; one primary per case (partial-unique) so no row multiplication ‚Üí totalCount is honest (no count inflation that could mask/leak via pagination math). Same WHERE clause + params reused for COUNT and data query (consistent filtering).
  - OPEN (NEW, carried): **cases LIST has no row-level scope** ‚Äî any `case.view` holder sees every case (pre-existing; deferred operational row-scope, sibling of B-20 assignment territory gap). Re-verify when row-scoping lands that it applies to BOTH the data query and the COUNT query (else totalCount leaks existence of out-of-scope rows).
  - OPEN (carried): re-verify `sortMap` = real columns only on every future list; never interpolate raw `sortBy`; `filters` echo must stay parsed-values-only.
- **2026-06-06 ¬∑ Slice 1B ‚Äî B-22 options endpoints (`GET /{clients,products,verification-units,users}/options`)** ‚Äî **VERDICT: PASS.**
  - (a) **Injection ‚Äî N/A, zero attack surface.** All four `repository.options()` are raw SELECTs taking **no arguments** (`query<‚Ä¶>(sql)` with no params array) ‚Äî no `sortBy`/`search`/`limit`/`kind` from the request reaches them. `ORDER BY` is a HARDCODED literal in every one: clients/products `ORDER BY name ASC` (repo:57-59), VU `ORDER BY sort_order ASC, name ASC` (repo:80-82), users `ORDER BY name ASC` (repo:95-97). Service is a pure passthrough (`options(): Promise<‚Ä¶> { return repo.options(); }`), controller is `res.json(await svc.options())` with no `req` read (`_req` arg). Nothing interpolated, nothing bound ‚Äî injection-proof by construction.
  - (b) **RBAC ‚Äî same gate as the list it feeds, confirmed in each routes.ts.** clients/products/VU `/options` mount `authorize(PERMISSIONS.MASTERDATA_VIEW)` (clients routes:13, products:13, VU:13) ‚Äî identical to their `GET /`. users `/options` mounts `authorize(PERMISSIONS.USER_VIEW)` (users routes:13) ‚Äî identical to its `GET /`. Default-deny intact; no perm weakened, no write path touched. Tests assert the gate: 401 unauth on all four; **BACKEND_USER 200** for clients/products/VU (holds MASTERDATA_VIEW) and **BACKEND_USER 403 for users** (lacks USER_VIEW ‚Äî clients.api.test:142-145, products:144-147, vu:170-173, users:153-156).
  - (c) **Route ordering ‚Äî verified non-shadowed.** clients/products/VU register `/options` BEFORE `/:id` (literal beats param in Express; comment present in each) so it is never captured as `id="options"` ‚Üí no 404/500 from an int-keyed `WHERE id='options'` cast. users has **no `GET /:id`** route at all, so ordering is moot there (still placed before the param-bearing `PUT /:id` etc., harmless).
  - (d) **USABLE-row exposure matches existing semantics ‚Äî no over/under-exposure.** Every options SELECT filters `WHERE is_active AND effective_from <= now()` ‚Äî byte-identical to the list's `?active=true` predicate (clients repo:27-29 `is_active=$n AND effective_from<=now()`). No `effective_to`/expiry column exists in the model, so "active AND in effect (ADR-0017)" is fully captured. Tests confirm inactive + future-dated rows are excluded (all four). Trimmed projection (no version/audit/created_by) ‚Äî strictly LESS data than the list. No `SELECT *`, no `console.*`, no secrets in diff (scanned).
  - (e) **PII/DPDP ‚Äî `users/options` exposes `{id,username,name,role}` of USABLE users to any `USER_VIEW` holder.** Per `project_rbac_hierarchy_model`, USER_VIEW is admin-tier (SUPER_ADMIN/MANAGER class; FIELD_AGENT/BACKEND_USER/TEAM_LEAD do NOT hold it ‚Äî BE 403 test proves it). This is the same audience and a SUBSET of the columns already returned by `GET /users` list (which adds email/reports_to). No new sensitive field (no email/phone/password); **ACCEPTABLE ‚Äî no broadened exposure vs the existing list.** NOTE for the record: this is internal-staff directory data behind an admin perm, not customer/applicant PII.
  - **B-22 RESOLVED (the standing SHOULD-FIX, both ledgers):** all 7 FE feeders that used `?active=true&limit=200` + `.then(r=>r.items)` (CpvPage clients/products/units, RateManagementPage clients/products/units, CaseCreatePage clients/products, UsersPage manager picker) now call the unpaginated `/options` feeds ‚Äî the silent-truncation latent bug is removed at the source. Security-neutral (same perm, same/fewer columns, same USABLE set).
- **2026-06-06 ¬∑ Slice ‚Äî Server-side column-filter contract (`platform/pagination.ts` `FilterField`/`PageSpec.filterMap`/`AppliedFilter`/`resolveFilters`; clients+products service/repo)** ‚Äî **VERDICT: PASS.**
  - (a) **`${f.column}` interpolation ‚Äî INJECTION-SAFE by construction (the critical question).** Traced end-to-end: `resolveFilters` (pagination.ts:43-61) iterates `Object.entries(spec.filterMap)` ‚Äî `field` and `def` come ONLY from the service's hardcoded `CLIENT_PAGE_SPEC.filterMap`/`PRODUCT_PAGE_SPEC.filterMap` (service.ts:17-20 both: `{code:{column:'code'},name:{column:'name'}}`), NEVER the request. The only request contribution is `query['f_'+field]` ‚Üí `raw` ‚Üí trimmed `value`. The emitted `AppliedFilter.column` is a verbatim copy of `def.column` (a server literal); `AppliedFilter.value` carries the user string. Repo loop (clients repository.ts:40-43, products 38-43) interpolates ONLY `f.column` + the fixed `ILIKE`/`=` token into SQL, and `params.push`es `f.value` (or `%v%`) bound as `$N`. **No request-controlled string ever reaches the SQL string** ‚Äî request fields that aren't a filterMap KEY are dropped (the loop only ever sees server keys), and the value is always parameterized. Same trust model as the established `sortMap` control.
  - (b) **Whitelist + drop semantics proven by tests.** platform: `f_dropTable:"x'; DROP TABLE clients --"` ‚Üí `[]` (unknown field, pagination.test.ts:96), missing `f_` prefix ‚Üí `[]`, blank-trimmed ‚Üí `[]`; enum out-of-set (`f_status:'maybe'`) ‚Üí dropped (test:90). clients api: `?f_secret=x&f_is_active=true%3BDROP` ‚Üí 200, totalCount unaffected (clients.api.test.ts:315-319) ‚Äî both unwhitelisted, both dropped, no SQL effect. Injecting a malicious VALUE into a whitelisted text field (`f_code`) is harmless: it's bound as `$N` (identical mechanism to the existing parameterized `search` ILIKE). enum kind eq-only against `def.values`; anything else rejected before SQL.
  - (c) **RBAC unchanged.** No routes/controller auth touched (diff name-only: only pagination.ts + clients/products service+repo+tests). GET `/` still `authorize(MASTERDATA_VIEW)`. Default-deny intact.
  - (d) **No new PII / no `filters`-echo leak.** `filters` echo (service.ts clients:48 / products:54) reflects only server-PARSED, whitelisted, trimmed `f.value`s (`filters['f_'+f.field]=f.value`) ‚Äî never raw query keys; an unwhitelisted `f_secret` is never echoed (it produced no AppliedFilter). No new column in SELECT. No secrets/`console.*`/`SELECT *` in diff.
  - SHOULD-FIX (none blocking): text filters allow `%`/`_` ILIKE metacharacters in the value (un-escaped, same as the pre-existing `search`) ‚Äî a wildcard-injection at worst returns extra/fewer matching rows on a tiny reference table, NOT a security issue (no SQL injection; value is bound). Consistent with the existing search behavior.
  - OPEN (carried): standing rule reaffirmed ‚Äî any new list's `filterMap[field].column` (like `sortMap`) MUST be a real server-defined column literal, NEVER derived from request input; `filters` echo stays parsed-values-only. When this contract rolls to user-scoped tables (cases/locations), re-verify column filters apply to BOTH the items AND count query (they do here ‚Äî see DB ledger) so totalCount can't leak out-of-scope row existence.

- **2026-06-06 ¬∑ B-4 Excel-style header multi-select (¬ß7) ‚Äî `pagination.ts` `filterClauses` + multi-value enum filters** ‚Äî **VERDICT: PASS.**
  - **Injection trace re-confirmed, incl. the new `= ANY($n)` path:** `f.column` originates ONLY from each service's hardcoded `filterMap[field].column` (string literals: `code`/`name`/`category`/`kind`/`is_active`). No request string reaches SQL TEXT. The new `kind` enum is gated to the `KINDS` literal tuple (`packages/sdk/src/verificationUnit.ts:8` = `['FIELD_VISIT','KYC_DOCUMENT','DESK_DOCUMENT']`); `resolveFilters` (`pagination.ts:60-73`) splits comma input, keeps ONLY `def.values`-allowed values, de-dupes, and produces op `in`(>1)/`eq`(1) ‚Äî any out-of-set token (e.g. `HACKER`, `x'; DROP TABLE‚Ä¶`) is silently dropped before a filter exists.
  - **`filterClauses` (`pagination.ts:85-100`)** interpolates ONLY `f.column` + a FIXED operator string; every value is BOUND: `in`‚Üí`${col} = ANY($n)` binds the JS array as one param (node-postgres sends a typed array, never string-interpolated ‚Üí no IN-list injection), `ilike`‚Üíbinds `%v%`, `eq`‚Üíbinds the scalar. Confirmed `= ANY($n)` is the safe parameterized form, NOT a built `IN (...)` string.
  - Tests prove it: unit `filterClauses` asserts `['code ILIKE $2','is_active = $3','kind = ANY($4)']` w/ params `['%hd%','true',['A','B']]`; `resolveFilters` enum-multi + injection-drop (`f_dropTable`, missing `f_` prefix, blank) all ‚Üí `[]`; VU api `f_kind=FIELD_VISIT,HACKER`‚Üíonly FIELD_VISIT. 16/16 pagination unit tests GREEN (re-ran locally, coverage gate disabled for single-file run).
  - Sort-injection control (`sortMap` whitelist) UNCHANGED. RBAC unchanged (lists keep `masterdata.view`). No secrets. **DON'T-REGRESS:** when this contract reaches scoped tables (cases/locations), the row-scope WHERE must be applied to BOTH count+items (shared-`where` makes this automatic ‚Äî preserve) so filtered totalCount can't leak out-of-scope existence (carried OPEN).

- **2026-06-06 ¬∑ Slice ‚Äî Column-filter rollout to the 5 remaining lists (users ¬∑ report-templates ¬∑ locations ¬∑ rates ¬∑ cases)** ‚Äî **VERDICT: PASS.**
  - (a) **`${f.column}` interpolation ‚Äî INJECTION-SAFE by construction (the critical question), re-traced for all 5.** Every `filterMap[field].column` is a HARDCODED string literal in the service's PageSpec ‚Äî including the join-aliased ones: `u.role`/`u.username`/`u.name` (users service.ts:32-35), `pa.name`/`cs.case_number`/`cs.status` (cases :33-37), `vu.kind`/`vu.name`/`l.pincode`/`l.area`/`r.rate_type` (rates :33-38), `code`/`name`/`template_type` (templates :26-29), `pincode`/`area`/`city`/`state` (locations :21-25). `resolveFilters` (pagination.ts:55-77, UNCHANGED in this diff) iterates `Object.entries(spec.filterMap)` so only server KEYS are ever consulted; the request contributes ONLY `query['f_'+field]` ‚Üí trimmed value. `filterClauses` (pagination.ts:85-96) interpolates ONLY `f.column` (the server literal) + a fixed operator, and ALWAYS binds the value (`= ANY($n)` typed-array for enum-multi, `ILIKE $n` `%v%` for text, `= $n` for enum-single). No request string reaches SQL TEXT in any of the 5 modules. Same trust model as the established `sortMap` control.
  - (b) **Enum values validated ‚àà enum before SQL.** `f_role`‚ààUSER_ROLES, `f_status`‚ààCASE_STATUSES, `f_templateType`‚ààREPORT_TEMPLATE_TYPES, `f_kind`‚ààKINDS ‚Äî `resolveFilters` drops any out-of-set token (e.g. `f_role=HACKER` or `f_status=x';DROP`) before an AppliedFilter exists, so a bogus enum just yields 0 matches, never SQL. Tests prove the live paths: users `f_role=MANAGER,TEAM_LEADER` multi-IN (users.api.test.ts:169), cases `f_status=NEW/CANCELLED` count-safety (cases:140-141), rates `f_kind` on the joined `vu.kind` count+items (rates:106-117), locations `f_state`/`f_city` AND-combine (locations:134-149), templates `f_templateType=KYC_DOCUMENT` (templates:229-235).
  - (c) **No `filters`-echo leak.** Each service echoes `filters['f_'+f.field] = f.values.join(',')` (cases:96, locations:56, rates:84, templates:64, users:72) ‚Äî reflects only the server-PARSED, whitelisted, validated values (the AppliedFilter that survived `resolveFilters`), NEVER a raw query key. An unwhitelisted `f_secret` produces no AppliedFilter so is never echoed. Consistent with the parsed-values-only rule.
  - (d) **RBAC unchanged.** No routes/controller auth files in this diff (services + repos + tests + FE pages only). GET lists keep their existing perms (`USER_VIEW`/`MASTERDATA_VIEW`/`CASE_VIEW`). Default-deny intact; no write path touched.
  - (e) **No new PII / no new column.** SELECT column lists unchanged; the new filters only add WHERE predicates. cases row-scope gap is pre-existing (DB ledger) and column filters only NARROW the returned set, never widen it.
  - **OPEN (carried, reaffirmed):** any future list's `filterMap[field].column` MUST stay a real server-defined literal (never request-derived); `filters` echo stays parsed-values-only; when row-scope lands on cases, apply it to BOTH count+items.

- **2026-06-06 ¬∑ CPV effective-from reschedule edit (`PUT /client-products/:id` + `PUT /cpv-units/:id`)** ‚Äî **VERDICT: PASS.**
  - (a) **RBAC ‚Äî same gate as the create/toggle writes (SUPER_ADMIN-only).** Both new routes mount `authorize(PERMISSIONS.MASTERDATA_MANAGE)` (routes.ts:13 cp, :20 cpv) ‚Äî byte-identical to `POST /` and `/:id/activate`/`/:id/deactivate` on the same routers. No perm weakened, default-deny intact; per `project_rbac_hierarchy_model` MASTERDATA_MANAGE is admin-tier.
  - (b) **Injection ‚Äî all values bound, nothing interpolated.** repository.ts cp:107-110 / cpv:201-204: `UPDATE ‚Ä¶ SET effective_from=$2, version=version+1, updated_at=now() WHERE id=$1 AND version=$3` ‚Äî `effectiveFrom`‚Üí`$2`, `expectedVersion`‚Üí`$3`, `id`‚Üí`$1`. `id` is `parseId` (controller.ts:7-11) `Number.isInteger(id) && id>0` else 400 BAD_REQUEST, so no string reaches the int `WHERE id` cast. No dynamic SQL, no `${}` of request data.
  - (c) **Immutable-key invariant PRESERVED ‚Äî the critical check.** The `SET` clause touches ONLY `effective_from`, `version`, `updated_at`. NO key column is settable: client_products `client_id`/`product_id` and CPV `client_product_id`/`verification_unit_id` never appear in any SET. The zod schemas (`UpdateClientProductSchema`/`UpdateCpvUnitSchema` = `{ effectiveFrom: isoDate }`, cpv.ts:71-72) accept ONLY `effectiveFrom`; `version` is read via the separate OCC envelope (`requireVersion`) and is only ever `version+1` server-side, never written from input. A client cannot rekey the link/unit. Verified.
  - (d) **VERSION_REQUIRED enforced.** service.ts cp:29-33 / cpv:47-51 calls `requireVersion(input)` (platform/occ.ts:11-15 ‚Üí 400 VERSION_REQUIRED) independent of the field-schema `.parse` (400 VALIDATION) ‚Äî distinct error codes preserved. Live-verified: PUT no-version‚Üí400 VERSION_REQUIRED.
  - (e) **No new PII / no secrets / no new column.** SELECT projection unchanged (`CP_COLS`/`CPV_COLS`, repository.ts:18-19 ‚Äî no key/sensitive column added); these are admin master-data link rows, not customer PII. No `console.*`/secrets in diff (scanned). 404 CLIENT_PRODUCT_NOT_FOUND/CPV_UNIT_NOT_FOUND on miss (IDOR-safe; live-verified cpv-units/999999‚Üí404).
  - OPEN (carried, unchanged): standing sortMap/filterMap literal-only + parsed-filters-echo rules unaffected (no list code touched).

- **2026-06-06 ¬∑ ADR-0020 correctable identity keys (clients + products `code`) ‚Äî VERDICT: PASS.**
  - (a) ‚úÖ **Lock cannot be bypassed ‚Äî dependents check runs BEFORE any mutation.** service.ts clients:73-76 / products:79-82: `codeChanged = validated.code !== undefined && validated.code !== existing.code` then `if (codeChanged && await repo.hasDependents(id)) throw AppError.conflict('CODE_LOCKED')` ‚Äî the 409 is thrown in the service, BEFORE `repo.updateRow` is ever called, so no SQL UPDATE of `code` executes for an in-use row. `hasDependents` is a read-only `SELECT EXISTS(...)` (repository.ts clients:104-110 / products:104-110), no side effects. Order verified: gate ‚Üí throw, or gate ‚Üí pass ‚Üí update.
  - (b) ‚úÖ **`code` is bound, not interpolated.** UPDATE `SET code = COALESCE($2, code)` with `code ?? null` passed as `$2` (repository.ts clients:124-131 / products); name `$3`, effectiveFrom `$4`, userId `$5`, version `$6`, id `$1`. No `${}` of request data in the SQL. The error message `code already exists: ${code}` is a server-side string in the AppError body, not SQL. `id` reaches `WHERE id=$1` via the same `parseId` integer guard as the other write routes (unchanged).
  - (c) ‚úÖ **UPDATE touches only code/name/effective_from/version/updated_by/updated_at.** SET clause = `code, name, effective_from, version=version+1, updated_by, updated_at=now()`. No other column settable; `code` is the ONLY newly-writable column and it is gated. version is server-side `+1`, never from input.
  - (d) ‚úÖ **RBAC unchanged.** PUT `/:id` still `authorize(PERMISSIONS.MASTERDATA_MANAGE)` (clients routes.ts:16; products mirror). No perm weakened; admin-tier gate per `project_rbac_hierarchy_model`. No new route added.
  - (e) ‚úÖ **COALESCE($2,code) is wipe-safe.** When code unchanged the service passes `undefined` ‚Üí repo `code ?? null` ‚Üí `$2 = NULL` ‚Üí `COALESCE(NULL, code)` keeps the stored value. A NULL `code` can never be written (column is NOT NULL anyway, and COALESCE prevents it). Confirmed no accidental wipe; the FE always sends `code` now but an in-use unchanged code computes `codeChanged=false` ‚Üí `undefined` ‚Üí preserved.
  - DISPOSITION: APPROVED. The `CODE_LOCKED` (409, IDOR-safe ‚Äî only reachable post-auth on an existing row, 404 on miss via service findById) honours ADR-0020 exactly.

- **2026-06-06 ¬∑ ADR-0020 rollout to report_templates ¬∑ locations ¬∑ users (`code`/`pincode`/`username` correctable) ‚Äî VERDICT: PASS.**
  - (a) ‚úÖ **Keys are BOUND, never interpolated.** All 3 UPDATEs set the key via `COALESCE($N, key)` with the value `params.push`ed (`input.{pincode|code|username} ?? null`) ‚Äî bound parameters, no `${}` of request data anywhere in the SQL. The only interpolation is the static `${COLS}` projection literal. No injection surface on the rekey path. `id` reaches `WHERE id=$1` via the existing `parseId` int-guard (locations/templates) or the uuid id (users) ‚Äî unchanged.
  - (b) ‚úÖ **locations PINCODE_LOCKED thrown PRE-mutation.** service.ts:71-72: `pincodeChanged = validated.pincode !== undefined && validated.pincode !== existing.pincode`; `if (pincodeChanged && await repo.hasDependents(id)) throw AppError.conflict('PINCODE_LOCKED', ‚Ä¶)` ‚Äî the 409 fires in the service BEFORE `repo.update` runs, so no SQL UPDATE of `pincode` executes for an in-use row. `hasDependents` is a read-only `SELECT EXISTS` (no side effects). Order verified. API test exercises full path: correct-while-unreferenced (200) ‚Üí reference via rate ‚Üí blocked (409 PINCODE_LOCKED).   - (c) ‚úÖ **users uniqueness enforced on rename.** A username rename can collide on the `username` unique index ‚Üí caught by the existing `mapWriteError` ‚Üí 409 USER_EXISTS (test: rename to a taken username ‚Üí 409). No dependents gate is the CORRECT posture ‚Äî `username` carries no FK (all user refs are by uuid `id`: cases.assigned_to, sessions.user_id, reports_to ‚Äî all REFERENCES users(id)), so a rename cannot orphan any row; nothing to lock. A rename is still gated by USER_MANAGE on PUT `/:id`.
  - (d) ‚úÖ **report_templates ‚Äî lock never fires (0 referrers), still injection/authz-safe.** `hasDependents`‚Üí`false` ‚áí `CODE_LOCKED` is unreachable today; a code correction always proceeds and a collision maps to 409 REPORT_TEMPLATE_EXISTS via the NEW try/catch (`pgCode===23505`). PUT `/:id` keeps `authorize(MASTERDATA_MANAGE)` (locations, report-templates) and `authorize(USER_MANAGE)` (users) ‚Äî both admin-tier per project_rbac_hierarchy_model. Default-deny intact, no perm weakened, no new route. No new PII/sensitive column added (SELECT `${COLS}` projection unchanged in all 3); `username` is internal-staff login data behind USER_MANAGE, not customer PII. No `console.*`/secrets/`SELECT *` in the diff (scanned).
  - SHOULD-FIX (non-blocking, cosmetic): 4 stale doc-comments now contradict shipped behavior ‚Äî `reportTemplates/service.ts:42` & `sdk/reportTemplates.ts:47` ("`code` is immutable"), `locations/service.ts:34` ("pincode is the immutable key"), `users/service.ts:43` ("`username` is immutable (identity)"). Misleading but no security/behavior impact (same stale-header class flagged on the clients/products ADR-0020 entry).
  - OPEN (carried): standing sortMap/filterMap literal-only + parsed-filters-echo rules unaffected (no list code touched). SEC-RATCHET: when reporting tables FK `report_templates`, replace the `false` `hasDependents` stub with the real probe so an in-use template code locks (that lock is the integrity control there).

- **2026-06-06 ¬∑ ADR-0020 final entity: verification_units `code` correctable (the $23 trailing-param one) ‚Äî VERDICT: PASS.**
  - (a) ‚úÖ **Lock cannot be bypassed ‚Äî dependents check runs BEFORE any mutation.** service.ts:103-105: `codeChanged = patch['code']!==undefined && patch['code']!==existing.code` then `if (codeChanged && await repo.hasDependents(id)) throw AppError.conflict('CODE_LOCKED', ‚Ä¶)` ‚Äî the 409 fires in the service BEFORE `repo.update` is ever called, so no SQL UPDATE of `code` executes for an in-use row. `hasDependents` is a read-only `SELECT EXISTS(...)` (repository.ts:150-156), no side effects. No `${}` of request data in the SQL ‚Äî the only interpolation is the static `${SELECT_COLS}` projection literal. The unique-violation error body `code already exists: ${input.code}` is a server-side AppError string, not SQL. `id` reaches `WHERE id=$1` via the existing `parseId` int-guard (unchanged). No injection surface on the rekey path.

The SDK `UpdateVerificationUnitSchema` drops `.omit({code})` ‚Üí `code` is an optional UPPER_SNAKE-validated field (baseShape + .partial()); no other field opened up.
  - (d) ‚úÖ **RBAC unchanged ‚Äî no route/controller in the diff.** `git diff --name-only` = service/repo/test + sdk + dialog only; NO routes/controller file. FE dialog adds a user-facing CODE_LOCKED message (server literal echoed via ApiError.code branch) ‚Äî no data leak. UNIT_CODE_EXISTS on a rename collision (unique index) ‚Äî bound `code`, server-side message.

- **2026-06-07 ¬∑ B-13 DataGrid Export (synchronous CSV/XLSX; `current`+`all`; clients+products) ‚Äî VERDICT: PASS (overall).**
  - (1) ‚úÖ **SQL injection ‚Äî SAFE; export REUSES the list's whitelisted path verbatim, zero new SQL surface.** `clientService.exportData`/`productService.exportData` (clients service.ts:60-75, products :61-76) call the IDENTICAL `resolvePage(rawQuery,SPEC)` + `resolveFilters(rawQuery,SPEC)` as `list`, then call the SAME `repo.list(...)`. No new query is written. `sortColumn`=`SPEC.sortMap[sortBy]` (server literal, default-fallback on unknown), `columnFilters` come from `resolveFilters` (only filterMap KEYS consulted; `f.column` = `def.column` server literal; values bound via `filterClauses` `= ANY($n)`/`ILIKE $n`/`= $n` ‚Äî pagination.ts:85-99). The request strings unique to export ‚Äî `format`/`mode`/`cols` ‚Äî NEVER reach SQL: `resolveExport` (export/index.ts:23-35) whitelists `format`‚àà`['xlsx','csv']` (else 400 BAD_EXPORT_FORMAT) and `mode`‚àà`['current','all']` (else 400 BAD_EXPORT_MODE); `cols` is split to a string[] and used ONLY by `selectColumns` (format.ts:20-26) to pick from the server's hardcoded `ExportColumn[]` manifest by `id` (unknown ids dropped, empty‚Üífull manifest) ‚Äî it never touches SQL or the projection (SELECT_COLS is a fixed literal). Same trust model as the established sortMap/filterMap control.
  - (2) ‚úÖ **CSV formula injection (CWE-1236) ‚Äî CORRECT.** `escapeCsvCell` (format.ts:40-45): leading `=`/`+`/`-`/`@`/`\t`/`\r` ‚Üí prefix `'` (`/^[=+\-@\t\r]/`), THEN RFC4180 wrap if `/[",\n\r]/` present, doubling embedded `"`. Order is right (neutralize-then-quote). Header CRLF row endings (`\r\n`, format.ts:51) per RFC4180. Headers ARE also escaped (format.ts:48) ‚Äî defensive even though they're server literals. Every cell is `String(v)` first (Date‚ÜíISO), so numeric/bool/Date can't bypass the string regex. NOTE (non-blocking): a leading `\n`-only cell is RFC-quoted but not formula-prefixed ‚Äî harmless (newline isn't a formula trigger char); and a `\t`/`\r` lead is prefixed (formula-safe) and `\r` additionally triggers quoting. Coverage of the documented attack set (`= + - @ \t \r`) is complete. **XLSX path:** exceljs `addRow` writes cell VALUES as data (not parsed formulas) ‚Äî `cell()` returns the same neutralized-source string but via exceljs's typed cell write; sheet name sanitized (`[\\/?*[\]:]`‚Üíspace, ‚â§31). Acceptable: exceljs does not auto-evaluate a leading `=` in a string cell as a formula on write.
  - (3) ‚úÖ **RBAC ‚Äî default-deny, NEW `data.export` perm, gated; scope identical to the list.** Routes mount `authorize(PERMISSIONS.DATA_EXPORT)` on `GET /export` (clients routes.ts:14, products :14), placed BEFORE `/:id` so it's never captured as `id='export'`. `DATA_EXPORT='data.export'` (permissions.ts:36) granted to SA(auto via Object.values)/MANAGER/TEAM_LEADER/BACKEND_USER, EXCLUDED from FIELD_AGENT/KYC_VERIFIER (permissions.ts:41-65) ‚Äî both hold only `case.view`, so they get 403 on export (default-deny, no fallthrough). **No IDOR / no broadened exposure:** export re-runs the SAME unscoped `repo.list` the user can already GET via `MASTERDATA_VIEW`; clients/products are admin master-data (no per-owner/territory row), so the export set ‚äÜ the list set the caller can already see. SELECT_COLS unchanged; the export manifest (masterDataExport.ts:18-27) exposes only code/name/effectiveFrom/created/updated/status ‚Äî a SUBSET of the list projection (omits version/created_by/updated_by). No new column, no PII added.
  - (4) ‚úÖ **DoS ‚Äî `all` path capped.** `exportData` with `mode==='all'` calls `repo.list` with `limit: exportThreshold()` (=`EXPORT_JOB_THRESHOLD`, config default 10000 ‚Äî config/index.ts:19), so AT MOST ~10k rows are ever materialized into memory, THEN `assertExportable(totalCount)` (export/index.ts:47-56) throws **413 EXPORT_TOO_LARGE** when `totalCount >= threshold`. Both guards combine: the LIMIT clamps the fetch, the count gates the response. `current` mode keeps the normal page LIMIT (‚â§500, clamped by resolvePage). No unbounded query, no full-table stream. (Minor: at exactly threshold-1 rows a ~10k-row CSV/XLSX builds synchronously in-process ‚Äî within spec's synchronous ceiling; background-job offload is the deferred report-worker path.)
  - (5) ‚úÖ **Content-Disposition header injection ‚Äî SAFE.** `filename` = `${filenameBase}-${stamp()}.${format}` (export/index.ts:79) where `filenameBase` is a HARDCODED controller literal (`'clients'`/`'products'`, controller.ts:49), `stamp()` is `YYYYMMDD` digits only (index.ts:58), and `format` is the whitelisted enum. NO request string reaches the filename ‚Üí no CR/LF/`"` injection into the response header. (Even the FE-supplied `cols` never flows here.)
  - (6) ‚ÑπÔ∏è **exceljs supply-chain ‚Äî note, not a blocker.** `toXlsx` lazy-imports `exceljs` (format.ts:61) only when an XLSX export runs. exceljs is a large transitive-dep surface; it parses no untrusted INPUT here (write-only, in-process buffer) so the attack surface is minimal. WATCH: keep it patched (it has had ReDoS/zip CVEs historically on the READ path, unused here); pin + audit in CI. No secrets, no `console.*`, no `SELECT *` in the diff (scanned).
  - DISPOSITION: **PASS.** No BLOCK, no FLAG. Export adds zero new SQL/auth surface ‚Äî it is the list query behind a new default-deny `data.export` gate, with correct CWE-1236 escaping, a 10k DoS cap (LIMIT + 413), and an injection-proof filename. OPEN (carried): when this export contract reaches row-scoped tables (cases), the row-scope WHERE must apply to the export query too (it will automatically, since export reuses `repo.list`) AND `assertExportable` must count the SCOPED total ‚Äî else a 413 could leak out-of-scope row existence (same class as the cases-list totalCount note). Standing sortMap/filterMap literal-only rule reaffirmed.

- **2026-06-09 ¬∑ Export `mode:'selected'` ‚Äî caller-supplied `ids` row-slice (clients + products) ‚Äî VERDICT: PASS.**
  - (1) ‚úÖ **SQL injection ‚Äî SAFE; `ids` is BOUND as a typed array, never interpolated.** Repo appends `params.push(o.ids); where.push(\`id = ANY($${params.length})\`)` (clients repository.ts:43-46, products :43-46) ‚Äî the int[] is bound as a single `$N` param (node-postgres sends a typed array, NOT a built `IN (‚Ä¶)` string ‚Üí no IN-list injection), exactly the established safe form from the ¬ß7 enum-multi `= ANY($n)` control. The only thing interpolated is `$${params.length}` (a digit) + the literal `id = ANY()`. **Non-numeric / `'1) OR 1=1--'` ids CANNOT reach SQL:** the service maps `ex.ids.map(Number).filter((n)=>Number.isInteger(n))` (clients service.ts:68-69, products :67-68) BEFORE binding ‚Äî `Number('1) OR 1=1--')` ‚Üí `NaN` ‚Üí `Number.isInteger(NaN)` false ‚Üí dropped; only genuine integers survive into `o.ids`. Even if a string slipped through, it'd be a bound param value against an int column (type error ‚Üí query rejected), never SQL text. `resolveExport` (export/index.ts:36-37) only `split(',').filter(Boolean)`s the raw `ids` string ‚Äî it does no SQL and hands raw strings to the module, which does the int-coercion. Confirmed end-to-end: no path interpolates any request-derived string into the query.
  - (2) ‚úÖ **Empty/invalid-ids guard ‚Äî the data-exposure check ‚Äî CORRECT, fails CLOSED.** `if (ex.mode==='selected' && (!selectedIds || selectedIds.length===0)) return { rows: [], columns: ‚Ä¶ }` (clients service.ts:70-71, products :69-70) runs BEFORE `repo.list` ‚Äî so `mode=selected` with NO valid ids returns ZERO rows, never the whole table. The guard is positioned correctly (early-return ahead of the query). Critically, the `repo.list` `ids` predicate is itself guarded `if (o.ids && o.ids.length)` (repo:43) so an empty array would not emit `id = ANY('{}')` anyway ‚Äî but the service early-return is the real protection (an empty `ANY('{}')` matches nothing too, defense-in-depth). API test proves it: `mode=selected` with no `ids` ‚Üí 200 + header-only (1 line, zero data rows) "never falls through to all" (clients.api.test.ts). The `mode=all` fallthrough is impossible: `limit = ex.mode==='current' ? r.limit : exportThreshold()` only branches current-vs-other, and the selected early-return fires first.
  - (3) ‚úÖ **IDOR / scope-leak ‚Äî PATTERN is scope-safe; `ids` is ANDed ON TOP of the (future) scope WHERE.** The `id = ANY($n)` clause is pushed into the SAME `where[]` joined by ` AND ` (repo:47) as the active/search/columnFilter predicates ‚Äî it INTERSECTS, never replaces or widens. A caller passing arbitrary out-of-scope ids gets only rows that ALSO satisfy every other WHERE term; when row-scope lands on cases the scope predicate sits in the same `AND` chain, so out-of-scope ids simply don't match (return fewer rows, never more). Clients/products have no row-scope today (admin master-data, `MASTERDATA_VIEW`), so the selected set ‚äÜ the list set the caller can already GET ‚Äî no new exposure. **No existence-leak:** `selected` has NO `assertExportable` call (only `all` does ‚Äî service.ts:82/:81), so it never emits a 413 and cannot leak out-of-scope-id existence via a count-gated error; an out-of-scope/nonexistent id just silently yields one fewer row in a 200. CONFIRMED correct that `selected` skips `assertExportable` ‚Äî the ids set is inherently bounded by what the user ticked, not by table size.
  - (4) ‚úÖ **Authz unchanged ‚Äî `selected` does NOT bypass `data.export`.** No routes/controller file in the diff (services + repos + platform/export + sdk + FE/e2e only). `GET /export` still mounts `authorize(PERMISSIONS.DATA_EXPORT)` (clients routes.ts:14, products :14) ‚Äî `mode` is parsed AFTER the middleware gate, so `selected` is reachable only by a `data.export` holder. FIELD_AGENT/KYC_VERIFIER still 403 (default-deny, unchanged from the B-13 entry). No perm weakened, no new route.
  - (5) ‚úÖ **DoS ‚Äî result is bounded by `exportThreshold()` LIMIT (clamps materialized rows to ~10k).** `limit: ex.mode==='current' ? r.limit : exportThreshold()` ‚Üí `selected` uses the 10k LIMIT cap (same as `all`), so even a huge ticked set materializes ‚â§ threshold rows. NOTE (non-blocking, same class as B-13): the `ids` ARRAY ITSELF is unbounded in the URL ‚Äî a caller could POST‚Ä¶ actually GET a multi-thousand-id `?ids=` querystring; node-postgres binds it as one array param (no per-element SQL cost) and the LIMIT still caps output rows, but a pathologically long querystring is an un-capped INPUT (URL-length limits + the int filter are the only bound). LOW severity (auth'd `data.export` actor, array is parameterized, output LIMIT-capped); WATCH if `selected` reaches large scoped tables ‚Äî consider an explicit `ids.length` cap (e.g. ‚â§ a few thousand) at `resolveExport` then. Not a blocker.
  - DISPOSITION: **PASS.** No BLOCK, no FLAG. The `ids` path is injection-safe (int-filtered + `= ANY($n)` typed-array bind, zero interpolation), fails-closed on empty/invalid (early-return ‚Üí 0 rows, never the table), scope-safe by AND-intersection (out-of-scope ids can't widen the set; no 413 existence-leak since `selected` skips `assertExportable`), and behind the unchanged `data.export` gate. SHOULD-FIX (non-blocking): bound the `ids` array length at `resolveExport` before this rolls to large/scoped tables. OPEN (carried, reaffirmed): when export reaches row-scoped tables (cases), the scope WHERE must sit in the same `AND` chain as `id = ANY` (it will, since `selected` reuses `repo.list`) so ticked-but-out-of-scope ids return nothing; standing sortMap/filterMap literal-only rule reaffirmed.

- **2026-06-09 ¬∑ Bulk (de)activate ‚Äî `POST /api/v2/{clients,products}/bulk-{activate,deactivate}` (body `{items:[{id,version}]}`, per-row OCC) ‚Äî new `platform/bulk.ts` + `packages/sdk/src/bulk.ts` + per-module service/controller/routes; FE `BulkStatusActions.tsx` + DataGrid `BulkSelection<T>.rows` (untracked) ‚Äî VERDICT: PASS.**
  - (a) ‚úÖ **Authz ‚Äî SUPER_ADMIN-only, default-deny, identical to the single activate/deactivate; NO privilege escalation via bulk.** Both bulk routes mount `authorize(PERMISSIONS.MASTERDATA_MANAGE)` (clients routes.ts:19-20, products :19-20) ‚Äî byte-identical gate to `POST /:id/activate` / `/:id/deactivate` (:21-22). `authorize` (packages/access/src/authorize.ts:14-27) is default-deny: no `req.auth` ‚Üí **401 UNAUTHENTICATED**; `!roleHas(role,perm)` ‚Üí **403 FORBIDDEN** (`roleHas` = `ROLE_PERMISSIONS[role]?.includes(perm) ?? false`, permissions.ts:67-68 ‚Äî unknown role/perm fails closed). `MASTERDATA_MANAGE` is granted ONLY to SUPER_ADMIN (via `Object.values(PERMISSIONS)`, permissions.ts:42); MANAGER/TEAM_LEADER/BACKEND_USER hold only `MASTERDATA_VIEW` (NOT manage ‚Äî :44/:52/:58), FIELD_AGENT/KYC_VERIFIER hold only `CASE_VIEW` (:63-64). So a read-only role gets 403, unauth 401. API test proves the gate: FIELD_AGENT bulk-deactivate ‚Üí 403, no-auth ‚Üí 401 (clients.api.test.ts:551-558). Bulk gives a MASTERDATA_MANAGE holder no capability they lack on the single endpoint ‚Äî same perm, same write (`repo.setActive`), just batched.
  - (b) ‚úÖ **Injection ‚Äî nothing request-derived reaches SQL unbound; malformed item ‚Üí 400, zero partial execution.** `parseBulkItems(body,'int')` (bulk.ts:36-53) validates EAGERLY before any write: `version=Number(o.version)` must be `Number.isInteger && >=0` else 400 BULK_ITEM_INVALID; for `idKind:'int'` (both modules pass `'int'`, service.ts clients:131/products:127) `id=Number(o.id)` must be `Number.isInteger && >0` else 400 ‚Äî `Number('1) OR 1=1--')`‚ÜíNaN‚Üírejected. The whole parse runs over the full `items` array and THROWS on the first bad item (not a per-row skip) ‚Üí the controller's `catch(e)‚Üínext(e)` returns 400 and `applyBulkOcc` never runs ‚Üí **no partial-but-wrong batch**. Surviving ids/versions are real integers, then bound: service `apply=(id,version)=>repo.setActive(Number(id),isActive,userId,version)` ‚Üí `UPDATE clients SET is_active=$2, version=version+1, updated_by=$3, updated_at=now() WHERE id=$1 AND version=$4` (clients repository.ts:172-176, products mirror) ‚Äî `id`‚Üí`$1`, `isActive`‚Üí`$2`, `userId`‚Üí`$3`, `expectedVersion`‚Üí`$4`, all params, zero `${}` of request data. (The uuid branch ‚Äî bulk.ts:50-51, `UUID_RE`-gated ‚Äî is unused by these two int-keyed resources but is the DON'T-REGRESS path for uuid tables.) No injection surface.
  - (c) ‚úÖ **Mass-mutation / DoS ‚Äî capped at MAX_BULK_ITEMS=500.** `parseBulkItems` (bulk.ts:38-40): empty/non-array ‚Üí 400 BULK_ITEMS_REQUIRED; `raw.length>500` ‚Üí **400 BULK_TOO_LARGE** `{max,got}`. The cap is checked on the RAW array length BEFORE the per-row map, so an oversized batch is rejected without doing any per-row work. `applyBulkOcc` (bulk.ts:60-86) is a sequential `for` loop of ‚â§500 single-row OCC UPDATEs (each its own `withTransaction`); no transaction-wide table lock, no unbounded query. 500 is reasonable for a synchronous admin master-data toggle (clients/products are tiny reference tables); the doc-comment correctly notes larger ‚áí a background job (deferred). Bounded work, no DoS.
  - (d) ‚úÖ **No silent overwrite ‚Äî OCC holds per-row under bulk.** Each `repo.setActive` is version-guarded `WHERE id=$1 AND version=$4`; 0 rows with the row present ‚Üí `AppError.stale(before)` (repository.ts:177; errors.ts:55-59 ‚Üí 409 + code `STALE_UPDATE`). `applyBulkOcc` (bulk.ts:74-79) classifies `STALE_UPDATE`‚ÜíCONFLICT and `status===404`(`AppError.notFound`‚Üíerrors.ts:35-37)‚ÜíNOT_FOUND, **per row, reported not retried, never overwritten**; ANY other error re-throws (bulk.ts:81 ‚Äî a real failure is NOT swallowed as a row status, surfaces to `next(e)`). A row bumped between selection and submit comes back CONFLICT with its version untouched. Test proves the mixed batch: OK / stale‚ÜíCONFLICT / 999999‚ÜíNOT_FOUND, `{okCount:1,conflictCount:1,notFoundCount:1}` (clients.api.test.ts:520-545). The classification codes/statuses (`STALE_UPDATE`, `HTTP_STATUS.NOT_FOUND`) match the AppError factories exactly ‚Äî verified.
  - (e) ‚úÖ **Audit trail ‚Äî bulk does NOT bypass it; every successful row appends an audit row.** `repo.setActive` calls `appendAudit({entityType,entityId:id,action:isActive?'ACTIVATE':'DEACTIVATE',actorId:userId,before,after,versionAfter})` inside the same `withTransaction` (repository.ts:178-189) ‚Äî bulk reuses this verbatim per row, so each OK row emits its own actor+action audit entry (one per mutated row, append-only). A CONFLICT/NOT_FOUND row throws before the UPDATE/append (no audit for a non-mutation ‚Äî correct). `userId` flows from `req.auth.userId` (controller `userId(req)`, controller.ts:13/92/100) ‚Üí real actor, never spoofable from the body. Confirmed.
  - (f) ‚úÖ **IDOR / scope ‚Äî no NEW exposure; clients/products are global master-data (no row-scope), same as the single endpoint.** `setActive` enforces no row-scope today and **none is needed** ‚Äî these are admin reference tables behind SUPER_ADMIN `MASTERDATA_MANAGE`; any holder may already toggle any client/product via the single route, so bulk-by-id widens nothing. ‚öÝÔ∏è **DON'T-REGRESS (the scoped-resource carry):** when this bulk pattern lands on a SCOPED resource (cases/locations/portfolio rows), the per-row write MUST enforce server-side scope so a caller cannot deactivate a row OUTSIDE their scope by passing its id ‚Äî `parseBulkItems` only validates id SHAPE, NOT ownership, and `applyBulkOcc` faithfully applies whatever `apply` does. The scope check must live INSIDE the per-row `apply`/`repo` write (a `WHERE ‚Ä¶AND <scope predicate>` that yields NOT_FOUND/FORBIDDEN for an out-of-scope id), exactly as `validateTaskRecordAccess` gates task writes ‚Äî NOT in the bulk harness. Same class as the carried cases-list row-scope OPEN.
  - SHOULD-FIX (non-blocking): `BulkRowStatus` has no per-row FORBIDDEN/scope-denied bucket ‚Äî when scope lands, an out-of-scope id should map to a distinct status (or be coerced to NOT_FOUND to avoid existence-leak), decide then. No secrets / `console.*` / `SELECT *` in the diff (scanned). The new `bulk.ts` `AppError`/`HTTP_STATUS` imports resolve to `platform/errors.ts` (status+code factories verified) and `platform/http.ts`.
  - DISPOSITION: **PASS.** No BLOCK, no FLAG. Bulk adds zero new SQL/auth surface: same SUPER_ADMIN `MASTERDATA_MANAGE` gate (403 read-only / 401 unauth), eager 400 on any malformed item (no partial exec), 500-item DoS cap, fully-parameterized reuse of the OCC-guarded `repo.setActive` (per-row CONFLICT not overwrite), and per-row audit preserved. OPEN (NEW, carried): **scoped-resource bulk DON'T-REGRESS** ‚Äî per-row write must enforce server-side scope inside `apply`/repo (id-shape validation ‚âÝ ownership); add a scope/forbidden row-status then. OPEN (carried): sortMap/filterMap literal-only + parsed-filters-echo rules unaffected (no list code touched); cases-list row-scope still deferred.

- **2026-06-10 ¬∑ C-3 Slice 2: CPV `client_products` LIST ‚Üí `Paginated` envelope w/ server-side search/sort/filter (`cpv/repository.ts` `clientProductRepository.list` + `cpv/service.ts` `CP_PAGE_SPEC` + controller passes `req.query` straight through) ‚Äî VERDICT: PASS.** Same DataGrid pattern already audited PASS on clients/products; this entry confirms CPV inherits the SoT trust boundary with NO new injection surface.
  - (a) ‚úÖ **ORDER BY ‚Äî `sortColumn` NEVER request-derived; the `sortBy=client;DROP TABLE clients` test proves the fallback.** The repo (`repository.ts` `ORDER BY ${o.sortColumn} ${o.sortOrder}, cp.id ${o.sortOrder}`) interpolates `o.sortColumn`, but that value is produced ONLY by `resolvePage` (pagination.ts:155-160): `sortBy` is kept ONLY if `Object.prototype.hasOwnProperty.call(spec.sortMap, reqSortBy)` else `spec.defaultSort`; `sortColumn = spec.sortMap[sortBy]` ‚Äî a `CP_PAGE_SPEC.sortMap` literal (`c.code`/`p.code`/`unit_count`/`cp.is_active`/`cp.effective_from`/`cp.created_at`/`cp.updated_at`, service.ts), never the raw request string. `sortOrder` is a hard `'desc'|'asc'` ternary (pagination.ts:163-164) ‚Äî no third value reaches SQL. Injected `client;DROP TABLE clients` is not a sortMap key ‚Üí falls back to `client`‚Üí`c.code`; API test asserts `inj.status===200` and `inj.body.sort.sortBy==='client'` (cpv.api.test.ts). No ORDER BY injection.
  - (b) ‚úÖ **Filter COLUMNS are filterMap literals only; filter VALUES are ALWAYS bound; global `search` bound.** `resolveFilters` (pagination.ts:58-92) iterates the SPEC's `filterMap` entries (server-defined `CP_PAGE_SPEC.filterMap` ‚Üí `c.code`/`p.code`/`cp.created_at`/`cp.effective_from`), reading request params by `f_<field>` for VALUES only ‚Äî the `column` is the trusted filterMap literal, never a request string; unknown `f_*` keys and out-of-set values are silently dropped. `filterClauses` (pagination.ts:99-122) interpolates only `f.column` (the literal) and pushes EVERY value as a bound `$N` (`ILIKE %$N%` / `= ANY($N)` / `>= $N::date` / `< ($N::date + 1)`). Global `search` (repository.ts) is `params.push(\`%${o.search}%\`)` then `c.code ILIKE $n OR ‚Ä¶` ‚Äî bound, not interpolated. `active`/`clientId` parsed to bool/int in the service before binding. Zero request data reaches SQL text.
  - (c) ‚úÖ **RBAC unchanged + no IDOR regression.** List route still `clientProductRoutes.get('/', authorize(PERMISSIONS.MASTERDATA_VIEW), cp.list)` (cpv/routes.ts:11) ‚Äî untouched by the diff (controller body changed, route line did not). MASTERDATA_VIEW is the pre-existing read gate (held by SUPER_ADMIN/MANAGER/TEAM_LEADER/BACKEND_USER; FIELD/KYC denied ‚Üí 403, unauth ‚Üí 401, default-deny). CPV is **unscoped admin master-data** (no row-scope on the single endpoint either) ‚Äî the new search/sort/filter widens no row visibility; a caller already able to list all client_products can now page/sort/filter the SAME global set. Not an IDOR (existing model, not a regression). The controller now forwards `req.query` wholesale, but every consumer (`resolvePage`/`resolveFilters`/service int/bool parse) is allow-list ‚Äî extra params are inert.
  - DISPOSITION: **PASS.** No BLOCK, no FLAG. CPV list reuses the audited SoT pagination boundary verbatim: whitelisted-only ORDER BY (fallback proven by the DROP-TABLE test), filterMap-literal columns + always-bound values, bound global search, unchanged MASTERDATA_VIEW gate, no IDOR. OPEN (carried): standing **sortMap/filterMap literal-only + values-always-bound + parsed-filters-echo** rule now exercised by a 3rd resource ‚Äî DON'T-REGRESS if a future CPV filter adds an enum (must set `values` so out-of-set is dropped) or if any sortMap value ever becomes request-derived. cases-list row-scope + scoped-bulk DON'T-REGRESS still deferred (unaffected).

- **2026-06-10 ¬∑ C-3 Slice 3: CPV `client_products` DataGrid EXPORT (`cpv/service.ts` `CP_EXPORT_COLUMNS` manifest + `clientProductService.exportData`; `cpv/controller.ts` `export`‚Üí`resolveExport`/`writeExport`; `cpv/routes.ts` `GET /export` perm `DATA_EXPORT`; SDK `clientProducts.export=reqBlob('client-products',r)`; FE `CpvPage.tsx` `exportFn`; +4 api tests) ‚Äî VERDICT: PASS (overall).** Inherits the B-13 export contract verbatim; CPV adds NO new SQL/auth surface.

- **2026-06-10 ‚Äî User-Management parity Slice 3: `users` profile fields incl. optional initial password. VERDICT: PASS ‚Äî no BLOCK/FLAG/SHOULD-FIX.** (1) ‚úÖ **Password handling correct.** Optional initial `password` validated by `StrongPasswordSchema` (‚â•8, lower+upper+digit+symbol, max 200) in zod BEFORE any storage; hashed via platform `hashPassword` (scrypt, ADR-0014 ‚Äî salted, `scrypt$N$r$p$salt$hash` format) in the SERVICE layer, never client-side, never stored plaintext. Written only to `password_hash`/`password_set_at` (set_at via the `CASE WHEN $10::text IS NOT NULL` guard so it's NULL when no password supplied). The read column set `COLS` and the `User`/`UserView` SDK interfaces contain NO password field ‚Üí credential never returned on any read/create/update/list/export. Weak-password create ‚Üí 400 (test-covered). (2) ‚úÖ **No client-controlled identity.** `employee_id` is minted server-side (`'CRM-'||lpad(nextval(...),5,'0')`) inside the INSERT ‚Äî NOT in any request schema, so a client cannot set, spoof, or collide it; UNIQUE constraint + sequence guarantee monotonic uniqueness. (3) ‚úÖ **RBAC unchanged** ‚Äî reads `USER_VIEW` (`page.users`, SUPER_ADMIN-only), writes `USER_MANAGE` (`user.manage`, SUPER_ADMIN-only) ‚Üí default-deny 403 to all other roles; export `DATA_EXPORT`. No new permission, no widened surface. (4) ‚úÖ **No injection / no error leak.** New phone/dept/desig values fully bound (`$n`); FK columns bound (`input.departmentId ?? null`); the dept/design names come from bound LEFT JOINs (no request string interpolated). FK violation 23503 ‚Üí 400 INVALID_REFERENCE (server-literal, no raw pg error). The `$10::text` cast is a type-annotation, not user input ‚Äî injection-irrelevant. (5) ‚úÖ **No IDOR / no PII exposure of note** ‚Äî `department_id`/`designation_id` are FKs to admin master-data (not per-owner rows); `phone` is the user's own staff contact, visible only to the `page.users` SUPER_ADMIN audience. Audit chain intact (CREATE/UPDATE append immutable `audit_log` via `appendAudit` inside the tx; OCC stale-vs-notfound disambiguation preserved). DISPOSITION: **PASS.** OBSERVATION (carried, FE-wide): admin routes/nav unconditionally rendered ‚Äî server-side 403 is the boundary.

- **2026-06-10 ‚Äî User-Management parity Slice 4: password & login security (strong policy, self-service change-password, admin one-time-password + unlock, 5-strike lockout; migration 0026). VERDICT: PASS (1 LOW-sev accepted-tradeoff FLAG, no BLOCK).** (1) ‚úÖ **Lockout sound.** `recordFailedLogin` is ONE atomic `UPDATE ‚Ä¶ count=count+1, locked_until=CASE WHEN count+1>=$2 THEN now()+interval ELSE locked_until` under the row lock ‚Üí no lost-update race; locks EXACTLY on the 5th failure (pre-inc 4 ‚Üí `4+1>=5`), `ELSE locked_until` so a 6th failure doesn't slide the window. **`isLocked` checked BEFORE `verifyPassword` (service.ts:57)** so a locked account is never password-probed; auto-unlock is a pure `locked_until>now()` read (no write). Success ‚Üí `resetLoginState`. (2) ‚úÖ **Strong policy on ALL three paths** ‚Äî `SetPasswordSchema`‚Üí`StrongPasswordSchema`, `ChangePasswordSchema.newPassword`‚Üí`StrongPasswordSchema`, and the minted one-time password (`generateTempPassword`: 1 char/class then Fisher‚ÄìYates shuffle w/ crypto `randomBytes` ‚Üí policy-guaranteed, no class always-front; len 14, ambiguous chars dropped; test asserts all 4 classes). (3) ‚úÖ **change-password** proves current (`verifyPassword`) ‚Üí strong new ‚Üí `revokeAllForUser` (re-auth forced everywhere); 401 on wrong-current/no-auth, 400 on weak-new. (4) ‚úÖ **Secrets** ‚Äî passwords hashed (scrypt, ADR-0014) WRITE-only; never logged (no `console.*`), never returned except the one-time plaintext returned ONCE by design. (5) ‚úÖ **RBAC** ‚Äî generate-temp/unlock `USER_MANAGE` (admin-tier); change-password authenticated-any-user via `requireUserId` (401 when no `req.auth`); IDOR-safe (`parseId` UUID-validates ‚Üí 400 on miss; unlock/temp scoped to the path id, actor recorded as `updated_by`). **FLAG (LOW, ACCEPTED):** locked known-user ‚Üí 423 vs unknown ‚Üí 401 = a username-enumeration oracle (5 attempts to confirm existence). Inherent to a user-facing lockout (the 423 tells a legit user WHY) + v1/industry parity; generic-401/silent-lockout or IP-throttle is a product trade-off, not a defect. Lockout is per-account only ‚Äî pair with edge/WAF IP rate-limiting at GA (username-spray still possible). DISPOSITION: **PASS.**

- **2026-06-10 ‚Äî User-Management parity Slice 5: MFA / TOTP (RFC 6238 over node:crypto, AES-256-GCM secret-at-rest, one-time recovery codes; migration 0027). VERDICT: PASS (1 LOW-sev hardening FLAG + 1 dead-code SHOULD-FIX, no BLOCK).** (1) ‚úÖ **TOTP crypto sound** ‚Äî HOTP dynamic truncation correct (offset `hmac[19]&0xf`, `&0x7f` top byte, `bin%10**6` padded), true 8-byte BE counter, RFC 4648 base32 (`'foobar'‚Üí'MZXW6YTBOI'` pinned), ¬±1 step window, `timingSafeEqual` with the mandatory equal-length guard, non-6-digit rejected pre-compare. 160-bit `randomBytes` secret. No new dep (node:crypto only). (2) ‚úÖ **Secret-at-rest** ‚Äî AES-256-GCM, fresh 12-byte random IV/encrypt, auth tag enforced (tamper‚Üíthrow), key=`scrypt(MFA_ENC_KEY,salt,32)`; decrypted secret NEVER returned after enrol-start (only the base32 for setup) and never logged (grep clean). Dev-default key marked dev-only in-schema like JWT_SECRET ‚Üí **prod MUST override (deploy-gate carry).** (3) ‚úÖ **Recovery codes** ‚Äî 10 codes stored ONLY as scrypt hashes, returned plaintext ONCE, single-use (unused-scan + `verifyPassword` constant-time match + burn via parallel bool array), normalised identically on mint+verify. (4) ‚úÖ **Login challenge ordering-safe** ‚Äî MFA verified strictly AFTER `verifyPassword` (no MFA probe without the password); `mfaEnrolled` requires `enrolled_at NOT NULL` so a PENDING enrolment can't lock a user out; 401 MFA_REQUIRED (same status as bad password). (5) ‚úÖ **RBAC/IDOR** ‚Äî enroll/status/disable take the subject from `req.auth.userId` (never a param) ‚Üí self-only; admin-disable `USER_MANAGE`+`:userId` (intended cross-user admin authority; `deleteMfa` is idempotent DELETE-by-PK ‚Üí bad id = harmless no-op, no leak); `mfa_required` settable only via `UpdateUserSchema` (USER_MANAGE). FK `ON DELETE CASCADE` reaps secrets with the user. **FLAG (LOW, hardening):** an invalid `mfaCode` on login does NOT trip the lockout counter (only a wrong password does) ‚Üí an attacker holding the password could brute-force TOTP unthrottled (practically ~3e-6/guess; normally an edge/IP-rate-limit concern) ‚Äî add a per-account MFA-attempt throttle at GA; pairs with the Slice-4 no-IP-rate-limit carry. **SHOULD-FIX (dead code):** `jwt.ts` `sign/verifyMfaToken` (challenge-token model) are imported by NOTHING and reference a non-existent `/auth/mfa/verify` route ‚Äî remove (the shipped design uses same-request `mfaCode`). DISPOSITION: **PASS** (commit after the dead helper is dropped). NOTE: live DB-bound flow tests + triple-write not runnable in this sandbox (no PG) ‚Üí deferred to implementer.

- **2026-06-15 ¬∑ B-7.1 jobs spine (ADR-0030) ‚Äî `platform/jobs/{repository,index}.ts` + `modules/jobs/{service,controller,routes}.ts` + migration `0050_jobs.sql`. VERDICT: PASS ‚Äî no BLOCK, no FLAG.** Identity-scoped read API (own-user, like /notifications); jobs are CREATED by producers via `platform/jobs enqueue`, never by these routes.
  - (1) ‚úÖ **IDOR / cross-user read ‚Äî NONE; every read filters `WHERE created_by = actor`, non-owner ‚Üí 404.** Both read paths bind the actor: `getOwned(id,userId)` = `SELECT ‚Ä¶ FROM jobs WHERE id=$1 AND created_by=$2` (repository.ts:67-73) ‚Üí `rows[0] ?? null`; service.get throws `AppError.notFound()` on null (service.ts:34-38) ‚Üí 404, so B requesting A's job id gets an indistinguishable 404 (no existence-leak, no row returned). `listOwned`/`countOwned` are `WHERE created_by=$1` (repository.ts:75-91) ‚Äî a user's list is strictly their own rows; there is NO unscoped list route and no `:id` path that omits the owner predicate. `requireUserId` (controller.ts:5-9) throws `AppError.unauthenticated()` (401) when `req.auth?.userId` is absent, so the actor id is always present and server-derived (never from the body/query). **No cross-user read path exists.** The runner-mutation methods (setRunning/setProgress/setSucceeded/setFailed/payload) are server-internal (called only by `runJob` in index.ts with the jobId it created) ‚Äî not reachable from any route. ‚öÝÔ∏è I could NOT find a `jobs.api.test.ts` in the slice (the rest of the slice ships source + ADR only) ‚Äî the "B-cannot-read-A's job ‚Üí 404" assertion is the obvious test to add; the CODE is correct by construction (owner predicate in the SQL), but the regression test is MISSING. Recorded as SHOULD-FIX, not a BLOCK (the scope is enforced in SQL, not test-dependent).
  - (2) ‚úÖ **SQL injection ‚Äî ORDER BY whitelisted via `JOB_PAGE_SPEC.sortMap`; all values bound `$1..$N`.** `listOwned` interpolates `${p.sortColumn} ${p.sortOrder}` (repository.ts:79) but `sortColumn` is produced ONLY by `resolvePage(rawQuery, JOB_PAGE_SPEC)` (service.ts:20): `JOB_PAGE_SPEC.sortMap = { createdAt: 'created_at' }` (service.ts:8) is the ONLY sortable field; `resolvePage` (pagination.ts:172-177) keeps `sortBy` only if `hasOwnProperty(sortMap, reqSortBy)` else falls back to `defaultSort='createdAt'`, then `sortColumn = sortMap[sortBy]` ‚Äî a server literal (`created_at`), NEVER the raw request string. `sortOrder` is hard-coerced `'desc'|'asc'` (pagination.ts:179-181). So `sortBy=created_at;DROP TABLE jobs` is not a sortMap key ‚Üí falls back to `created_at` ‚Üí injection-proof. The owner id (`$1`), limit (`$2`), offset (`$3`) are all bound; `countOwned` binds `$1`. No request-derived string reaches SQL text. Same trust model as the established sortMap control (DON'T-REGRESS rule honored: the single sortMap value is a real column literal). ‚úÖ
  - (3) ‚úÖ **`:id` uuid-shape guard PRESENT on `/jobs/:id` ‚Äî prevents pg 22P02 ‚Üí 500.** `jobController.get` (controller.ts:23-32) does `if (!UUID_RE.test(id)) throw AppError.notFound()` BEFORE calling `svc.get` (`UUID_RE = /^[0-9a-f]{8}-‚Ä¶-[0-9a-f]{12}$/i`, controller.ts:12). A non-uuid `:id` is a clean 404, never a `WHERE id=$1` cast error against the uuid column (22P02‚Üí500). Mirrors the audited `validateTaskRecordAccess`/parseId pattern. The list route has no `:id` so no guard needed. ‚úÖ
  - (4) ‚úÖ **No sensitive-data leak via `error`/`result`; `payload` NOT exposed.** `READ_COLS` (repository.ts:9) = `id, type, status, progress, stage, result, error, created_at, started_at, completed_at` ‚Äî **`payload` is DELIBERATELY EXCLUDED** from every client-facing read (insert RETURNING, getOwned, listOwned all use READ_COLS); the only `payload` reader is the server-internal `payload(id)` method (repository.ts:34-37) consumed by the runner, not any route. Confirmed the SDK `JobView` (packages/sdk/src/jobs.ts:16-28) also has no `payload` field ‚Äî DB projection ‚ü∑ SDK contract agree. `error` stores ONLY an AppError CODE or `Error.message` (index.ts:102: `e instanceof AppError ? e.code : e instanceof Error ? e.message : 'JOB_FAILED'`) ‚Äî **no stack trace** (the header comment is accurate; stack is logged server-side via `logger.warn`, never stored/returned). `result` is an artifact POINTER (`{storageKey,filename,rowCount}` per the header/SDK) ‚Äî no row data inlined; the actual download is a separate presigned-URL fetch (B-13, `JobResultUrl`), so the result column itself carries no PII bytes. NOTE (non-blocking): a processor that throws a `new Error()` with a sensitive message would persist that message into `error` (returned on read to the OWNER only) ‚Äî producers must keep processor error messages non-sensitive; for EXPORT/IMPORT the failure modes are row-count/format/storage errors, not credential-bearing ‚Äî acceptable today, WATCH as new job types land. ‚úÖ
  - (5) ‚úÖ **No `authorize()` gate on /jobs IS the CORRECT default-deny posture ‚Äî identity-scope, not a permission.** `jobRoutes` mounts `GET /` and `GET /:id` with NO `authorize(...)` (routes.ts:11-12) ‚Äî intentional and correct: a job tray is per-user personal state, scoped by IDENTITY (the `created_by` SQL predicate) exactly like `/notifications` and `/auth/me`, NOT by a role permission. The protection is twofold and complete: (a) the controller's `requireUserId` ‚Üí 401 when unauthenticated (so the route is NOT anonymous ‚Äî it requires a valid JWT, just no specific perm), and (b) every query is `created_by = actor` so a holder can only ever see their OWN rows. A permission gate here would be WRONG ‚Äî it would either over-restrict (a FIELD_AGENT who legitimately ran an export couldn't see their own job) or be redundant with the identity scope. This is the same posture the security ledger already blessed for the notification feed (identity-scoped, no perm). Default-deny is satisfied because the SQL owner-predicate is the deny boundary: absent a matching `created_by`, zero rows / 404. ‚úÖ Producers (the export/import endpoints that CREATE jobs via `enqueue`) keep their OWN `data.export`/`MASTERDATA_MANAGE` gates ‚Äî job CREATION is permissioned at the producer; job READING is identity-scoped here. Correct separation.
  - DISPOSITION: **PASS.** No BLOCK, no FLAG. IDOR-safe by SQL owner-predicate (404 for non-owner, no existence-leak), 401 unauth via requireUserId; ORDER BY whitelisted (single `createdAt`‚Üí`created_at` sortMap literal, all values bound); uuid-shape guard on `:id` (no 22P02‚Üí500); `payload` excluded from READ_COLS (DB‚ü∑SDK agree), `error`=code/message-no-stack, `result`=artifact pointer (no PII); no-authorize is the correct identity-scope default-deny (matches /notifications). **SHOULD-FIX (non-blocking):** add `jobs.api.test.ts` asserting (i) B requesting A's job id ‚Üí 404, (ii) `sortBy=created_at;DROP TABLE jobs` ‚Üí 200 + `sort.sortBy==='createdAt'`, (iii) non-uuid `:id` ‚Üí 404, (iv) unauth ‚Üí 401 ‚Äî the code is correct by construction but the regression net is missing. **WATCH (non-blocking):** new job types must keep processor error messages non-sensitive (persisted to `error`, returned to the owner). OPEN (carried, unaffected): standing sortMap/filterMap literal-only + parsed-filters-echo rules reaffirmed (this slice's single sortMap value is compliant).

- **2026-06-15 ¬∑ B-13 EXPORT-as-job slice (ADR-0030) ‚Äî `platform/export/job.ts` (NEW) + `modules/jobs/{service,controller}.resultUrl` + `modules/locations/{service.exportAllForJob,controller.export}` + `http/registerJobs.ts` (NEW) (uncommitted). VERDICT: PASS ‚Äî no BLOCK, no FLAG. (1 SHOULD-FIX: missing dedicated result-url IDOR test.)**
  - (1) ‚úÖ **result-url IDOR ‚Äî SAFE, gated at issuance by the owner-predicate; non-owner ‚Üí 404 BEFORE any URL is minted.** `GET /jobs/:id/result-url` ‚Üí `svc.resultUrl(userId,id)` (controller.ts:34-43, `userId` from `requireUserId(req)` = server-derived `req.auth.userId`, 401 if absent) ‚Üí `jobRepository.getOwned(id,userId)` = `SELECT ‚Ä¶ FROM jobs WHERE id=$1 AND created_by=$2` (repository.ts:67-73) ‚Üí `null` ‚Üí `AppError.notFound()` (service.ts:43-44). **The presigned URL is minted by `getStorage().signedUrl(result.storageKey)` (service.ts:49) ONLY AFTER `getOwned` returns a row** ‚Äî so user B requesting A's job id gets an indistinguishable 404 and NO URL is ever issued. No code path mints a URL without first passing the `created_by=actor` filter. The artifact is reachable ONLY via this owner-gated endpoint (the storageKey is never returned by `/jobs/:id` reads ‚Äî `payload` excluded from READ_COLS per the B-7.1 audit; `result` carries only `{storageKey,filename,rowCount}` to the owner). ‚öÝÔ∏è **SHOULD-FIX (test gap):** the test suite asserts B‚Üí404 on A's `/jobs/:id` (jobs.api.test.ts:114-118) and result-url‚Üí400 on B's OWN failed job (test:99-100), but there is NO assertion of B‚Üí404 on A's `/jobs/:id/result-url` specifically. The CODE is IDOR-safe by construction (result-url shares the identical `getOwned` owner-predicate as `/:id`), so this is a missing regression-net, NOT a defect ‚Äî add `B GET A's result-url ‚Üí 404` alongside the existing `/:id` IDOR test.
  - (2) ‚úÖ **Storage key ‚Äî no path traversal, both components server-derived.** `storageKey = exports/${p.actorId}/${ctx.jobId}.${p.format}` (job.ts:75). `actorId` = the payload's `actorId`, set server-side in `exportOrEnqueue` from `req.auth?.userId` (job.ts:97) ‚Üí flows verbatim into the payload (job.ts:125) ‚Äî NEVER client-supplied. `ctx.jobId` is the engine-minted job uuid (index.ts run loop). `format` is the ONLY component that originated from the request, but it is the validated `ex.format` ‚àà `{xlsx,csv}` enum (`resolveExport` throws 400 BAD_EXPORT_FORMAT on anything else, index.ts:25-29) ‚Üí no `../`, no slash, no traversal byte can reach the key. The key is fully server-controlled; a forged `format` can't escape the enum. ‚úÖ
  - (3) ‚úÖ **Worker re-resolves scope from the STORED server-trusted `actorId`, never a client value.** The job payload stores `{resource, query, format, cols, actorId}` (job.ts:59-65). The processor passes `p.actorId` (the stored, server-set id) to the builder (job.ts:73); the locations builder ignores it (`_actorId`, registerJobs.ts:15) because the pincode catalog is an UNSCOPED master-data table (no per-owner/territory predicate) ‚Äî correct for this resource. **Critically: `actorId` is set ONCE, server-side, from `req.auth?.userId` at enqueue (job.ts:97,110,125) and is the SAME id that owns the job row (`enqueue('EXPORT',payload,actorId)`, job.ts:126 ‚Üí `created_by`) ‚Äî so it is NOT spoofable** (no route accepts an `actorId` in the body/query; the only writer is `exportOrEnqueue` reading `req.auth`). PATTERN ASSESSMENT for when tasks/cases adopt this: ‚úÖ the design is correct ‚Äî the builder receives the trusted `actorId` and MUST re-resolve scope (userScope/dataScope) from it inside `exportAllForJob`, exactly as the synchronous list does, so a deferred job re-runs with the SAME scope the actor had at request time. **GATE (carry):** when a ROW-SCOPED resource (cases/tasks) registers a builder, its `exportAllForJob` MUST apply the scope WHERE clause keyed off the passed `actorId` (not echo the raw `query` filters unscoped) ‚Äî a builder that trusts `query` alone without re-deriving scope from `actorId` would export cross-scope rows. Locations is n/a (unscoped) so no leak today; flagged for the first scoped adopter.
  - (4) ‚úÖ **Presigned TTL from config ‚Äî bounded, no over-long exposure.** `signedUrl` passes `expiresIn: env.S3_SIGNED_URL_TTL_S` (storage/index.ts:98) ‚Äî `z.coerce.number().int().positive().default(900)` (config/index.ts:38) = 15 min default. URL is minted on-demand per result-url call (not at job creation), so the clock starts at download-request time, and each call is owner-gated (point 1). 15 min is a reasonable download window; no indefinite/long-lived link. ‚úÖ
  - (5) ‚úÖ **result-url on FAILED/PENDING/no-artifact ‚Üí 400, never a broken/forged URL.** `resultUrl` guards `if (status!=='SUCCEEDED' || !result) ‚Üí 400 JOB_NOT_READY` (service.ts:45-46) and `if (!result.storageKey) ‚Üí 400 JOB_NO_ARTIFACT` (service.ts:48) BEFORE calling `signedUrl` ‚Äî so a non-terminal/failed/artifact-less job yields a clean 400, never a URL pointing at a non-existent or wrong object (test:99-100 asserts the FAILED-job ‚Üí 400). ‚úÖ **CSV formula-injection UNAFFECTED ‚Äî escaping NOT bypassed.** The job path builds via `buildExportFile` ‚Üí `toCsv(rows, selected)` (job.ts:32-34) which is the SAME `toCsv` ‚Üí `escapeCsvCell` (format.ts:40-52: CWE-1236 leading `=+-@\t\r` ‚Üí `'`-prefix, RFC-4180 quoting) used by the synchronous `writeExport` (index.ts:84-87). The async builder reuses the identical `format.ts` engine ‚Äî no alternate CSV writer, no bypass. XLSX path likewise reuses `toXlsx`. ‚úÖ
  - DISPOSITION: **PASS.** No BLOCK, no FLAG. result-url IDOR-safe by the shared `getOwned` owner-predicate (404 before URL issuance, no existence-leak); storageKey fully server-derived (actorId from req.auth, jobId engine-minted, format enum-validated ‚Üí no traversal); worker scope re-resolves from the stored server-trusted actorId (unspoofable ‚Äî no route accepts it as input); TTL = config 900s on-demand; FAILED/PENDING/no-artifact ‚Üí 400 (no forged URL); CSV escaping reused unbypassed. **SHOULD-FIX (non-blocking):** add a `B ‚Üí A's /jobs/:id/result-url ‚Üí 404` regression test (code is correct by construction; net is missing). **GATE (carry):** the FIRST row-scoped resource (cases/tasks) to register a builder MUST re-derive scope from the passed `actorId` inside `exportAllForJob` ‚Äî locations is unscoped master-data so no cross-scope leak today.

---

## 2026-06-15 ‚Äî B-7.2 worker tier (Valkey + BullMQ out-of-process worker + 200k cap) ‚Äî VERDICT: PASS

Adversarial review of the uncommitted B-7.2 slice (`git diff`): `platform/jobs/index.ts`, `main.ts` (ROLE=worker), `registerJobs.ts`, `app.ts`, `platform/export/job.ts` + config (cap), `docker-compose.yml` (valkey :6380), `ALLOWED_DEPENDENCIES` (+bullmq), ADR-0030, `.env.example`.

### Findings

- **(1) SECRETS ‚Äî gitleaks-clean ‚úì.** No Valkey password in the diff. `connectionOpts(url)` parses host/port/username/password FROM the URL (`platform/jobs/index.ts`) ‚Äî prod supplies the credentialed `REDIS_QUEUE_URL` via env, never code. The only URLs in the slice are the commented dev examples `redis://127.0.0.1:6380` (auth-less localhost) in `.env.example` + `docker-compose.yml`. No `AKIA`, no PEM, no token literal. The single grep hit ("secret/token") was the unrelated nodemailer doc row in ALLOWED_DEPENDENCIES. Clean.
- **(2) actorId UNSPOOFABLE ‚úì.** The job payload (`{jobId,type,payload,userId}` into BullMQ + the `jobs` table) carries `actorId` set SERVER-SIDE at enqueue: `export/job.ts:112 actorId = req.auth?.userId` ‚Äî sourced from the verified JWT, never from the request body/query. No route accepts actorId as input, so a user cannot make their export job run as another actor. The worker re-runs `runJob(d.jobId, d.type, d.payload, d.userId)` using that stored, server-trusted userId; the storageKey it builds (`exports/${actorId}/${jobId}`) is therefore actor-namespaced from a trusted value ‚Äî no cross-actor artifact write. **GATE (carry, re-affirmed):** locations is UNSCOPED master-data so `exportAllForJob` applies no per-actor filter and leaks nothing today; the FIRST row-scoped resource (cases/tasks) to register a builder MUST re-resolve scope from the passed `actorId` INSIDE the worker (the worker has no req-scope), or a worker-run export silently bypasses dataScope. Code is correct for this slice; the pattern is the risk for adopters.
- **(3) VALKEY 0.0.0.0:6380 ‚Äî dev-acceptable, PROD-NOTE ‚úì.** `docker-compose.yml` binds `6380:6379` (host-published). For localhost dev this is acceptable (auth-less, ephemeral, queue data transient ‚Üí no volume). DEPLOY NOTE (must not regress): prod Valkey MUST NOT be publicly reachable ‚Äî bind to a private network/loopback and set an AUTH password in `REDIS_QUEUE_URL` (the code already reads it from the URL, so this is an ops/compose concern, not a code change). Flagged for deploy, not a slice defect.
- **(4) WORKER OPENS NO INBOUND PORT ‚úì.** `main.ts` ROLE=worker calls `initRealtime(createServer(), env)` with a FRESH `http.Server` that is never `.listen()`'d (only the `api` role calls `server.listen(env.PORT)` ‚Äî main.ts:20). socket.io attaches to the server object purely to engage the Valkey adapter for emit-only `job:progress`/`job:done` fan-out; no socket binds a TCP port. The worker carries DB + storage + FCM creds (same image) but exposes ZERO HTTP attack surface. Confirmed.
- **(5) PII LIFECYCLE IN VALKEY ‚Äî acceptable ‚úì.** `enqueue` adds with `{removeOnComplete: true, removeOnFail: 500}`. On success the BullMQ job (which held the payload) is dropped immediately ‚Üí no lingering data in Valkey. The payload itself carries only the export `query` (filter params: pincode/state/active flags) + `actorId` + format/cols ‚Äî NOT exported PII rows (the rows are fetched fresh at run time, written to S3, never put on the queue). So the ‚â§500 retained FAILED jobs hold only filter-params + a userId, not raw subject data ‚Äî low-sensitivity, acceptable. (Hygiene-only carry: a userId is weak PII; if a row-scoped/sensitive-filter resource later rides this queue, revisit removeOnFail retention.)

DISPOSITION: **PASS** ‚Äî no BLOCK, no FLAG-must-fix. Secrets clean (auth from env-URL, none committed); actorId server-set + unspoofable, worker re-runs on the trusted id; worker opens no port; success drops the payload, failures retain only low-sensitivity filter-params. **DEPLOY-GATE (carry):** prod Valkey must be private + AUTH-password'd (compose binds 0.0.0.0 for dev only). **SCOPE-GATE (carry):** first row-scoped builder MUST re-resolve dataScope from the passed actorId inside the worker.

---

## 2026-06-15 ‚Äî B-14 background large-import tier (ADR-0030) ‚Äî VERDICT: PASS

Adversarial review of the uncommitted B-14 slice: `platform/import/index.ts` (`importConfirmOrEnqueue`, `importJobProcessor`, `ImportRunner` registry), `platform/storage/index.ts` (+`get`), `modules/locations/{service,controller}.ts`, `http/registerJobs.ts`, `modules/locations/routes.ts`. Context: confirm ‚â•10k ‚Üí store uploaded bytes at `imports/{userId}/{uuid}.bin` + enqueue an IMPORT job `{resource,storageKey,fileName,userId}`; worker `storage.get` ‚Üí registered runner (`locationService.importConfirm`).
