Verified live: 10001-row ‚Üí SUCCEEDED 10001/10001, import_log written, file removed.

### Findings

- **(1) ‚úÖ Storage key ‚Äî no path traversal, both components server-derived; payload.userId UNSPOOFABLE.** `storageKey = imports/${ctx.userId}/${randomUUID()}.bin` (`import/index.ts:326`). `ctx.userId` = controller `userId(req) = req.auth?.userId` (`locations/controller.ts:14,70`) ‚Äî sourced from the verified JWT in `authenticate.ts:16` (`req.auth = {userId: claims.userId, role}`), NEVER from body/headers/query. `randomUUID()` is server-generated. No request-controlled component reaches the key ‚Üí no `../`, no slash-injection. The enqueued payload's `userId` is the SAME server-set value (`import/index.ts:330`), and the worker passes it verbatim as the import actor + `created_by` (`registerJobs.ts:33-35` ‚Üí `importConfirm(buffer, ctx.userId, ‚Ä¶)` ‚Üí `locationService.create(input, userId)` ‚Üí `repo.create` binds it into `created_by`/`updated_by` `INSERT ‚Ä¶ created_by=$7` `repository.ts:119-127`). No route accepts `userId` as input ‚Äî unspoofable. NOTE: the controller's `?? 'unknown'` fallback (`controller.ts:14`) is DEAD on this route ‚Äî `authorize` returns 401 if `req.auth` is absent (`packages/access/src/authorize.ts:25-28`), so by `c.import` `req.auth.userId` is guaranteed present; harmless (no key/actor ever becomes the literal 'unknown' here), but flagged so it isn't mistaken for a real anonymous-import path.
- **(2) ‚úÖ Import RBAC-gated at the upload endpoint ‚Äî the job-in-worker-runs-unauthenticated concern is mooted by the gate.** `POST /locations/import` mounts `authorize(PERMISSIONS.MASTERDATA_MANAGE)` (`routes.ts:21`, `masterdata.manage`) ahead of `raw({type:()=>true, limit:'10mb'})` + `c.import`. The IMPORT job itself runs with no req-auth in the worker, but ONLY an authorized upload can enqueue it (the only `enqueue('IMPORT',‚Ä¶)` writer is `importConfirmOrEnqueue`, reachable only via the gated controller). The worker re-runs `locationService.importConfirm` ‚Üí audited `create` per row, so every imported row appends an `audit_log` CREATE keyed to the trusted `created_by`. Same pattern as B-13 EXPORT ‚Äî server-trusted actor flows through the payload into the worker. ‚úÖ
- **(3) ‚öÝÔ∏è ORPHANED-FILE on FAILURE ‚Äî acceptable for locations (low-sensitivity), CARRY for future PII imports.** `getStorage().remove(p.storageKey)` is best-effort cleanup AFTER the runner returns (`import/index.ts:295`). If the runner THROWS (parse error, NO_IMPORT_RUNNER, storage.get failure, or worker crash mid-run) the `remove` line is never reached ‚Üí the uploaded file is RETAINED in object storage with no TTL/lifecycle reaping. For locations the bytes = pincode/area/city rows (public master-data, no PII) ‚Üí acceptable. **CARRY (gate for future scoped/PII imports ‚Äî users, case-creation):** when a domain whose import file carries PII adopts this runner, a failed/crashed job leaves subject PII orphaned in the bucket indefinitely. Mitigate before that adoption: either (a) a `try/finally` around the runner so `remove` runs on failure too (the file is re-uploadable; retaining it buys nothing on a hard failure), or (b) an S3/MinIO lifecycle expiry on the `imports/` prefix. Not gating for locations.
- **(4) ‚úÖ Content/magic-byte validation ‚Äî parse is the trust boundary, no RCE, no eval/formula execution.** No xlsx/csv magic-byte check before `put` (`importConfirmOrEnqueue` stores whatever bytes the gated caller POSTed). A malformed/non-spreadsheet file is parsed by `parseImportFile` (exceljs/CSV); a parse failure throws ‚Üí the job ends FAILED (and the file is retained per (3)), NOT code execution. exceljs READS cell values (no formula evaluation ‚Äî stored formula strings are read as text, not computed) and CSV is plain text; values then flow through the per-column zod `schema` (`validateRows`) before any DB write, and writes are parameterized (`$1..$7`, `repository.ts:119`) so no SQL injection from cell content. CSV-formula-injection on the EXPORT side is already escaped (`format.ts escapeCsvCell`, B-13 audit); on IMPORT the cells are validated input, never re-emitted to a CSV here. The 10mb `raw` limit bounds the upload. Trust boundary is sound ‚Äî worst case is a clean FAILED job. ‚úÖ

DISPOSITION: **PASS** ‚Äî no BLOCK, no FLAG-must-fix. storageKey fully server-derived (userId from req.auth via verified JWT, uuid server-gen ‚Üí no traversal); payload.userId = import actor + created_by is unspoofable (no route accepts it); upload gated by `masterdata.manage` (the unauthenticated worker job is reachable only via an authorized enqueue); parse is the trust boundary (malformed file ‚Üí FAILED job, no eval/formula exec/SQLi ‚Äî exceljs reads values, writes parameterized). **NOTE (non-blocking):** controller `userId ?? 'unknown'` fallback is dead behind `authorize`'s 401. **CARRY (gate for the first PII import ‚Äî users/case-creation):** on-FAILURE the uploaded file is NOT removed (only the success path calls `remove`) ‚Äî wrap the runner in `try/finally` or add an `imports/`-prefix lifecycle expiry before any PII-bearing domain adopts this runner; locations (public master-data) is n/a today.

---

## 2026-06-15 ‚Äî B-5 Saved Views (per-user DataGrid views, own-user/identity scope) ‚Äî VERDICT: PASS

Adversarial review of the uncommitted B-5 slice: `modules/saved-views/{routes,controller,service,repository}.ts` + `__tests__/saved-views.api.test.ts`, `db/v2/migrations/0051_saved_views.sql`, `packages/sdk/src/savedViews.ts`, `app.ts` mount, `apps/web/src/components/ui/data-grid/SavedViewsPicker.tsx`. The own-user scope IS the security boundary (identity, like /notifications, /jobs) ‚Äî scrutinized as such.

### Findings

- **(1) ‚úÖ IDOR / horizontal privesc ‚Äî SAFE by SQL owner-predicate on EVERY read+write; non-owner ‚Üí indistinguishable 404, no existence-leak.** `userId` is server-derived at every entry: `requireUserId(req)=req.auth?.userId` (controller.ts:6-9, 401 if absent) ‚Äî and `req.auth.userId` is set ONLY by `authenticate.ts:16` (verified JWT `claims.userId`) or the dev-only `testAuth.ts:11-12` (`x-test-auth` header, mounted behind `NODE_ENV!=='production'` app.ts:70). It is NEVER read from body/query. Every repo query carries `WHERE ‚Ä¶ user_id = $N` bound to that actor: `listByResource` (repository.ts:33), `update` (`WHERE id=$ AND user_id=$`, :86), `remove` (:99), `setDefault` (owner-check SELECT :113 + both UPDATEs :121/:126). A non-owner/unknown/absent id returns `null`/0-rows ‚Üí service maps to `AppError.notFound()` (service.ts:40,46,53) ‚Äî a non-owner gets the SAME 404 as a nonexistent id (no 403, no leak of existence). `list` is resource-filtered to the actor only (no `:id`, nothing to IDOR). Test proves cross-user isolation directly: B lists A's resource ‚Üí 0 rows (test:61-62); B PUT/set-default/DELETE A's id ‚Üí 404 (test:106-108, 162-170, 179). ‚úÖ
- **(2) ‚úÖ create() cannot set another user's user_id ‚Äî forced from req.auth, NOT body.** `svc.create(requireUserId(req), req.body)` (controller.ts:32) ‚Üí `repo.create({userId, ‚Ä¶input})` (service.ts:25-31) where `userId` is the actor and the zod `CreateSavedViewSchema` has NO `userId`/`user_id` field (savedViews.ts:29-34) ‚Äî a body-supplied `user_id` is simply dropped by zod parse. The INSERT binds `$1=r.userId` (repository.ts:50-53). No mass-assignment path. ‚úÖ
- **(3) ‚úÖ Injection ‚Äî `state` jsonb is bound + stored opaque, never interpolated; no user-controlled ORDER BY.** `state` is ALWAYS `JSON.stringify(...)` bound as a `$N::jsonb` parameter (insert repository.ts:53, update :78-79) ‚Äî never string-concatenated into SQL. The dynamic SET clause in `update` is built from a fixed `sets[]` of literal `name = $N` / `state = $N::jsonb` fragments with server-computed `$`-indices (repository.ts:71-88) ‚Äî the param VALUES are user data but the SQL TEXT is literal; the trailing `id=$N-1 AND user_id=$N` indices are correct (params pushed last, :82). `name`/`resourceKey` likewise bound. List ORDER BY is the static literal `is_default DESC, name ASC` (repository.ts:34) ‚Äî no `sortBy` reaches it, no whitelist needed. No raw user text in any SQL string. ‚úÖ
- **(4) ‚úÖ Input validation ‚Äî zod bounds prevent jsonb bloat / DoS.** `resourceKey` ‚â§64, `name` 1-120, `state` = `z.record(z.string().max(64), z.string().max(2000))` (savedViews.ts:27) ‚Äî bounds BOTH keys (‚â§64) and values (‚â§2000), capping row size. `UpdateSavedViewSchema` `.refine` rejects an empty body ‚Üí 400 (savedViews.ts:43-45; test:123). DB columns match (`varchar(64)`/`varchar(120)`, migration:14-15). Zod throws ZodError ‚Üí 400 before any DB call. Note: `z.record` does not cap the NUMBER of keys, so a payload with very many ‚â§64-char keys is theoretically large ‚Äî but the express `json` body limit bounds the request, and the values are FE URL-state keys (a fixed small set: q/sort/dir/size/cols/f_*), so practical bloat is negligible. Non-blocking observation, not a defect.
- **(5) ‚úÖ AuthN ‚Äî 401 unauth, uuid shape-guard prevents 22P02‚Üí500.** All routes sit behind `authenticate()`+`enrichAuth()` (app.ts:71-72, before the mount at :100); `requireUserId` 401s when `req.auth` is absent (test:36-37 asserts unauth ‚Üí 401). `requireUuid` (controller.ts:14-19) regex-validates `:id` before it reaches the uuid column ‚Üí a non-uuid id is a clean 404, never a pg `22P02` 500 (test:119-121). ‚úÖ
- **(6) ‚úÖ No wrong permission gate; no cross-tenant path.** Routes mount NO `authorize()`/`dataScope`/`userScope`/`validateTaskRecordAccess` (grep empty) ‚Äî correct for an identity-scoped resource (matches /notifications, /jobs; default-deny is satisfied by the mandatory `user_id=actor` predicate, not a permission code). There is genuinely no shared/cross-user read path: the table has no team/territory/portfolio column, every query keys on `user_id`, and `ON DELETE CASCADE` ties rows to the owner (migration:12). A TL/MGR cannot see a subordinate's views (none exists ‚Äî by design, these are personal UI prefs). ‚úÖ
- **(7) ‚úÖ PII/DPDP ‚Äî `state.q` may hold a search term (e.g. an applicant name typed into grid search); ACCEPTABLE for personal config.** The `state` map can contain a free-text search value the user typed, which COULD incidentally be PII (a name/phone the operator searched). Judged acceptable: (a) it is the user's OWN saved query, readable only by them (own-user scope, finding 1), never shared/exported; (b) it is UI preference, not a subject-data record, and is purged on user delete via CASCADE; (c) it is no more sensitive than the browser URL/history that already holds the same `?q=` param. Not flagged. WATCH (non-blocking): if a future "share this view with my team" feature is added, this PII judgment MUST be revisited ‚Äî a shared view would expose one user's typed search terms to others.
- **(8) ‚úÖ FE no injection sink.** `SavedViewsPicker.tsx`: `applyState` writes captured keys into a fresh `URLSearchParams` (:41-43) ‚Äî no `innerHTML`/`dangerouslySetInnerHTML`/`eval`; `v.name` is rendered as JSX text (React-escaped) and only used in `title`/`aria-label` strings. SDK `savedViews.*` takes no `userId` param and `encodeURIComponent`s `resourceKey` into the query string (client.ts:595). ‚úÖ

DISPOSITION: **PASS.** No BLOCK, no FLAG. IDOR-safe by mandatory `user_id=actor` predicate on every read+write (non-owner ‚Üí indistinguishable 404, no existence-leak); create forces userId from verified `req.auth`, not body (no mass-assignment ‚Äî schema has no userId field); `state` jsonb always bound `$N::jsonb` + stored opaque (no interpolation); ORDER BY is a static literal (no user-controlled sort); zod bounds key‚â§64/value‚â§2000/name‚â§120 cap row size; 401 unauth + uuid-shape-guard (no 22P02‚Üí500); correctly NO authorize() (identity scope) and no cross-tenant column/path; `state.q` search-term PII acceptable for an own-user, CASCADE-purged personal config. API test proves cross-user isolation across list/update/set-default/delete. **WATCH (non-blocking):** (a) `z.record` does not cap key COUNT (express json limit bounds it ‚Äî negligible today); (b) if a "share view with team" feature is ever added, the `state.q` PII judgment must be re-reviewed (a shared view would leak one user's typed search terms).

## 2026-06-15 ‚Äî ADR-0032 Case/Task Lifecycle Redesign (DESIGN-ONLY review of `2026-06-15-v2-lifecycle-redesign.md` ¬ß5/¬ß8) ‚Äî VERDICT: FLAG (no BLOCK)

Adversarial design review of the PROPOSED lifecycle redesign. No code in scope (design doc only). Reviewed ¬ß8 new perms, ¬ß5 ingest IDOR surface, ¬ß3 case-finalize scope, attachment serve, idempotency replay/forgery, REVOKE-of-COMPLETED, the `/api/mobile‚Üí/api/v2` rebase, and the office-queue ORDER BY. Verified against the shipped scope/auth seam: `platform/scope/index.ts:79` (`taskScopePredicate`), `platform/scope/repository.ts:36-59` (`getScopedUserIds`/`resolveScope`), `modules/cases/repository.ts:512-536` (`taskAssignmentState`), `modules/cases/routes.ts`, `packages/access/src/permissions.ts:63-95`.

### Findings

- **(1) ‚úÖ ¬ß8 default-deny grants ‚Äî CORRECT, no over-grant.** All four NEW perms are additive to the frozen 6-role model (`permissions.ts:5-12`); `Object.values(PERMISSIONS)` auto-includes SUPER_ADMIN (`:64`), so SA inherits each ‚Äî expected. `task.execute`‚ÜíFIELD_AGENT only (matches today's `FIELD_AGENT:[CASE_VIEW,LOCATION_CAPTURE]` minimal grant, `:93`); `task.revoke`‚ÜíBACKEND_USER+MANAGER; `case.finalize`‚ÜíBACKEND_USER+SA; `case.revoke`‚ÜíMANAGER+SA. KYC_VERIFIER stays read-only (`:94`, no execute/complete/finalize) ‚Äî consistent with the doc's ¬ß8 and ADR-0025. No perm granted to a role that shouldn't drive that surface; default-deny intact (any role not listed is denied by absence). Design is sound; the live gate will be the `role_permissions` table (ADR-0022), so the BUILD must seed these four rows for exactly the listed roles and the parity test must assert it.
- **(2) ‚öÝÔ∏è FLAG ‚Äî ¬ß5 ingest IDOR is "scope-guarded", NOT "assignee-guarded"; the two coincide ONLY because FIELD_AGENT hierarchy mode = SELF. Make this an explicit invariant or it silently rots.** The doc says "Auth = the assignee; scope-guarded (404 IDOR-safe)" (¬ß5 last line). But the shipped guard the spine will reuse ‚Äî `taskAssignmentState`‚Üí`taskScopePredicate` ‚Äî has hierarchy leg `ct.assigned_to = ANY($ids) OR cs.created_by = ANY($ids)` (`scope/index.ts:84`), where `$ids = getScopedUserIds(actor)`. For FIELD_AGENT that resolves to `[self]` (SELF mode / fail-closed default, `repository.ts:39,58`) and a field agent never creates cases, so the predicate collapses to "assigned_to = me" ‚Äî assignee-binding holds **today**. The risk: this is **scope ‚âÝ ownership**. If `task.execute` were ever granted to a role with a wider hierarchy mode (MANAGER=SUBTREE, TL=DIRECT_TEAM), that holder could start/submit/complete/revoke a SUBORDINATE'S task through the device endpoints ‚Äî there is NO `assigned_to = req.auth.userId` assertion anywhere in the complete path (confirmed: `01-v2-backend.md` ¬ß5 finalize guard uses only the scope predicate). **MUST (build-time):** either (a) keep `task.execute` FIELD_AGENT-only AND add a parity test that fails if any non-SELF-mode role holds it, or (b) add an explicit `assigned_to = actor` assertion on the device start/submit/complete/revoke writes (defence-in-depth ‚Äî the v1 IDOR-history surface deserves both). Record as a standing invariant: *device-execution endpoints bind to the CURRENT assignee, not merely to hierarchy scope.*
- **(3) ‚úÖ start/submit/complete/attachments/revoke IDOR otherwise sufficient.** Given (2)'s FIELD_AGENT-only constraint, "assignee + scope-guarded 404" IS sufficient: out-of-scope/missing ‚â° `null` ‚â° 404 TASK_NOT_FOUND (indistinguishable, no existence-leak ‚Äî same shape as the shipped finalize guard, `01-v2-backend.md` ¬ß5.3). `:id` = task UUID with a shape-guard (device throws on non-UUID; backend must `requireUuid` before the uuid-column WHERE to avoid `22P02`‚Üí500 ‚Äî carry the saved-views pattern). A field agent CANNOT act on a task not theirs because the scope predicate excludes it. ‚úÖ ‚Äî contingent on (2).
- **(4) ‚öÝÔ∏è FLAG ‚Äî ¬ß3 `case.finalize` scope-guard MUST be CASE-grain, applied to BOTH the queue read and the finalize write, and bound to the actor's portfolio ‚Äî not left unscoped like today's cases LIST.** The doc grants `case.finalize` to BACKEND_USER+SA and adds an AWAITING_COMPLETION office queue (¬ß9). Standing OPEN from 2026-06-06: the cases LIST has **no row-level scope** ‚Äî any `case.view` holder sees every case (carried gap, sibling of B-20). If the new office queue reuses that unscoped list, a BACKEND_USER sees (and can finalize) cases outside their portfolio. **MUST (build-time):** the finalize endpoint must `composeScopePredicate(..., 'CASE')` (the case-grain `cs.created_by = ANY($ids) OR <portfolio dimension>` leg) on the `WHERE` of BOTH the AWAITING_COMPLETION queue read AND the finalize UPDATE (404 on out-of-scope), so a backend user cannot finalize a case they can't see. BACKEND_USER hierarchy mode + CLIENT/PRODUCT portfolio RESTRICT wiring (`scope/repository.ts:94-119`) is the right scoping primitive. Without this, `case.finalize` is a horizontal-privesc surface on the single authoritative result (¬ß4).
- **(5) ‚úÖ Attachment serve = presigned, scope-at-issuance ‚Äî IDOR-safe pattern, with one caveat.** ¬ß5 reuses the ADR-0021 storage seam + ADR-0025-B2 `case_attachments`. The shipped `GET /:id/attachments/:attachmentId/url` is `case.view`-gated and scope-checked at issuance (`routes.ts`). Presigned-URL-at-issuance is IDOR-safe IF: (a) the scope check runs on the task/case BEFORE minting the URL (it does today), and (b) the presign TTL is short (the bearer of the URL has time-boxed access ‚Äî standard). **WATCH (build):** the device upload path (`POST ‚Ä¶/attachments` multipart) must run the SAME assignee/scope guard as (2) before storing bytes + linking ‚Äî an unscoped upload could attach evidence to another agent's task. Sha256 dedupe is fine (content-addressed, no cross-task leak since the link row is scoped).
- **(6) ‚úÖ Idempotency-Key replay/forgery ‚Äî LOW risk, contract-preserving.** The device sends `Idempotency-Key = operationId` on every write (`03-mobile.md` ¬ß2). Replay protection (same key+body ‚Üí dedup) is a *correctness* control, not an auth control ‚Äî every request is independently JWT+scope-gated, so a forged/guessed key cannot bypass auth (a forged key on a task the actor can't scope still 404s). The only forgery concern: if two DIFFERENT bodies share one key, the backend must return the FIRST result (not silently apply the second) ‚Äî standard idempotency semantics; not a security hole. 409=success on start/complete/revoke (NOT on submit/priority) is a locked contract shape (ADR-0012) ‚Äî preserve verbatim or the device DLQs (`03-mobile.md` risk #4). No new attack surface.
- **(7) ‚úÖ REVOKE on a COMPLETED task ‚Äî bounded, not abusable.** ¬ß2 allows `COMPLETED‚ÜíREVOKED` (office/MGR via `task.revoke`, requires reason, "no commission", rollup recheck). This is the kill-switch for a bad completion; abuse potential is low because: (a) `task.revoke` is BACKEND_USER+MANAGER only (not field), (b) it's append-only audited + version-bumped, (c) commission is gated on COMPLETED-&-!REVOKED (¬ß5/slice-5) so a revoke correctly claws back the payout ‚Äî no double-pay, no orphaned commission. WATCH (build): ensure the revoke-of-COMPLETED path is also CASE/TASK-scope-guarded (a MANAGER can only revoke within subtree) and that it CANNOT be device-initiated against a COMPLETED task (the doc says device revoke is allowed ‚Äî must be restricted to the agent's own non-terminal task, else a field agent could self-revoke a delivered task to dodge a result; ¬ß7 "never transition COMPLETED back on device" already covers this ‚Äî enforce server-side too).
- **(8) ‚úÖ Mobile rebase `/api/mobile ‚Üí /api/v2` ‚Äî JWT/auth UNCHANGED, design honors it.** D4 explicitly keeps the locked contract SHAPES (headers/idempotency/409-semantics/JWT) and moves ONLY the base path. `Authorization: Bearer` + `traceparent` + `X-Platform`/`X-App-Version` headers are unchanged (`03-mobile.md` ¬ß2). v2 already authenticates via the same JWT seam (`authenticate.ts` verified claims.userId, used by saved-views review). No re-auth, no token-shape change ‚Üí no auth regression. The path move is an API-contract concern (route 404 risk if device not rebased first) ‚Äî that's API/Contract auditor's lane, not a security defect.
- **(9) ‚úÖ Office queue ORDER BY ‚Äî must use the shipped sortMap whitelist.** The new AWAITING_COMPLETION queue is a list; the standing sort-injection control (`platform/pagination.ts resolvePage` ‚Üí `PageSpec.sortMap` whitelist, falls back to `defaultSort`, `sortOrder` pinned asc/desc) MUST apply. **MUST (build):** the queue's `PageSpec.sortMap` contains ONLY real server-literal columns; never interpolate raw `sortBy`. If the queue is CASE-grain, apply the case row-scope (finding 4) to BOTH the items AND the COUNT query so a filtered totalCount can't leak out-of-scope case existence.

DISPOSITION: **FLAG (no BLOCK).** The design is fundamentally sound and IDOR-safe BY THE FROZEN PATTERNS ‚Äî but two latent traps must become explicit build-time invariants, and three must-honors carried forward:
- **MUST-FIX (build, finding 2):** device-execution endpoints (start/submit/complete/revoke/attachments) must bind to the CURRENT ASSIGNEE, not merely hierarchy scope. Either keep `task.execute` FIELD_AGENT-only with a parity test, OR add an explicit `assigned_to = actor` assertion (prefer both ‚Äî v1 had IDOR history here).
- **MUST-FIX (build, finding 4):** `case.finalize` + the AWAITING_COMPLETION queue must apply CASE-grain scope (`composeScopePredicate 'CASE'`) on BOTH the read AND the finalize write ‚Äî do NOT inherit today's unscoped cases-LIST gap. A BACKEND_USER must not finalize a case outside their portfolio.
- **MUST-HONOR (findings 5/7/9):** scope-guard the device attachment UPLOAD; restrict device-revoke to the agent's own non-terminal task (no COMPLETED‚ÜíREVOKED from device); office-queue ORDER BY via the sortMap whitelist + scope on items+COUNT.
- **CONFIRMED SAFE:** ¬ß8 default-deny grants (no over-grant), Idempotency-Key (auth-orthogonal, no bypass), JWT unchanged on the v2 rebase, presigned-at-issuance pattern, REVOKE-of-COMPLETED commission clawback.

OPEN (carried): the cases-LIST row-scope gap (2026-06-06) now becomes BLOCKING for `case.finalize` ‚Äî must be closed as part of slice 1, not deferred. Re-verify all four new perms are seeded to exactly the ¬ß8 roles in `role_permissions` with a parity test.

## 2026-06-15 ‚Äî ADR-0032 slice-1 commit review (case finalize) ‚Äî VERDICT: PASS (my two design-review MUST-FIXes for the finalize path are met)

Adversarial per-commit review of the shipped slice-1 diff: `modules/cases/{routes,controller,service,repository}.ts`, `packages/access/src/permissions.ts`, `db/v2/migrations/0052_case_lifecycle.sql`, `sdk/cases.ts`, FE `CaseDetailPage.tsx`. Verified against the live scope/auth seam (`scope/repository.ts:36-119`, `composeScopePredicate`, `caseScopePredicate` repo:167-175). Scope of this slice = case FINALIZE + the status-rollup writer; **no AWAITING_COMPLETION queue endpoint ships yet** (finding-4's "queue READ scope" is therefore N/A this slice, carried).

- **(1) ‚úÖ CASE-grain scope on finalize ‚Äî MY BLOCKING REQUIREMENT MET (design finding 4).** `caseFinalizeState(caseId, scope)` (repo:725-740) composes `caseScopePredicate(params, scope)` (repo:167-175 ‚Üí `composeScopePredicate`, the case-grain `cs.created_by = ANY($ids) OR EXISTS(case_tasks assigned_to = ANY($ids))` leg, intersected with portfolio RESTRICT) into `WHERE cs.id=$1 AND (${pred})`; out-of-scope/missing ‚Üí `row ?? null` ‚Üí service maps to **404 CASE_NOT_FOUND** (service.ts:330-332). Identical IDOR-safe shape to the established `taskAssignmentState`. Not the unscoped cases-LIST path ‚Äî the design carry was honored. The finalize WRITE (`finalizeCase` repo:758) additionally re-pins `WHERE id=$1 AND version=$5 AND status='AWAITING_COMPLETION'`, so even if the pre-check scope read raced, the write cannot touch a row outside the version+status it was authorized against (scope is enforced at the read that gates the write; a TOCTOU here can only 409, never widen access). **Test proves it: out-of-scope BACKEND_USER ‚Üí 404** (cases.api.test.ts:901-909, `be_fin2_out` with no portfolio grant).
- **(2) ‚úÖ Route default-deny gated `case.finalize` (design finding 1).** `POST /:id/finalize` mounts `authorize(PERMISSIONS.CASE_FINALIZE)` (routes.ts:23). `authorize` is fail-closed (no auth‚Üí401, `!roleHas`‚Üí403). Test: KYC_VERIFIER ‚Üí **403** (cases.api.test.ts:893-900) ‚Äî fires BEFORE any scope/state check, so a read-only role never reaches the finalize logic.
- **(3) ‚úÖ Perm NOT over-granted ‚Äî BACKEND_USER + SA only.** `ROLE_PERMISSIONS.BACKEND_USER` adds `CASE_FINALIZE` (permissions.ts block line 28); SUPER_ADMIN inherits via `Object.values(PERMISSIONS)`. Grepped the block: `CASE_FINALIZE` appears in NO other role ‚Äî MANAGER, TEAM_LEADER, FIELD_AGENT (`[CASE_VIEW, LOCATION_CAPTURE]`), KYC_VERIFIER (`[CASE_VIEW, DASHBOARD_VIEW]`) all lack it. Migration 0052 seed (`role_permissions`) inserts ONLY `('BACKEND_USER','case.finalize')` ON CONFLICT DO NOTHING (SA covered by grants_all) ‚Äî matches `@crm2/access` exactly. **KYC_VERIFIER confirmed unable to finalize** (perm-absent + 403 test). No DB/code drift.
- **(4) ‚úÖ OCC version on the authoritative verdict ‚Äî no lost update.** `requireVersion(input)` (service.ts:327 ‚Üí 400 VERSION_REQUIRED if absent, OUTSIDE the zod schema). Write is compare-and-set `WHERE ‚Ä¶ version=$5 AND status='AWAITING_COMPLETION'` then `version=version+1` (repo:756-760); 0-row ‚Üí re-reads current ‚Üí 404 / INVALID_TRANSITION / `AppError.stale`‚Üí**409 STALE_UPDATE** (repo:763-769). The rollup writer (`recomputeCaseStatus`) ALSO bumps `version`, so a concurrent re-open between the scope-read and the finalize correctly trips the stale guard rather than overwriting. Test: `version-1` ‚Üí 409 (cases.api.test.ts:910-918). Money/verdict path is race-safe.
- **(5) ‚úÖ IDOR / injection / ORDER BY ‚Äî clean.** `:id` ‚Üí `parseId` = `parseUuidParam` (controller.ts:9-14): `UUID_RE.test(v)` else 400 BAD_REQUEST ‚Äî a non-uuid never reaches the uuid-column `WHERE id=$1` (no `22P02`‚Üí500, no injection). EVERY value in both new SQL statements is bound (`$1..$5`: caseId/outcome/remark/actorId/version); zero `${}` of request data. `result` is `z.enum(KYC_RESULTS)` (POSITIVE/NEGATIVE/REFER/FRAUD) ‚Äî DB CHECK `chk_cases_verification_outcome` is a defense-in-depth mirror; `remark` `z.string().trim().max(2000)`. No ORDER BY anywhere in the new code. `completed_by`/`updated_by`/`actorId` flow from `actor(req)` (verified JWT), never from the body ‚Äî no mass-assignment (schema has only `result`+`remark`).
- **(6) ‚úÖ No PII/secret regression; anti-staleness verdict-clear is sound.** New SELECT cols are case-verdict fields (`verification_outcome`/`result_remark`/`completed_at`/`version` + `completed_by_name` via LEFT JOIN users) ‚Äî staff-name + office decision, not new customer PII; behind the existing `case.view` gate. `recomputeCaseStatus` clears the verdict columns on any non-COMPLETED transition (re-open invalidation, ADR-0032 ¬ß4) ‚Äî correct: a stale verdict can't survive a revisit. No `console.*`/secrets/`SELECT *` in the diff (scanned). Migration is forward-only/idempotent, status widen is a strict superset (no data migration).

DISPOSITION: **PASS.** No BLOCK, no FLAG. My two design-review MUST-FIXes that apply to THIS slice are satisfied: **(finding 4) case-grain scope predicate IS on the finalize read‚Üíwrite (out-of-scope BACKEND_USER ‚Üí 404, test-proven), NOT the unscoped LIST path**; **(finding 1) perms seeded to exactly BACKEND_USER+SA in both code and the 0052 DB seed, KYC_VERIFIER read-only confirmed.** OCC compare-and-set guards the authoritative verdict; uuid-shape-guarded :id; fully parameterized; no ORDER BY surface. CARRIED (not in this slice, re-verify when they land): the AWAITING_COMPLETION office-QUEUE read must apply the SAME case-grain scope to items+COUNT (sortMap whitelist) ‚Äî finding 4's queue leg; and the device-execution assignee-binding MUST-FIX (design finding 2, slice 2 ingest) is untouched here. The 2026-06-06 cases-LIST row-scope gap remains OPEN for the list/queue, now non-blocking for finalize (finalize has its own scope guard).

## 2026-06-15 ‚Äî ADR-0032 slice-2c-1 commit review (FIELD-EXECUTION ingest spine) ‚Äî VERDICT: PASS (my design-review MUST-FIX finding-2 ‚Äî `task.execute` FIELD_AGENT-only + explicit assigned_to=actor binding ‚Äî is MET, test-proven)

Adversarial per-commit review of the NEW `modules/verification-tasks/{routes,controller,service}.ts` + `__tests__/verification-tasks.api.test.ts`, the device repo methods in `modules/cases/repository.ts` (esp. `taskForAssignee`), `packages/access/src/permissions.ts`, `db/v2/migrations/0053_task_execute_perm.sql`, `http/app.ts` mount. The field-execution surface where v1 had IDOR history ‚Äî reviewed paranoid. (VT module is untracked; read on disk.)

- **(a) ‚úÖ `task.execute` NOT over-granted ‚Äî FIELD_AGENT only (+ SA grants_all).** `ROLE_PERMISSIONS.FIELD_AGENT = [CASE_VIEW, LOCATION_CAPTURE, TASK_EXECUTE]` (permissions.ts:100); grepped the block ‚Äî `TASK_EXECUTE`/`'task.execute'` appears in NO other role (MANAGER/TEAM_LEADER/BACKEND_USER/KYC_VERIFIER all lack it); SUPER_ADMIN inherits via `Object.values(PERMISSIONS)`. **Code‚ÜîDB parity:** migration 0053 inserts ONLY `('FIELD_AGENT','task.execute') ON CONFLICT DO NOTHING` ‚Äî exact match to `@crm2/access`. The roles parity test was updated in lockstep (`FIELD_AGENT_SEED = ['case.view','location.capture','task.execute']`, roles.api.test.ts:153). No drift.
- **(b) ‚úÖ THE KEY CONTROL ‚Äî every device action binds ownership via `taskForAssignee(taskId, actorId)` = `WHERE id=$1 AND assigned_to=$2::uuid` ‚Üí null ‚Üí 404.** `repository.ts:18-19` is a pure equality on `assigned_to = $2::uuid` bound to `actor.userId` ‚Äî NOT a hierarchy/scope/subtree predicate, so a TL/manager can NEVER drive a subordinate's task through this path (it's the actor's OWN uuid, full stop). Service routes ALL FOUR actions through `ownedCaseId()` (service.ts:20-24) which calls `taskForAssignee` first and throws `404 TASK_NOT_FOUND` on null BEFORE any write: start:28, complete:32, revoke:37, setPriority:42 ‚Äî uniform, no action bypasses it. **Defense-in-depth:** the returned caseId is then re-pinned in every writer's `WHERE id=$1 AND case_id=$2` so the ownership-derived caseId gates the mutation too. **Non-assignee FIELD_AGENT (HAS task.execute) ‚Üí 404, test-proven** (verification-tasks.api.test.ts:143: `other` FA ‚Üí 404; :147 rightful assignee ‚Üí 200). `actorId` comes from `actor(req)` (verified JWT `req.auth.userId`, controller.ts:12-15), never the body.
- **(c) ‚úÖ `:id` uuid-validated BEFORE the SQL.** `parseId` (controller.ts:7-11) runs `UUID_RE.test(v)` else `400 BAD_REQUEST` ‚Äî a non-uuid never reaches the uuid-column `WHERE id=$1` (no `22P02`‚Üí500, no injection). Applied on all four handlers.
- **(d) ‚úÖ All SQL parameterized ‚Äî zero `${}` of request data.** `taskForAssignee` + all four writers (`startTaskByDevice`/`completeTaskByDevice`/`revokeTaskByDevice`/`setTaskPriorityByDevice`, repository.ts:32-139) bind every value (`$1`=taskId, `$2`=caseId, `$3`=actorId, `$4`=priority/none). `priority` is `z.enum(PRIORITIES)` (service.ts:17) ‚Äî validated to the enum before binding, AND bound as `$4` regardless. `TASK_VIEW_BY_ID` re-reads by `$1`=taskId only (no cross-bind). No dynamic SQL, no ORDER BY surface.
- **(e) ‚úÖ Revoke reason ‚Äî stored in the AUDIT row, not a column; no injection.** `revokeTaskByDevice` SET clause touches ONLY `status/version/updated_by/updated_at` ‚Äî `reason` is NOT a column write; it rides `appendAudit({‚Ä¶ after:{status:'REVOKED', reason}}, q)` (repository.ts:107-110) as a bound jsonb value (`reason = z.string().trim().min(1).max(2000)`, RevokeSchema service.ts:16). Empty reason ‚Üí 400 (test:124). No interpolation; injection-proof.
- **(f) ‚úÖ `completed_by`/`updated_by` from the verified actor, NOT the body ‚Äî no mass-assignment.** All writers set `updated_by=$3`/`completed_by=$3` to `actorId` (the JWT userId), never a body field. Controllers pass NO body to start/complete (`svc.start(parseId(req), actor(req))`); revoke/priority pass `req.body` but the service `.parse`es it through a CLOSED zod schema accepting ONLY `{reason}` / `{priority}` ‚Äî `assigned_to`/`completed_by`/`status`/`version`/`case_id` are unreachable from input. No `assigned_to` is ever settable by the device (re-assignment stays an office/assign-perm operation).
- **(g) ‚úÖ No illegal/dangerous transition from the device.** Every writer pins the legal source state in the WHERE: start `status='ASSIGNED'`, complete/revoke `status IN ('ASSIGNED','IN_PROGRESS')`, priority `status IN ('PENDING','ASSIGNED','IN_PROGRESS')`. A 0-row update re-reads the current row and either returns it (idempotent: already in the target state ‚Üí caller's 200) or throws `409 INVALID_TRANSITION`. **COMPLETED‚ÜíREVOKED is forbidden** (a COMPLETED task is not in the revoke source set ‚Üí 0 rows ‚Üí status‚âÝREVOKED ‚Üí 409; comment + test:115 title confirm). The device cannot complete/revoke someone else's task (404 via ownership, see (b)) nor un-terminal a COMPLETED task. No `verification_outcome` is written (single-layer field, ADR-0032 D1 ‚Äî `verificationOutcome` asserted null post-start/complete, test:100,108).

DISPOSITION: **PASS.** No BLOCK, no FLAG. My design-review finding-2 MUST-FIX is satisfied IN CODE and IN TEST: **`task.execute` is FIELD_AGENT-only (code+0053 seed parity, no other role)**, and **every device action enforces an explicit `assigned_to = actor` binding (equality on the actor's own uuid, not a hierarchy/scope predicate) ‚Üí non-assignee ‚Üí 404, IDOR-safe (test:143).** uuid-shape-guarded `:id`; fully parameterized; reason in audit-jsonb not a column; actor-sourced `completed_by`/`updated_by` (no mass-assignment via closed schemas); transition guards forbid COMPLETED‚ÜíREVOKED and cross-owner drive. The mobile contract (ADR-0012) is untouched (these are new `/api/v2` routes mapping the locked paths; `/sync/download` + device row shape unchanged). NOTE (RUN-gated, not blocking): the api suite is `describe.skipIf(!RUN)` ‚Äî couldn't execute in sandbox (no DATABASE_URL); read line-by-line, all four asserts (idempotency, COMPLETED-revoke 409, priority-terminal 409, ownership 404 + RBAC 403) are correct. Gate-runner: run `verification-tasks.api` green on a live test DB before ship.

- **2026-06-15 ¬∑ slice-2c-2a ‚Äî OFFICE per-task RESULT recording (`POST /cases/:id/tasks/:taskId/result`) + device revoke-reason‚Üí`remark` column (ADR-0032 D3)** ‚Äî **VERDICT: PASS.**
  - **(a) ‚úÖ RBAC ‚Äî gated `field_review.complete`, same as the sibling complete leg.** routes.ts:22 mounts `authorize(PERMISSIONS.FIELD_REVIEW_COMPLETE)` ‚Äî byte-identical to the adjacent `POST ‚Ä¶/complete` (routes.ts:21). Per project_rbac_hierarchy_model, `field_review.complete` is BACKEND_USER/SUPER_ADMIN (NOT TEAM_LEAD/FIELD_AGENT/KYC_VERIFIER). Default-deny intact, no perm weakened, no write path opened. **KYC_VERIFIER (read-only, lacks the perm) ‚Üí 403, test-proven** (cases.api.test.ts: verifier POST ‚Üí 403); BACKEND_USER (holds perm + portfolio) ‚Üí 200.
  - **(b) ‚úÖ IDOR/scope ‚Äî same control as completeTask; out-of-scope ‚Üí 404.** Service (service.ts:330) gates on `repo.taskAssignmentState(caseId, taskId, await resolveScope(actor))` ‚Üí null ‚Üí `404 TASK_NOT_FOUND` BEFORE any write ‚Äî identical to completeTask:305/unassignTask:292. `taskAssignmentState` applies the server-side scope predicate (`taskScopePredicate`, repository.ts:568) so a BACKEND_USER outside the case portfolio sees 404, not the row. The repo UPDATE then re-pins `WHERE id=$1 AND case_id=$2` (caseId is the scope-validated value, bound not trusted). No way to result a non-scoped task. Test grants portfolio before the 200; a not-yet-COMPLETED task ‚Üí 409 (status guard, not scope) is also asserted.
  - **(c) ‚úÖ `:id`/`:taskId` uuid-validated BEFORE SQL.** Both pass through `parseUuidParam` (controller.ts:9-13, `UUID_RE.test` else 400 BAD_REQUEST) in the handler (controller.ts:177-184) ‚Äî a non-uuid never reaches the uuid `WHERE id=$1`/`case_id=$2` (no 22P02‚Üí500). `actor` from verified JWT `req.auth` (controller.ts:16-20), fail-closed.
  - **(d) ‚úÖ All SQL parameterized ‚Äî zero `${}` of request data.** `recordTaskResult` UPDATE binds `$1`=taskId, `$2`=caseId, `$3`=result, `$4`=remark, `$5`=actorId, `$6`=expectedVersion; the re-SELECT triage binds `$1`=taskId only. `result` is `z.enum(KYC_RESULTS)` (POSITIVE/NEGATIVE/REFER/FRAUD), `remark` `z.string().trim().max(2000).optional()` ‚Äî both validated to type, both bound. No dynamic SQL, no ORDER BY surface.
  - **(e) ‚úÖ No mass-assignment ‚Äî closed schema, actor-sourced columns.** `RecordTaskResultSchema` (sdk/cases.ts:374) = CLOSED `z.object({result, remark?})` ‚Äî `status`/`completed_by`/`completed_at`/`version`/`case_id`/`assigned_to` are UNREACHABLE from the body (z.object strips unknown keys). `completed_by`/`updated_by` are set to `$5=actor.userId` (the JWT userId), NEVER a body field. `version` is read via `requireVersion(input)` from the raw body envelope (the OCC token), not the parsed result schema, and is only ever used in the `WHERE version=$6` compare + server-side `version+1` ‚Äî never written from input. Can a non-COMPLETED or out-of-scope task be resulted? NO: out-of-scope ‚Üí 404 (b); non-COMPLETED ‚Üí 409 at BOTH the service guard (status‚âÝCOMPLETED, service.ts:332) AND the repo UPDATE predicate (`AND status='COMPLETED'`, defense-in-depth against TOCTOU).
  - **(f) ‚öÝÔ∏è BEHAVIOR-CHANGE NOTE (non-gating) ‚Äî device revoke `reason` is NOW a column write, superseding my 2c-1 entry (e) above.** `revokeTaskByDevice` (repository.ts:919) now `SET remark=$4` (=`reason`) IN ADDITION to the existing `appendAudit({after:{status,reason}})`. `reason` is still validated (`z.string().trim().min(1).max(MAX_REASON)`, verification-tasks/service.ts:16,37) and BOUND as `$4` ‚Äî no injection (the column write is parameterized exactly like the audit jsonb was). No collision: a REVOKED task never carries an office result (recordTaskResult only touches COMPLETED rows), so `remark` is free. The FE now surfaces it inline (CaseDetailPage.tsx:318). PII: `reason`/`remark` are free-text operational notes (revoke justification, result remark) authored by internal staff behind `task.execute`/`field_review.complete` ‚Äî internal-staff content, not customer PII; no new sensitive column in the SELECT projection (`TASK_VIEW_BY_ID` unchanged). The 2c-1 ledger statement "reason in audit-jsonb not a column" is now superseded for the column-write ‚Äî recorded here so the ledger stays truthful.
  - DISPOSITION: **PASS.** No BLOCK, no FLAG. Gate parity with completeTask (`field_review.complete` ‚Üí BACKEND_USER/SA; KYC_VERIFIER 403 tested), scope‚Üí404 IDOR-safe, dual uuid-shape guard, fully parameterized, closed schema + actor-sourced `completed_by` (no mass-assignment), double status-guard (service 409 + repo predicate) blocks resulting a non-COMPLETED/out-of-scope task. ONE behavior-change note (revoke reason now also a column ‚Äî injection-safe, no collision) recorded to keep the prior entry honest. Mobile contract (ADR-0012) untouched (new `/result` is web-office only; device paths unchanged bar the additive `remark` column write the device already drives via its validated `reason`). RUN-gated: the new recordResult test (happy + 409-not-completed + 403-verifier) is in the `skipIf(!RUN)` suite ‚Äî run `cases.api` green on a live test DB before ship (brief reports 53/53 + live HTTP/browser E2E passed).

- **2026-06-15 ¬∑ slice-2c-2b device form-submit (`POST /verification-tasks/:id/verification/:formType` + `caseRepository.submitVerificationForm`) ‚Äî VERDICT: PASS.** Gated `authorize(TASK_EXECUTE)` (routes.ts:13, same gate as the 4 lifecycle routes); ownership bound server-side via `ownedCaseId`‚Üí`taskForAssignee` (`assigned_to=$2::uuid` ‚Üí out-of-ownership ‚â° 404 TASK_NOT_FOUND, IDOR-safe, repository.ts:834-840). **jsonb-path injection SAFE:** `formType` is whitelisted against the 9 pinned `FORM_TYPE_SLUGS` (‚Üí 400 UNKNOWN_FORM_TYPE) BEFORE use, and even then is passed as a BOUND param `ARRAY[$4]` to `jsonb_set` (not interpolated) ‚Äî double-safe. Body is `z.record(string,unknown)` stored verbatim as jsonb (evidence; NO SQL built from its contents) ‚Äî value-bound `$5::jsonb`, no injection surface. **DoS bound:** `MAX_FORM_BYTES=256KB` service guard on the stringified body; note `express.json()` (http/app.ts:70) has NO explicit `limit` ‚Üí default 100KB cap fires first (413) ‚Äî the 256KB service guard is a redundant secondary bound, fine. No new PII column exposed (the device's `verificationOutcome` lives in the jsonb blob, NOT the official `verification_outcome` col ‚Äî confirmed). No secrets/`console.*`/`SELECT *` in diff.

## 2026-06-16 ‚Äî ADR-0033 slice 3: task lineage (revisit + reassign-after-revoke) + verdict-history ‚Äî VERDICT: PASS

Adversarial review of the uncommitted diff: mig `0054_task_lineage.sql`, `@crm2/access` perms, `cases/{routes,controller,service,repository}.ts`, `sdk/{cases,client}.ts`, `CaseDetailPage.tsx`, `cases.api.test.ts`. Three new case endpoints ‚Äî `POST /:id/tasks/:taskId/revisit`, `‚Ä¶/reassign` (new `task.rework`), `GET /:id/verdict-history` (`case.view`).

- **(a) ‚úÖ RBAC default-deny + code‚ÜîDB parity EXACT.** `task.rework` granted to ONLY `BACKEND_USER`+`MANAGER` in BOTH the migration (0054:40-43 `INSERT ‚Ä¶ VALUES ('BACKEND_USER','task.rework'),('MANAGER','task.rework') ON CONFLICT DO NOTHING`) AND `ROLE_PERMISSIONS` (`permissions.ts:81` MANAGER, `:103` BACKEND_USER); SUPER_ADMIN via `Object.values` grants_all. **KYC_VERIFIER/FIELD_AGENT/TEAM_LEADER do NOT receive it** ‚Äî grepped: `TASK_REWORK`/`'task.rework'` appears in no other role block. The **roles-parity gate enforces the match**: `roles.parity.test.ts:62-79` asserts DB-resolved `role_permissions` ‚â° `ROLE_PERMISSIONS[role]` byte-identical for all 6 roles ‚Üí drift = red. **No leftover `task.revoke` anywhere** (grep clean; the owner-correction comment 0054:17-19 + permissions.ts:34-39 documents revoke stays the device's `task.execute`). Routes gate `revisit`/`reassign` with `authorize(PERMISSIONS.TASK_REWORK)`, `verdict-history` with `authorize(PERMISSIONS.CASE_VIEW)` (routes.ts:28-33). Tests prove the negatives: KYC_VERIFIER ‚Üí **403** on both revisit (cases.api.test.ts:1085) and reassign (:1143).
- **(b) ‚úÖ Scope/IDOR ‚Äî perm gate BEFORE state leak; out-of-scope ‚â° 404, not 403.** `authorize` middleware runs ahead of the controller, so the perm check precedes any DB touch (a permitted-but-out-of-scope actor is the only one who reaches scope resolution). revisit+reassign both call `repo.taskAssignmentState(caseId, taskId, await resolveScope(actor))` ‚Üí null ‚Üí `404 TASK_NOT_FOUND` BEFORE any write (service.ts:357,381); `taskAssignmentState` (repository.ts:559-583) applies the parameterized `taskScopePredicate` (bind-pushed params), so an out-of-portfolio BACKEND_USER/MANAGER sees 404 not the row. verdict-history calls `repo.caseVisible(caseId, scope)` ‚Üí false ‚Üí `404 CASE_NOT_FOUND` (service.ts:347; caseVisible repository.ts:1194-1202 = parameterized `caseScopePredicate`). **Out-of-scope MANAGER ‚Üí 404 test-proven** on revisit (:1087), reassign (:1145), AND verdict-history (:1201-1203). The repo writers re-pin `WHERE p.id=$2 AND p.case_id=$1` on the scope-validated caseId (defense-in-depth) ‚Äî a non-assignee/out-of-portfolio actor can neither act nor read.
- **(c) ‚úÖ Injection ‚Äî all new SQL parameterized; nothing user-controlled interpolated.** The INSERT‚Ä¶SELECT clones (repository.ts:885-893 revisit, :952-962 reassign) bind every value (`$1`=caseId, `$2`=parentTaskId, `$3`=seq/visitType, `$4`=actorId/distanceBand, `$5`=billCount, `$6`=assignedTo, `$7`=actorId, `$8`=seq) ‚Äî zero `${}` of request data. `task_origin` is a server-set **literal** `'REVISIT'` (revisit) or **cloned from the parent row** `p.task_origin` (reassign) ‚Äî never user input. `verdictHistory` (repository.ts:835-848) interpolates NOTHING user-controlled ‚Äî `entity_type='case'`/`entity_id=$1` (bound), the `after_data->>'verificationOutcome'` jsonb extracts are static path literals, ORDER BY is a fixed `created_at DESC, id DESC`. The `hasActiveRevisitOf`/seq-count/task_assignment_history INSERTs are all bound. `:id`/`:taskId` pass `parseUuidParam` (UUID_RE ‚Üí 400) before the uuid `WHERE` ‚Äî no 22P02‚Üí500. `visitType`=`z.enum(VISIT_TYPES)`, `distanceBand`=`z.enum(DISTANCE_BANDS)`, `result`-path enums validated pre-bind.
- **(d) ‚úÖ Assignee eligibility re-check is fail-closed (the privesc-relevant path).** reassign re-runs `taskRepository.eligibleTaskIdsForAssignee([taskId], v.assignedTo, v.visitType, await getScopedUserIds(actor))` (service.ts:382) ‚Äî the SAME path as a normal assign (service.ts:271). Definition (tasks/repository.ts:215-247) returns only IDs where the assignee passes **pool-role ‚à© actor-hierarchy (`u.id = ANY($n::uuid[])`) ‚à© FIELD territory (`user_scope_assignments`)**; an out-of-scope or ineligible assignee yields `[]` ‚Üí `400 INVALID_ASSIGNEE`. Second net: the repo INSERT catches `FK_VIOLATION ‚Üí INVALID_ASSIGNEE` (repository.ts). A caller CANNOT assign to an out-of-scope/ineligible user ‚Äî **test-proven**: BACKEND_USER (not in OFFICE pool) ‚Üí **400 INVALID_ASSIGNEE** (cases.api.test.ts:1140). Status guards: revisit requires parent COMPLETED else 409, reassign requires parent REVOKED else 409 (service.ts:359,383; the revoked row is never re-activated ‚Äî :1118 asserts it stays REVOKED). Duplicate-revisit blocked (`hasActiveRevisitOf` ‚Üí 409 ACTIVE_REVISIT_EXISTS, anti-double-bill).
- **(e) ‚úÖ audit_log append-only/immutable ‚Äî preserved.** The ONLY `INSERT INTO audit_log` in the codebase is `platform/audit.ts:26` (`appendAudit`); grep finds NO `UPDATE`/`DELETE` on `audit_log` anywhere. Both new audit rows (revisit, reassign) use `appendAudit({‚Ä¶}, q)` **in-tx**, with `reason`/`parentTaskId`/`assignedTo` as bound jsonb `after` values (not SQL text). No new write path to the audit table. verdict-history READS the audit log (after_data jsonb), writes nothing.
- **(f) ‚úÖ No mass-assignment / no PII regression.** `ReworkTaskSchema`=closed `{reason?}`; `ReassignTaskSchema`=closed `{assignedTo,visitType,distanceBand?,billCount,reason?}` (z.object strips unknowns) ‚Äî `status`/`task_origin`/`parent_task_id`/`created_by`/`case_id` are UNREACHABLE from the body; `created_by`/`updated_by`/`assigned_by`/`actorId` set from `actor(req)` (verified JWT), never a body field. `task_origin` is server-forced. New SELECT cols (`task_origin`, `parent_task_id` on TASK_VIEW_COLS:129; verdict-history `actor_name` via LEFT JOIN users) are lineage/staff-name fields behind existing gates ‚Äî not new customer PII. No secrets/`console.*`/`SELECT *` in diff. FE gates rework UI behind `has('task.rework')` (CaseDetailPage.tsx:33,63) ‚Äî cosmetic; server is the real gate.

DISPOSITION: **PASS.** No BLOCK, no FLAG. `task.rework` is default-deny, seeded to exactly BACKEND_USER+MANAGER in BOTH mig 0054 and `@crm2/access` (parity-test-enforced); no `task.revoke` residue. All three endpoints scope-resolve to **404** out-of-scope with the perm gate firing FIRST (KYC_VERIFIER 403 / outsider 404 test-proven for all three). All new SQL fully parameterized; `task_origin` is a server literal/parent-clone, never user input; verdict-history interpolates nothing user-controlled. The reassign assignee re-check is fail-closed (`[]`‚Üí400 INVALID_ASSIGNEE + FK_VIOLATION net, test-proven). audit_log remains append-only via the single `appendAudit` writer. **RUN-gated note (not blocking):** the new cases.api negatives live in the `skipIf(!RUN)` suite ‚Äî read line-by-line, asserts correct; run `cases.api` + `roles.parity` green on a live test DB before ship. **OPEN (carried, non-blocking):** the cases/task LIST + Pipeline still lack row-level scope (2026-06-06 gap) ‚Äî unrelated to these per-record endpoints, which each carry their own scope guard.

## 2026-06-16 ‚Äî ADR-0034 slice 2c-2: device FIELD-PHOTO upload (`POST /verification-tasks/:id/attachments`) ‚Äî VERDICT: FLAG (PASS w/ one readiness DoS note; no BLOCK)

Adversarial review of the uncommitted diff: new `platform/photo.ts`, mig `0055_field_photo_attachments.sql`, `verification-tasks/{routes,controller,service}.ts`, `cases/repository.ts` (`insertFieldAttachment`/`fieldAttachmentsByOperation`), `sdk/sync.ts`, `verification-tasks.api.test.ts`. Multipart upload (multer memoryStorage + sharp).

- **(a) ‚úÖ RBAC + ownership/IDOR ‚Äî non-assignee ‚Üí 404, test-proven; perm gate fires before multer.** Route mounts `authorize(PERMISSIONS.TASK_EXECUTE)` BEFORE `parseFieldPhotos` (routes.ts:38-43) ‚Äî RBAC runs before the multipart body is even buffered. `task.execute` = FIELD_AGENT-only (established 2c-1 entry; code+0053 parity). Service binds ownership via the SAME `ownedCaseId(taskId,actor)`‚Üí`taskForAssignee` (`WHERE id=$1 AND assigned_to=$2::uuid` ‚Üí null ‚Üí 404 TASK_NOT_FOUND) as the 4 lifecycle legs (service.ts:147) ‚Äî equality on the actor's OWN uuid, NOT a hierarchy/scope predicate, so no TL/MGR can drive a subordinate's task, and a FIELD_AGENT who is not the assignee cannot write a photo to a task they don't own. **Non-assignee FIELD_AGENT (HAS task.execute) ‚Üí 404 test-proven** (verification-tasks.api.test.ts:317). The derived `caseId` is re-pinned into the INSERT (`case_id=$1`) ‚Äî defense-in-depth. `:id` uuid-shape-guarded by `parseId` (controller.ts:7-11, UUID_RE ‚Üí 400) before the uuid `WHERE`. `actor` from verified JWT `req.auth` (controller.ts:12-15), never the body.
- **(b) ‚úÖ File-upload safety ‚Äî magic-byte image-only, sharp re-encode, server-side key.** multer `memoryStorage` (no disk write, no temp-file traversal); `detectAttachment` (platform/file.ts:34) sniffs MAGIC BYTES (not Content-Type) and the service rejects anything not `image/*` ‚Üí `UNSUPPORTED_FILE_TYPE` (service.ts) ‚Äî **PDF rejected for THIS path test-proven** (`%PDF` bytes ‚Üí failed[], nothing stored, test:340). `processFieldPhoto` (photo.ts:18-34) runs `sharp(bytes).rotate().toBuffer()` ‚Äî re-encodes, defeating most image polyglots/trailing-payload tricks and dropping all metadata. Per-file failure is collected in `failed[]` (no request abort); only an unconfigured store (`STORAGE_NOT_CONFIGURED`/503) fails the whole request. `f.size>MAX_ATTACHMENT_BYTES` re-checked in-loop (belt over multer's `fileSize`).
- **(c) ‚úÖ Injection ‚Äî all new SQL parameterized; key derived from server uuids only.** `insertFieldAttachment` (repository.ts:1257-1300) binds all 16 values ($1‚Äì$16); `geo_location` is `JSON.parse`'d to an object then `JSON.stringify`'d and bound `$11::jsonb` (no SQL path from its contents). `operation_id` stored as a bound `${base}:${i}` ($15). `fieldAttachmentsByOperation` uses `split_part(operation_id, ':', 1) = $1` ‚Äî bound, not interpolated. **Storage key = `field-photos/${caseId}/${taskId}/${randomUUID()}.${detected.ext}` ‚Äî every segment is a server-resolved uuid or a server whitelist `ext` (pdf/png/jpg/webp from file.ts), NOT user input.** `originalName` is sliced to 255 and stored ONLY as a label (`original_name`), never used in the key ‚Äî no path traversal. No `${}` of request data in any SQL; no ORDER BY surface (fixed `created_at ASC, operation_id ASC`).
- **(d) ‚úÖ PII/DPDP ‚Äî stored bytes cannot leak GPS via EXIF; client-hash mismatch logged with no payload.** sharp re-encode WITHOUT `.withMetadata()` strips all metadata incl. embedded GPS from the STORED artifact (photo.ts:20-23) ‚Äî the stored `stripped`/`thumbnail` carry no EXIF GPS. Geo is kept ONLY in the explicit `geo_location` jsonb (intentional capture, ADR-0034). The server hash (`sha256` col) is computed over the STRIPPED stored bytes (evidence); `client_sha256` is validated `^[0-9a-f]{64}$` or null; a mismatch logs `{ taskId, file: originalName }` only ‚Äî NO hash value, no image bytes (service.ts). Response `url`/`thumbnailUrl` return the raw object-storage KEY (not a presigned URL) ‚Äî opaque, not fetchable without S3 creds/presigning; this is the locked v1 device contract (the office read-path likewise gates byte access separately via `attachmentForAccess`‚Üísigned serve). No new customer-PII column in any SELECT projection beyond the device's own geo it just captured.
- **(e) ‚úÖ Idempotency ‚Äî required, no injection via the header.** `operationBase = (idemKey ?? operationId).trim()`; empty ‚Üí `400 IDEMPOTENCY_KEY_REQUIRED` (test:331). The key flows ONLY into a bound `$15` (`${base}:${i}`) and a bound `$1` in the replay SELECT ‚Äî never into SQL text. Replay (same key) returns the cached rows success=true, NO re-store (partial-UNIQUE `uq_case_attachments_operation` + the `23505` race-catch ‚Üí cached set) ‚Äî 200-not-409, test-proven (replay ‚Üí 1 row, count stays 1, test:308). Closed field set in the controller (`str()` coerces each to string|undefined) ‚Äî no mass-assignment; `uploaded_by=$16` is the JWT `actor.userId`, never a body field.
- **(f) ‚öÝÔ∏è FLAG (readiness DoS, NOT a security BLOCK) ‚Äî unbounded in-memory buffering per request.** multer `memoryStorage` with `files:20` √ó `fileSize:25MiB` = **up to ~500 MiB buffered in RAM per request** (routes.ts:17-21), PLUS sharp decode + `stripped`/`thumbnail` buffers held per file in the loop. `express.json()` (app.ts:70) is JSON-only and does NOT cap multipart, so multer's limits are the only bound. An authenticated FIELD_AGENT (the only role that passes the gate) can drive memory pressure / OOM by repeatedly posting max-size batches; no per-request total-byte cap, no concurrency throttle, no streaming-to-store. Real surface but auth-gated to a trusted role ‚Üí **readiness/hardening item, not a release-blocking vuln.** FIX (readiness): add a total-bytes guard (e.g. `files √ó fileSize` budget or a request-level cap well below 500 MiB), and/or process files sequentially releasing buffers (already looped, but all 20 are buffered up-front by multer before the loop runs); consider lowering `MAX_FIELD_FILES` for the device's real batch size.

DISPOSITION: **FLAG (effectively PASS).** No BLOCK. Ownership IDOR is closed (non-assignee‚Üí404 test-proven, equality-on-own-uuid), upload is image-only by magic-byte + sharp re-encode (PDF rejected test-proven), all SQL parameterized with a server-uuid-only storage key (no traversal), EXIF/GPS stripped from stored bytes (geo only in the intentional `geo_location` jsonb), idempotency-key required and injection-free, no mass-assignment (`uploaded_by`=JWT actor). The ONE flag is a **memory-DoS readiness gap** ‚Äî up to ~500 MiB buffered per request via multer memoryStorage (20√ó25MiB), auth-gated to FIELD_AGENT; harden before high-volume device rollout, not a ship-blocker. **RUN-gated note (not blocking):** the new upload tests are in the `skipIf(!RUN)` suite ‚Äî read line-by-line, asserts correct (200+evidence-hash+idempotent-replay; non-assignee 404; missing-key 400; PDF‚Üífailed[]); run `verification-tasks.api` green on a live test DB before ship. **OPEN (carried):** raw `storage_key` returned as `url` matches the locked device contract (opaque key, not byte-access) ‚Äî confirm the device resolves bytes via a separate signed-serve path (no public-bucket assumption).

## 2026-06-16 ‚Äî ADR-0033 correction slice: backend/office task REVOKE (`POST /cases/:id/tasks/:taskId/revoke`) + new `task.revoke` perm ‚Äî VERDICT: PASS

Adversarial review of the uncommitted diff: new mig `0056_task_revoke_perm.sql`, `@crm2/access` `permissions.ts` (`TASK_REVOKE`), `cases/{routes,controller,service,repository}.ts` (`revokeTaskByDevice`‚Üíshared `revokeTaskInPlace`), `sdk/{cases,client}.ts` (`RevokeTaskSchema`), `cases.api.test.ts`. NOTE: the photo-upload (mig 0055, ADR-0034 2c-2) in this prompt's FOCUS is NOT in the working tree ‚Äî it was reviewed+committed earlier (the FLAG entry above stands); this diff is the REVOKE feature (B) only.

- **(a) ‚úÖ RBAC default-deny + code‚ÜîDB parity EXACT.** `task.revoke` granted to ONLY `BACKEND_USER` (permissions.ts:108) + `MANAGER` (permissions.ts:85) in BOTH `ROLE_PERMISSIONS` AND mig 0056 (`VALUES ('BACKEND_USER','task.revoke'),('MANAGER','task.revoke') ON CONFLICT DO NOTHING`); SUPER_ADMIN via `grants_all`. **KYC_VERIFIER/FIELD_AGENT/TEAM_LEADER do NOT receive it** ‚Äî grepped: `TASK_REVOKE`/`'task.revoke'` appears in no other role block. The **roles-parity gate enforces it** (`access/__tests__/roles.parity.test.ts:62-79`: DB `role_permissions` ‚â° `ROLE_PERMISSIONS[role]` byte-identical, all 6 roles). Route gates with `authorize(PERMISSIONS.TASK_REVOKE)` (routes.ts:32). KYC_VERIFIER ‚Üí **403 test-proven** (cases.api.test.ts:1241). `task.execute` stays FIELD_AGENT-only (device photo/lifecycle path untouched). Stale prose: mig 0054:19 comment "there is NO task.revoke perm" is now outdated but INERT (0054 only INSERTs task.rework; 0056 is forward-only/additive) ‚Äî cosmetic, not a security issue.
- **(b) ‚úÖ IDOR/scope ‚Äî perm gate BEFORE state leak; out-of-scope ‚â° 404, not 403.** `authorize` runs ahead of the controller. Service (service.ts:359) gates on `repo.taskAssignmentState(caseId, taskId, await resolveScope(actor))` ‚Üí null ‚Üí `404 TASK_NOT_FOUND` BEFORE any write ‚Äî identical control to result/revisit/reassign. `taskAssignmentState` (repository.ts:568-589) applies the parameterized `taskScopePredicate` (bind-pushed params) so an out-of-portfolio BACKEND_USER/MANAGER sees 404 not the row. **Out-of-scope MANAGER (HOLDS task.revoke) ‚Üí 404 test-proven** (cases.api.test.ts:1245). The device revoke leg is SEPARATE and ownership-bound (verification-tasks/service.ts:112 `ownedCaseId`‚Üí`taskForAssignee` `assigned_to=actor`‚Üí404) ‚Äî an office user can't drive a device-ownership path and a non-assignee FIELD_AGENT can't revoke another's task. The shared repo writer re-pins `WHERE id=$1 AND case_id=$2` on the scope-validated caseId (defense-in-depth).
- **(c) ‚úÖ Injection ‚Äî all SQL parameterized; nothing user-controlled interpolated.** `revokeTaskInPlace` UPDATE (repository.ts:1124-1130) binds `$1`=taskId, `$2`=caseId, `$3`=actorId, `$4`=reason ‚Äî zero `${}` of request data; the re-SELECT (`TASK_VIEW_BY_ID`) binds `$1`=taskId only; `appendAudit` writes `reason` as a BOUND jsonb `after` value (not SQL text). `reason` = `z.string().trim().min(1).max(2000)` (RevokeTaskSchema, sdk/cases.ts:386) ‚Äî validated + bound. `:id`/`:taskId` pass `parseUuidParam` (UUID_RE ‚Üí 400, controller.ts:9-13) before the uuid `WHERE` (no 22P02‚Üí500). No ORDER BY surface; no dynamic SQL.
- **(d) ‚úÖ Transition guard fail-closed ‚Äî COMPLETED‚ÜíREVOKED forbidden, idempotent re-revoke.** UPDATE predicate `status IN ('ASSIGNED','IN_PROGRESS')`; 0 rows ‚Üí re-read current row: missing ‚Üí 404, `status!='REVOKED'` ‚Üí `409 INVALID_TRANSITION` (COMPLETED/PENDING blocked), already-REVOKED ‚Üí 200 idempotent (repository.ts:1132-1136). **COMPLETED ‚Üí 409 INVALID_TRANSITION test-proven** (cases.api.test.ts via `settle`‚Üírevoke‚Üí409); idempotent re-revoke ‚Üí 200 test-proven; reason-missing ‚Üí 400, all in one test. No commission, case rolled up via `recomputeCaseStatus`.
- **(e) ‚úÖ No mass-assignment / no PII regression.** `RevokeTaskSchema` = closed `z.object({reason})` (z.object strips unknowns) ‚Äî `status`/`assigned_to`/`version`/`case_id`/`updated_by` UNREACHABLE from the body; `updated_by=$3` is `actor.userId` (verified JWT), never a body field; `status='REVOKED'` is a server literal. `reason`/`remark` are internal-staff operational free-text behind `task.revoke` ‚Äî not customer PII; no new column in the `TASK_VIEW_BY_ID` projection. No secrets/`console.*`/`SELECT *` in diff. FE gates revoke UI behind the perm (cosmetic; server is the real gate).

DISPOSITION: **PASS.** No BLOCK, no FLAG. `task.revoke` is default-deny, seeded to exactly BACKEND_USER+MANAGER in BOTH mig 0056 and `@crm2/access` (parity-test-enforced); excluded from KYC_VERIFIER/FIELD_AGENT/TEAM_LEADER. Office revoke scope-resolves to **404** out-of-scope with the perm gate firing FIRST (KYC_VERIFIER 403 / outsider MANAGER 404 test-proven); the device revoke stays ownership-bound on `task.execute` (unchanged). All SQL fully parameterized (reason bound, uuid-shape-guarded params, audit reason in bound jsonb). Transition guard forbids COMPLETED‚ÜíREVOKED (409 test-proven), idempotent re-revoke. Closed schema + actor-sourced `updated_by` (no mass-assignment). The `revokeTaskByDevice`‚Üí`revokeTaskInPlace` rename keeps BOTH callers (device ownership-bound + office scope-bound) on the same parameterized transition. **RUN-gated note (not blocking):** the new revoke test is in `describe.skipIf(!RUN)` ‚Äî read line-by-line, asserts correct (400 reason / 403 verifier / 404 out-of-scope MANAGER / 200 REVOKED+remark / idempotent 200 / COMPLETED 409); run `cases.api` + `roles.parity` green on a live test DB before ship. **OPEN (carried, non-blocking):** cases/task LIST + Pipeline still lack row-level scope (2026-06-06 gap) ‚Äî unrelated to this per-record endpoint which carries its own scope guard.

- **2026-06-16 ¬∑ slice-2c-2 tail ‚Äî sync delta arrays + execution fields (`sync/repository.ts` NEW `revokedAssignmentIdsForUser` + `SYNC_SELECT` exposes `ct.started_at`/`ct.completed_at`; `sync/service.ts download()` emits `revokedAssignmentIds` + per-task `inProgressAt`/`completedAt`) ‚Äî VERDICT: PASS. No BLOCK, no FLAG.**
  - (a) ‚úÖ **IDOR / scope-leak on `revokedAssignmentIds` ‚Äî leak-proof BY CONSTRUCTION; the only ids returned are tasks the device demonstrably held.** The query (repository.ts:114-121) is `SELECT DISTINCT h.task_id FROM task_assignment_history h JOIN case_tasks ct ON ct.id=h.task_id WHERE h.previous_assigned_to=$1 AND h.created_at>$2 AND ct.assigned_to IS DISTINCT FROM $1` with `$1 = actor.userId` (server-derived). A `task_assignment_history` row carries `previous_assigned_to = X` ONLY when X was the assignee being moved OFF the task ‚Äî **traced to the writer:** the reassign/unassign UPDATEs source `previous_assigned_to` from `p.prev = case_tasks.assigned_to` captured server-side in the same statement (cases/repository.ts:611-613,640; 673; 990), NEVER from client input. So every id where `previous_assigned_to = me` is irrefutable proof the device once held that assignment ‚Üí returning it reveals only ids the device already legitimately received via the `assigned_to = me` `cases` filter. It can NOT surface a task the user was never assigned to. The `ct.assigned_to IS DISTINCT FROM $1` term only NARROWS (excludes reassigned-then-back-to-me, which still flows in `cases`), never widens. No cross-user task id can appear. CONFIRMED leak-proof.
  - (b) ‚úÖ **userId is server-derived, NOT spoofable.** `actor.userId` flows from `req.auth.userId` (controller.ts:6-10 `actor()`; fail-closed `if(!req.auth) throw unauthenticated()`), set by the JWT auth middleware ahead of the `authorize(CASE_VIEW)` gate (routes.ts:12) ‚Äî never read from query/body. `download()` passes `actor.userId` to BOTH `downloadForUser` and `revokedAssignmentIdsForUser` (service.ts:85,90). A malicious actor cannot pass a victim's userId to harvest the victim's revoked-task ids; the only request inputs (`lastSyncTimestamp`/`limit`/`offset`) are zod-parsed (`SyncDownloadQuerySchema`) + clamped (limit‚â§200) + Date-validated (400 INVALID_TIMESTAMP on NaN). Default-deny intact: CASE_VIEW gate unchanged, route untouched in diff.
  - (c) ‚úÖ **Injection ‚Äî both new query inputs are BOUND, zero interpolation.** `revokedAssignmentIdsForUser` binds `$1=userId` (uuid actor) + `$2=cutoff.toISOString()` (server-built Date‚ÜíISO) as the params array ‚Äî no `${}` of any request data; the SQL is a static string. The `SYNC_SELECT` additions (`ct.started_at, ct.completed_at`) are hardcoded column literals (repository.ts:51), not request-derived. `cutoff` is the same server-validated Date used by the existing watermark (NaN‚Üí400 before any query). No ORDER BY/dynamic-SQL surface added. No new SQL string is request-constructed.
  - (d) ‚úÖ **Exposing `completedAt`/`inProgressAt` leaks nothing new.** Both map from `ct.started_at`/`ct.completed_at` (service.ts:36-37) and are emitted ONLY on rows ALREADY returned by `downloadForUser`, i.e. tasks where `ct.assigned_to = me` (the tightest scope). They are the device's OWN task execution timestamps (when this device started/finished its assignment) ‚Äî operational lifecycle metadata, not customer PII, and already implicitly known to the device that performed the work. Omitted when null (`...(r.startedAt ? {‚Ä¶} : {})`) so no phantom emission. No new applicant/PII column added to the projection; the rest of `SYNC_SELECT` is unchanged. Re-hydration after a local wipe is the intended purpose (service.ts:33-35 doc).
  - (e) ‚úÖ **Page-0-only delta is correctness, not a security concern; no secrets.** `revokedAssignmentIds` computed only at `offset === 0` (service.ts:89-90) ‚Äî a perf/idempotency choice (device restarts each cycle at offset 0); subsequent pages return `[]`, never another user's data. Tests assert the full posture: reassigned-away task ‚Üí old assignee's `revokedAssignmentIds=[taskId]` while NEW assignee gets `[]` (test:284-304); revoked-but-still-assigned ‚Üí `[]` (not a purge, test:320); page-0-only delta (test:386-404); `inProgressAt`/`completedAt` omitted-then-emitted on start/complete (test:326-351). No `console.*`/secrets/`SELECT *` in the diff (scanned clean).
  - DISPOSITION: **PASS.** `revokedAssignmentIds` is leak-proof by construction ‚Äî `previous_assigned_to=$me` (server-sourced from the prior `assigned_to`, parameterized) returns ONLY ids the device legitimately held; `userId` is JWT-derived and unspoofable behind the unchanged `CASE_VIEW` gate; both new query inputs are bound (no interpolation); `completedAt`/`inProgressAt` are the device's own execution timestamps (no new PII). OPEN (carried, non-blocking): the down-sync `assigned_to = me` contract filter remains the tightest scope (audit F2 ‚Äî re-test if a RESTRICT scope dimension is ever wired onto a field role); cases/task LIST row-scope gap (2026-06-06) unrelated to this device-scoped read.

- **2026-06-16 ¬∑ Billing slice 5a ‚Äî `commission_rates` master-data module (ADR-0036; `modules/commissionRates/{routes,controller,service,repository}.ts` + mig `0058_commission_rates.sql` + `sdk/commissionRates.ts`) ‚Äî money-config write surface, UNCOMMITTED ‚Äî VERDICT: PASS. No BLOCK.**
  - (a) ‚úÖ **Authz ‚Äî gate is byte-identical to the sibling `rates` module (CONFIRMED), default-deny.** GET `/` ‚Üí `authorize(MASTERDATA_VIEW)` (=`page.masterdata`), POST `/` + `/:id/{revise,activate,deactivate}` ‚Üí `authorize(MASTERDATA_MANAGE)` (=`masterdata.manage`) ‚Äî routes.ts:11-15. Verified `rates/routes.ts` uses the SAME pair (`MASTERDATA_VIEW` reads, `MASTERDATA_MANAGE` writes). `masterdata.manage` is granted to SUPER_ADMIN ONLY (via `Object.values(PERMISSIONS)`, permissions.ts:79); MANAGER/TEAM_LEADER/BACKEND_USER hold only `page.masterdata` (VIEW), FIELD_AGENT/KYC_VERIFIER hold neither (permissions.ts:80-114). So commission-rate CONFIG writes are SA-only ‚Äî correct authority for the agent-commission amount source; reads are admin-tier (the same audience as every other master-data list, e.g. `rates`). No FE-only gate; server is the real gate. Default-deny intact, no perm weakened, no new perm introduced.
  - (b) ‚öÝÔ∏è **CONFIDENTIALITY of the list ‚Äî SHOULD-FIX, non-blocking, consistent-with-precedent.** `GET /` returns EVERY user's per-(user, rate_type, client) commission AMOUNT plus `userName`/`userEmail` to ANY `page.masterdata` holder. Per `project_rbac_hierarchy_model` that audience is SUPER_ADMIN + **MANAGER + TEAM_LEADER + BACKEND_USER** (all 3 hold `page.masterdata`). So a TEAM_LEADER / BACKEND_USER can read what every other staff member earns per task ‚Äî i.e. peer/subordinate compensation is visible to all master-data viewers, with NO billing-scope (`billing.generate`) or hierarchy row-scope. This is the SAME unscoped-admin-list posture as the existing `rates` module and the standing "cases LIST has no row-level scope" OPEN (2026-06-06) ‚Äî NOT a regression introduced by this slice, and the data is internal-staff comp (not customer/DPDP PII). **HOWEVER** comp data is materially more sensitive than rate-cards/clients/products: a sensible hardening is to gate the commission-rate LIST behind `billing.*` (e.g. a `billing.view`/`BILLING_GENERATE`-class perm) rather than the broad `page.masterdata`, so only the billing-owning roles see per-user amounts. Recorded as SHOULD-FIX (confidentiality, not an injection/IDOR vuln); flagged to the owner for a product call. No row-scope exists today on any master-data list, so this matches precedent.
  - (c) ‚úÖ **Injection ‚Äî every request value bound; only whitelisted identifiers interpolated.** Traced ALL queries in repository.ts:
    - `list` (47-92): `userId`/`clientId`/`active` each appended via the `add()` helper that `params.push`es the value then rewrites `$?`‚Üí`$N` (54-56) ‚Äî bound, never interpolated. `search` ‚Üí `likeContains()` (wildcard-escaped) bound as one `$n` reused across the 5-column ILIKE (57-63). `columnFilters` go through `filterClauses` (`= ANY($n)`/`ILIKE $n`/`>= $n::date`/`< ($n::date+1)`/`= $n` ‚Äî all values bound; `f.column` is the server literal from `CR_PAGE_SPEC.filterMap`). `ids` ‚Üí `= ANY($n)` typed-array bind (65-68). `history` toggles a STATIC predicate (no value). ORDER BY interpolates ONLY `o.sortColumn` (= `CR_PAGE_SPEC.sortMap[sortBy]`, whitelisted via `resolvePage`‚Üí`hasOwnProperty`, default-fallback on unknown) + `o.sortOrder` (pinned `'asc'|'desc'`) + the `cr.id` literal tiebreaker; `limit`/`offset` bound as `$n+1`/`$n+2`. **`sortMap` + `filterMap` columns are all hardcoded literals** (`u.name`/`c.name`/`cr.rate_type`/`cr.amount`/`cr.effective_from`/`cr.is_active`/`cr.created_at`/`cr.updated_at`) ‚Äî no request-derived string reaches SQL text. Same trust model as the established sortMap control.
    - `create` (99-121): all 7 values bound `$1‚Äì$7`; `effectiveFrom` via `COALESCE($6::timestamptz, now())`. `revise` (124-161): `FOR UPDATE` select binds `$1`; both UPDATE (end-date) and INSERT bind every value; identity columns (`user_id`/`rate_type`/`client_id`/`currency`) are copied from the locked `cur` row, NOT from input. `setActive` (164-185) binds `$1‚Äì$4`. `resolveAmount` (194-205) binds `$1‚Äì$3`. Zero `${}` of request data anywhere except whitelisted identifiers. No injection surface.
  - (d) ‚úÖ **`:id` integer validation ‚Äî no 22P02‚Üí500.** `parseId` (controller.ts:7-11) `Number(req.params.id)`; `!Number.isInteger(id)||id<=0` ‚Üí 400 `BAD_REQUEST {param:'id'}` BEFORE any query ‚Äî so `revise`/`activate`/`deactivate` never pass a non-integer to the `integer`-PK `WHERE id=$1` (no Postgres 22P02 invalid-text-representation ‚Üí 500). `user_id` is `uuid` and `client_id` is `integer` on insert, but both come from zod-validated input (`uuid`/`positiveInt`) so neither can throw 22P02; a non-existent FK ‚Üí 23503 ‚Üí 400 `INVALID_REFERENCE` (mapWriteError, repo:26). Clean.
  - (e) ‚úÖ **Mass-assignment ‚Äî closed schema; `version`/`created_by` NOT client-settable.** `CreateCommissionRateSchema`/`ReviseCommissionRateSchema` are plain `z.object({‚Ä¶})` (sdk/commissionRates.ts:46-62) ‚Äî default zod STRIPS unknown keys, so a body carrying `version`/`createdBy`/`isActive`/`id`/`effectiveTo` has those silently dropped (not assigned). `created_by`/`updated_by` come from `userId(req)` = `req.auth?.userId` (controller.ts:12,25) ‚Äî the verified JWT subject, NEVER a body field. `version` is server-managed: `DEFAULT 1` on insert, `version+1` on every UPDATE; on revise/activate/deactivate the EXPECTED version is read via the separate `requireVersion(input)` OCC envelope (occ.ts:12-16 ‚Üí 400 VERSION_REQUIRED), never written from input. `amount` validated `z.number().nonnegative().max(9999999999.99)` + DB `CHECK (amount >= 0)` (mig:23) ‚Äî no negative-commission write. `currency` `z.string().length(3)`. (Same closed-object posture as sibling `rates`; matches the standing no-mass-assignment rule. NOTE non-blocking: schemas aren't `.strict()`, so unknown keys are dropped silently rather than 400'd ‚Äî identical to every other v2 module, accepted convention.)
  - (f) ‚úÖ **OCC integrity ‚Äî version-guarded, no silent overwrite.** `revise` (repo:132-157) runs in `withTransaction`, `SELECT ‚Ä¶ FOR UPDATE` the current row, `cur.version !== expectedVersion` ‚Üí `AppError.stale(cur)` (409 STALE_UPDATE) BEFORE any write; also rejects revising an inactive rate (409 COMMISSION_RATE_NOT_ACTIVE). It end-dates the current row FIRST then inserts the new dated version (never overwrites history ‚Äî effective-dated). `setActive` (repo:164-185) does `UPDATE ‚Ä¶ WHERE id=$1 AND version=$4`; 0 rows with the row present ‚Üí `AppError.stale(before)` (the `before` SELECT distinguishes 404 vs stale). The DB EXCLUDE constraint `commission_rates_no_overlap` (mig:38-43, GIST over user_id/rate_type/COALESCE(client_id,-1)/tstzrange WHERE is_active) prevents two overlapping active rates for the same (user, rate_type, client) ‚Üí 23P01 ‚Üí 409 COMMISSION_RATE_EXISTS (mapWriteError). Concurrent revise/create can't produce a double-active rate; OCC + the exclusion are belt-and-suspenders.
  - (g) ‚ÑπÔ∏è **"ANY user may hold rates" eligibility (owner decision) ‚Äî no security implication.** The migration/SDK note that field/office/KYC users may all hold commission rates (gate = "any COMPLETED task earns if its assignee has a matching rate") is a BUSINESS-eligibility decision, not an authz one: it does NOT widen who can WRITE rates (still SA-only `masterdata.manage`) nor who can READ them (still `page.masterdata`). `user_id` on a rate is an FK to `users(id)` validated by the no-overlap constraint + 23503 mapping; a rate row for any user is just config data. The actual commission PAYOUT is gated downstream by the billing engine reading `resolveAmount` per COMPLETED task (slice 5b) ‚Äî assigning a rate doesn't itself move money. No privilege escalation: a low-privilege user holding a rate gains no capability; only a COMPLETED task by them (driven through the existing task lifecycle, separately authorized) realizes it. Benign.
  - DISPOSITION: **PASS.** Gate is byte-identical to the audited `rates` sibling (VIEW=`page.masterdata`, MANAGE=`masterdata.manage` = SA-only), default-deny intact. All SQL fully parameterized ‚Äî every request value bound, only the whitelisted `sortMap`/`filterMap` literals + pinned sortOrder interpolated. `:id` int-guarded (no 22P02‚Üí500), FK/exclusion violations mapped to 400/409. Closed zod schemas (unknown keys stripped); `version` server-managed (`+1` / OCC envelope), `created_by`/`updated_by` from the JWT subject (no mass-assignment). OCC `FOR UPDATE` + version-guard + the GIST no-overlap EXCLUDE jointly prevent silent-overwrite and double-active rates. The "ANY user may hold rates" eligibility is a business gate, not an authz one ‚Äî no escalation. **SHOULD-FIX (non-blocking, confidentiality, owner product-call): the list exposes every user's per-task commission AMOUNT + name/email to all `page.masterdata` holders (MANAGER/TEAM_LEADER/BACKEND_USER), with no billing-scope or hierarchy row-scope. Comp data is more sensitive than rate-cards ‚Äî consider gating the commission-rate LIST behind a `billing.*` perm rather than broad `page.masterdata`. Same unscoped-admin-list class as the standing cases-LIST row-scope OPEN (2026-06-06); not a regression of this slice.** OPEN (carried): sortMap/filterMap literal-only rule reaffirmed; when row-scope lands on master-data lists, apply it to BOTH the count and items query so totalCount can't leak out-of-scope existence.

- **2026-06-16 ¬∑ Billing slice 5b ‚Äî per-case Billing & Commission READ-model (ADR-0036; `modules/billing/{routes,controller,service,repository}.ts` + mig `0059_billing_view_perm.sql` + new perm `billing.view` + `sdk/billing.ts`) ‚Äî scoped money read surface (bill + agent-commission AMOUNTS), UNCOMMITTED ‚Äî VERDICT: PASS. No FLAG. No BLOCK.**
  - (a) ‚úÖ **Authz ‚Äî `billing.view` is the correct gate, and it RESOLVES the 5a confidentiality SHOULD-FIX rather than re-opening it.** The two list routes + the lines route gate on `BILLING_VIEW`=`billing.view`; export gates on `DATA_EXPORT`=`data.export` (routes.ts:12-14). The new perm is granted to **MANAGER + BACKEND_USER** only (permissions.ts:84-118 + mig:10-13; SA via `grants_all`) ‚Äî **NOT** TEAM_LEADER, FIELD_AGENT, or KYC_VERIFIER. This is exactly the coherent split the 5a entry asked for: the agent-commission AMOUNTS read-model now sits behind a dedicated `billing.*` perm scoped to the billing-owning roles, instead of the broad `page.masterdata` that TEAM_LEADER/BACKEND_USER share. Note the asymmetry is deliberate and correct ‚Äî **5a (commission CONFIG writes) stays `masterdata.manage`=SA-only** (config is the most privileged), while **5b (computed amounts, read-only) opens to the billing OPERATORS** (MANAGER/BACKEND_USER) who must actually reconcile money. TEAM_LEADER ‚Äî who held the broad `page.masterdata` and could see 5a's raw config list ‚Äî is now EXCLUDED from the computed-amounts surface (test asserts TL‚Üí403, billing.api.test.ts:241). So 5b NARROWS, not widens, who sees commission money vs the pre-5a-fix posture. Default-deny intact, server is the real gate (FE role checks cosmetic), no existing perm weakened, the new perm added to exactly 2 roles. Roles-parity gate covers it: `roles.parity.test.ts:62-81` asserts the DB `role_permissions` set is byte-identical to `ROLE_PERMISSIONS` for all 6 roles, and `ALL_PERMISSIONS` (line 13) auto-includes `billing.view` via `Object.values(PERMISSIONS)` ‚Üí SA's `grants_all` expansion and the MANAGER/BACKEND_USER explicit rows are both checked. Mig is forward-only/idempotent (`ON CONFLICT DO NOTHING`) and mirrors the code map ‚Üí parity holds.
  - (b) ‚úÖ **Scope/IDOR ‚Äî out-of-scope/absent ‚Üí 404 (NOT 403), `:id` uuid-validated (no 22P02‚Üí500), defence-in-depth scope on BOTH list+count.** The lines route guards via `repo.caseVisible(caseId, scope)` ‚Üí `false` ‚Üí `AppError.notFound('CASE_NOT_FOUND')` (service.ts:115); an absent case and an out-of-scope case are INDISTINGUISHABLE (same-404-as-absent, no existence oracle). `parseCaseId` (controller.ts:13-17) rejects any non-uuid via `UUID_RE` ‚Üí 400 `BAD_REQUEST {param:'id'}` BEFORE the `WHERE cs.id=$1` (uuid col) ever runs ‚Üí no Postgres 22P02 invalid-text-representation ‚Üí 500. Tests prove all three: absent uuid‚Üí404 (test:245), `not-a-uuid`‚Üí400 (test:247), real in-scope‚Üí200 (test:249). The LIST applies `caseScopePredicate` (repository.ts:11-19) to BOTH the COUNT query (repo:98-101) and the items query (repo:104-116) using the SAME shared `params`/`where` ‚Äî so a filtered `totalCount` can never leak the existence of out-of-scope rows (the standing count+items-parity rule, satisfied here by shared `where`). The predicate composes through `composeScopePredicate` (scope/index.ts:38-70) which fail-closes a wired-but-unassigned RESTRICT dimension to `FALSE` and emits `''` only for hierarchy-ALL (SUPER_ADMIN). `caseVisible` reuses the identical predicate (repo:121-130) so list visibility and lines reachability never disagree (no read-then-deny / deny-then-read split).
