  - (c) ‚úÖ **Adversarial: can a MANAGER see commission AMOUNTS for users OUTSIDE their hierarchy via the billing list? ‚Äî BOUNDED at case grain, with one honestly-disclosed sum-aggregation edge that is NOT a leak.** The scope predicate is CASE-grain: a case is visible iff `cs.created_by = ANY(in-scope uids) OR EXISTS(task on that case assigned_to = ANY(in-scope uids))` (repo:16). MANAGER hierarchy mode = SUBTREE (parity test:39-43 ‚Üí self + recursive reports_to subtree), so the visible case SET is bounded to cases the manager's subtree created or works. **Edge (analyzed, benign):** within a VISIBLE case, `commission_total` SUMs `com.commission_amount` over ALL its completed tasks, and commission resolves per-task on `cmr.user_id = ct.assigned_to` (COMMISSION_LATERAL repo:44). So if a visible case happens to also carry a task assigned to an agent OUTSIDE the manager's subtree, that out-of-subtree agent's per-task commission is INCLUDED in the case's aggregate `commissionTotal`. This is (i) only reachable for a case ALREADY in scope (the case-grain gate is the boundary ‚Äî you cannot conjure visibility of an arbitrary user's earnings; you must first legitimately see the case), (ii) an AGGREGATE per case, not a per-user breakdown in the list (the list never names the out-of-subtree agent), and (iii) the per-task `assigneeName` + `commissionAmount` breakdown is ONLY in the lines endpoint, which is itself gated by the same `caseVisible` scope ‚Äî so the only names/amounts a manager sees belong to tasks on cases they can already see. The CASE is the unit of authorization for billing (a billing operator reconciles money per CASE, and a case's total cost legitimately includes every task on it regardless of who executed each) ‚Äî this is the intended, coherent grain, not an IDOR. Recorded as an OPEN note, not a flag: IF product later wants per-user commission isolation (an agent's earnings never visible to a manager outside that agent's hierarchy even when they share a case), the commission leg would need an additional `ct.assigned_to ‚àà in-scope` predicate ‚Äî but that would distort the case's true total cost, so it is a product decision, not a security defect. Today operators are office-wide (repo:50-51 comment) so the practical exposure is the intended office-wide billing view; the scope predicate is correct defence-in-depth that will tighten automatically if a RESTRICT dimension is ever wired onto a billing role.
  - (d) ‚úÖ **Injection ‚Äî every request value bound; only whitelisted identifiers interpolated; the LATERAL subqueries are static.** `clientId` ‚Üí `toPosInt` (service.ts:35-37, `Number.isInteger && >0` else dropped) bound via the `add()` helper that `params.push`es then rewrites `$?`‚Üí`$N` (repo:77-79). `completedFrom`/`completedTo` ‚Üí `asStr` (non-empty string) bound as `ct.completed_at >= $? / <= $?` (repo:82-83). `search` ‚Üí `likeContains()` (wildcard-escaped, pagination.ts:106-109) bound once and reused across the 3-column ILIKE (repo:84-88). `columnFilters` go through `resolveFilters`‚Üí`filterClauses` (whitelisted `f.column` from `BILLING_PAGE_SPEC.filterMap` = `cl.name`/`cs.case_number`/`ct.completed_at` literals; all values bound ‚Äî `ILIKE $n`/`>= $n::date`/`< ($n::date+1)`). `ids` (export selected mode) ‚Üí `cs.id = ANY($n)` typed-array bind (repo:90-93), pre-filtered to strings (service.ts:92). ORDER BY interpolates ONLY `o.sortColumn` (= `BILLING_PAGE_SPEC.sortMap[sortBy]`, whitelisted via `resolvePage`‚Üí`hasOwnProperty`, default-fallback `lastCompletedAt` on unknown) + `o.sortOrder` (pinned `'asc'|'desc'`) + the `cs.id` literal tiebreaker; `limit`/`offset` bound `$n+1`/`$n+2`. The two LATERALs (RATE_LATERAL repo:28-39, COMMISSION_LATERAL repo:41-48) are STATIC strings containing only column refs + `now()` + the `rt.rate_type` correlation ‚Äî ZERO request-derived input reaches them (the rate ladder reuses the cases/repository TASK_VIEW_COLS shape, not forked). No request string reaches SQL text anywhere; same trust model as the established sortMap/filterMap control. Aggregate-alias sort targets (`bill_total`/`commission_total`/`completed_task_count`/`last_completed_at`) are valid PG ORDER BY over the GROUP BY (service.ts:13-14 note); filters land in the pre-aggregation WHERE so no HAVING-injection surface.
  - (e) ‚úÖ **Export path enforces scope + caps rows; actor JWT-derived, unspoofable.** `export` (controller.ts:28-43) builds `actor(req)` from `req.auth` (fail-closed `if(!req.auth) throw unauthenticated()`, controller.ts:8-12) and calls `svc.exportData` which RE-RUNS the SAME scoped `repo.listCases` (resolveScope + caseScopePredicate, service.ts:85-109) ‚Äî the export cannot bypass row-scope (it is the identical query the list uses, never an unscoped variant). `mode:'all'` calls `assertExportable(totalCount)` (service.ts:108 ‚Üí 413 EXPORT_TOO_LARGE at the job threshold, export/index.ts:51-60) so a scoped-but-large set can't stream unbounded inline; `mode:'current'` honours the page limit, `mode:'selected'` binds the ticked `ids` through the same scoped WHERE (so a victim can't export an out-of-scope case by passing its id ‚Äî the scope predicate still ANDs). Export gated on `data.export` (held by MANAGER/TEAM_LEADER/BACKEND_USER) ‚Äî but note the EXPORTED COLUMNS include `commissionTotal`/`billTotal` (BILLING_EXPORT_COLUMNS service.ts:41-50), and the route is reached only after `authorize(DATA_EXPORT)`; since TEAM_LEADER holds `data.export` but NOT `billing.view`, **the `/cases/export` route is correctly gated on `DATA_EXPORT` and the LIST/lines on `BILLING_VIEW`** ‚Äî verify FE never surfaces the billing export to a TL (server lets a TL hit `/billing/cases/export` because it only checks `data.export`). ‚öÝÔ∏è **SHOULD-FIX (non-blocking, minor authz gap): `/cases/export` gates ONLY on `DATA_EXPORT`, so a TEAM_LEADER (holds `data.export`, NOT `billing.view`) CAN export the billing+commission amounts even though they are 403'd from the `/cases` list itself.** The export thus leaks the exact money columns the `billing.view` gate is meant to withhold from TL. Low severity (TL is still in-org, subtree-scoped, and the data is internal comp not customer PII) but it is an inconsistency ‚Äî the export should ALSO require `billing.view` (e.g. `authorize(BILLING_VIEW, DATA_EXPORT)` or a combined check) so the export audience matches the list audience. Recorded as SHOULD-FIX, not a BLOCK: no injection/IDOR, scope still enforced, only the perm-pairing is looser than the list.
  - DISPOSITION: **PASS.** `billing.view` is the right gate and its grant to MANAGER+BACKEND_USER (excluding TEAM_LEADER/FIELD_AGENT/KYC) is the coherent split that RESOLVES the 5a confidentiality SHOULD-FIX ‚Äî computed commission amounts now sit behind a dedicated billing perm, not broad `page.masterdata`, and 5a config writes correctly stay SA-only. Scope is defence-in-depth on BOTH list+count (shared `where`, no totalCount existence-oracle); lines endpoint is same-404-as-absent (no IDOR oracle); `:id` uuid-validated (no 22P02‚Üí500). All SQL parameterized ‚Äî every request value bound, only whitelisted `sortMap`/`filterMap` literals + pinned sortOrder interpolated; the two amount LATERALs are static (no request input). Export re-runs the scoped list + `assertExportable`. The case-grain commission aggregation edge (a visible case's total may include an out-of-subtree agent's commission) is the intended billing grain, not a leak. **SHOULD-FIX (non-blocking): `/cases/export` is gated on `DATA_EXPORT` alone, letting a TEAM_LEADER (no `billing.view`) export the very money columns they're 403'd from on the list ‚Äî pair the export gate with `BILLING_VIEW` so export and list share one audience.** OPEN (carried): if product later wants per-user commission isolation within a shared case, add an `assigned_to ‚àà in-scope` leg to the commission LATERAL (a product call ‚Äî it would distort true case cost); sortMap/filterMap literal-only + count+items-scope-parity rules reaffirmed.

- **2026-06-16 ¬∑ ADR-0036 BILLING SLICE 5d ‚Äî derived `billAmount`/`commissionAmount` on the Pipeline TaskView + Commissionable bucket/filter/export, gated by `billing.view` (uncommitted) ‚Äî VERDICT: PASS.**
  - **The central question (can a non-`billing.view` actor get amounts via ANY path?) ‚Äî NO, every path is fail-closed at the controller's single `canViewBilling` flag.** `canViewBilling(req)` (controller.ts:18-20) = `req.auth.grantsAll === true || (req.auth.permissions ?? []).includes(BILLING_VIEW)`. Both fields are populated by the GLOBAL `enrichAuth()` (app.ts:75, mounted before every `/api/v2` module) ‚Üí never undefined at read time; an unknown/inactive role ‚Üí `grantsAll=false, permissions=[]` ‚Üí flag `false` (default-deny). `billing.view` is held ONLY by SUPER_ADMIN (grants_all), MANAGER, BACKEND_USER (permissions.ts:94-118) ‚Äî NOT FIELD_AGENT/TEAM_LEADER/KYC_VERIFIER, who hold the `case.view`(list/stats)/`data.export`(export) gates on the tasks routes (routes.ts:12-16). Traced controller‚Üíservice‚Üírepo for each surface:
    - **list** (`GET /api/v2/tasks`): `svc.list(q, actor, canViewBilling)` threads the flag ‚Üí service adds `billing:true` to repo opts ONLY when `canViewBilling` (service.ts:128) ‚Üí repo `const billing = o.billing ?? false` selects `selectFrom = billing ? TASK_FROM_BILLING : TASK_FROM` and `amountCols = billing ? BILLING_AMOUNT_COLS : NULL_AMOUNT_COLS` (repo:148-158). For a non-holder the laterals are NEVER joined and the SELECT emits `NULL::float8 AS bill_amount, NULL::float8 AS commission_amount` ‚Äî the amounts are absent from the SQL, not merely hidden in JS. `billable` (=`ct.status='COMPLETED'`, status-derived, NOT sensitive) is always present. Test asserts FA sees `billable:true, billAmount:null, commissionAmount:null` (tasks.api.test.ts:744-746).
    - **stats** (commissionable existence-count leak?): `svc.stats(...canViewBilling)` adds `billing:true` only when holder (service.ts:160). Repo computes `commissionable` in a SEPARATE guarded block `if (o.billing){...}` else leaves it `0` (repo:190-209) and spreads it onto the base row. A non-holder gets `commissionable:0` UNCONDITIONALLY ‚Äî the count never runs, so it cannot leak how many commissioned tasks exist. Test: FA `stats.commissionable===0` (test:748-749). The existing PENDING/ASSIGNED/IN_PROGRESS/COMPLETED/REVOKED/outOfTat buckets are non-sensitive status counts, unchanged, over lateral-free `TASK_FROM`.
    - **commissionable=1 filter (does ignoring it leak commissioned-row membership?)**: NO. Service only sets `commissionable:true` when `canViewBilling && d.commissionable` (service.ts:127); for a non-holder the flag is dropped AND not echoed into `filters` (service.ts:144 same guard). Repo defence-in-depth: `const commissionable = billing && !!o.commissionable` (repo:140) ‚Äî a stray `commissionable:true` can never reach the WHERE without `billing` also true (which a non-holder never has). So the predicate `ct.status='COMPLETED' AND com.commission_amount IS NOT NULL` (repo:129, references the `com` lateral) is unreachable for non-holders, and the COUNT/items stay over lateral-free `TASK_FROM` (`countFrom = commissionable ? TASK_FROM_BILLING : TASK_FROM`, repo:146). Result for a TL: the filter is IGNORED ‚Äî the full scoped list comes back with `filters:{}` (CTO live-verified on :4000), so row MEMBERSHIP is NOT narrowed-to-commissioned (no oracle: you can't infer "these N rows are the commissioned ones" because the filter had no effect and the amounts are null anyway).
    - **export (CSV columns)**: `svc.exportData(...canViewBilling)` builds columns via `taskExportColumns(canViewBilling)` (service.ts:174,179) ‚Äî the `Bill Amount`/`Commission` columns are PUSHED only inside `if (canViewBilling)` (service.ts:36-41 new fn). For a non-holder those two columns are OMITTED from the manifest entirely AND the underlying rows carry null amounts (repo nulls them ‚Äî `billing` only true when holder, service.ts:191). So even if a column slipped through, the value would be null. **This is the 5b money-export rule applied correctly**: the export carrying comp data does NOT rely on `data.export` alone ‚Äî the comp COLUMNS are gated on the resource perm (`canViewBilling`) and nulled+omitted for a `data.export`-only TEAM_LEADER. A TL CANNOT exfiltrate amounts via CSV. (Contrast the 5b billing-module `/cases/export` SHOULD-FIX where the whole route gates on `DATA_EXPORT` and leaks the money columns to a TL ‚Äî 5d AVOIDS that mistake by column-omission rather than route-perm, so no BLOCK here.) Note: the SA export header test asserts the columns ARE present for a holder (test:578).
    - **sort / crafted query param**: amount columns are NOT in `TASK_PAGE_SPEC.sortMap` (they live only in the billing FROM), so `?sortBy=billAmount` falls back to `defaultSort` via the established `resolvePage` whitelist (sort-injection control unchanged) ‚Äî no way to order-by or surface an amount through sort. No raw query key reaches the billing decision; `canViewBilling` derives solely from JWT-backed `req.auth`, unspoofable by query param.
  - **(2) Export columns gating ‚Äî CORRECT (5b money-export rule satisfied).** Confirmed a `data.export`-only TEAM_LEADER cannot exfiltrate amounts: columns omitted (`taskExportColumns(false)` drops Bill Amount/Commission) AND rows nulled (`billing` false ‚Üí `NULL_AMOUNT_COLS`). Double-gated. The route still gates on `data.export` (unchanged) but the SENSITIVE payload is keyed off `billing.view` ‚Äî exactly the resource-perm-not-just-data.export posture the 5b rule demands.
  - **(3) IDOR/scope ‚Äî orthogonal, fully preserved.** The billing gate ONLY nulls amounts / skips laterals / inerts the commissionable filter; it NEVER touches `taskScopePredicate`. `buildWhere` always appends `taskScopePredicate(params, o.scope)` (repo:131-132) regardless of `billing`, and `scope` is resolved from the actor independent of `canViewBilling` (service.ts:122,158,184). A non-holder sees exactly the SAME rows (their scoped set) as before 5d ‚Äî just with null amounts. Gating cannot widen visibility (it only subtracts columns); a holder sees amounts only on rows already in their scope. The COUNT and items share the same `where`/`params` (repo:143-160) so totalCount carries no out-of-scope existence oracle (count+items-parity rule intact). When `commissionable` filters the set it only NARROWS (adds an AND), never widens.
  - **(4) SQL injection ‚Äî none; laterals + commissionable predicate are param-free constants.** `RATE_LATERAL`/`COMMISSION_LATERAL` (the NEW `platform/billing/laterals.ts`) are static string constants ‚Äî only column refs, `now()`, `is_active`, and the `rt.rate_type` correlation; ZERO request-derived input. The commissionable predicate `ct.status='COMPLETED' AND com.commission_amount IS NOT NULL` is a literal (no bind, no interpolation of user data). `commissionable`/`billing` are booleans (coerced from `===  '1'|'true'` in `domainParams`, service.ts:101) that only SELECT which static FROM/cols/predicate string to use ‚Äî they never reach SQL text as values. The file is a pure REFACTOR-EXTRACTION: billing/repository.ts:21-48 previously held byte-identical `RATE_LATERAL`/`COMMISSION_LATERAL` locals (now imported from the shared module) ‚Äî diff confirms the two laterals moved verbatim, so the billing read-model is unchanged and the Pipeline read-model reuses the identical proven SQL (no fork/drift).
  - **(5b billing-export SHOULD-FIX status):** 5d does NOT re-introduce the 5b gap and is the CORRECT pattern (column-omission keyed on the resource perm). The 5b `/billing/cases/export` route-level `DATA_EXPORT`-only gap remains OPEN/carried from the prior entry ‚Äî unaffected by 5d.
  - **(non-security) SHOULD-FIX, flagged to Operations/CTO:** the export path's `repo.list` spread DROPPED the pre-existing `assignedTo` filter (the diff replaced `...(d.assignedTo? {assignedTo}:{})` with the `...commissionable`/`...billing` lines, service.ts:185-191) ‚Äî `GET /tasks/export?assignedTo=<uuid>` now ignores that narrowing. **Security-neutral**: dropping a filter can only WIDEN within the already-applied `scope` (which still fully constrains the rows), never bypass scope or leak amounts (still `billing.view`-gated). But it is a CORRECTNESS regression vs the list (which still honours `assignedTo`, service.ts:125) ‚Äî export and list now disagree. Recommend restoring the `assignedTo` spread in `exportData`. Not a BLOCK.
  - DISPOSITION: **PASS.** Single authoritative `canViewBilling` flag threaded controller‚Üíservice‚Üírepo gates every amount surface (list nulls+skips-laterals, stats commissionable=0, commissionable filter inert+unechoed, export columns omitted+rows nulled, sort whitelist excludes amounts) ‚Äî a non-`billing.view` actor (FIELD_AGENT/TEAM_LEADER) gets `billable` (non-sensitive status flag) but NULL ‚Çπ amounts and a 0 Commissionable bucket via EVERY path, matching CTO live evidence (:4000: SA ‚Çπ150/‚Çπ40 on CASE-000030-1; owning FA billable=true/amounts=null/commissionable=0; TL commissionable=1 ‚Üí filters:{}) and the 5DG/5DA/5DB gating tests (DB-gated `skipIf(!RUN)`; assertions read directly + CTO ran green live). Scope orthogonal and fully preserved (no widening); SQL param-free static laterals (no injection); laterals.ts is a verbatim refactor-extraction (no read-model drift). SHOULD-FIX (non-security, non-blocking): restore the dropped `assignedTo` filter in `exportData` (export‚Üîlist parity). OPEN (carried): 5b `/billing/cases/export` route still `DATA_EXPORT`-only (pair with `BILLING_VIEW`); FE must hide the Pipeline billing columns/bucket from non-holders (server is authoritative ‚Äî confirmed ‚Äî so FE is cosmetic).

- **2026-06-16 ¬∑ ADR-0037 MIS ENGINE SLICE 1 ‚Äî `reportLayouts` admin config module (routes/controller/service/repository + SDK `reportLayouts.ts` + mig 0060) ‚Äî VERDICT: PASS.**
  - (1) ‚úÖ **RBAC ‚Äî ALL 7 routes gate `report_template.manage` (TEMPLATE_MANAGE), no ungated route.** routes.ts:12-19: GET `/`, GET `/by-config`, GET `/:id`, POST `/`, PUT `/:id`, POST `/:id/activate`, POST `/:id/deactivate` ‚Äî every line `authorize(PERMISSIONS.TEMPLATE_MANAGE)`. Mounted behind global `authenticate()`+`enrichAuth()` (app.ts:74-75, mount :96). `authorize` (authorize.ts:30) is **default-deny**: 401 if no `req.auth`; 403 unless `grantsAll===true` OR `permissions.includes(perm)`. `report_template.manage` is granted to **SUPER_ADMIN ONLY** ‚Äî it appears in NO other role's list in `ROLE_PERMISSIONS` (permissions.ts:82-118); SA gets it via `Object.values(PERMISSIONS)` (:83). MANAGER/TEAM_LEADER/BACKEND_USER/FIELD_AGENT/KYC_VERIFIER all LACK it ‚Üí 403 on every route (read+write). Test asserts BACKEND_USER‚Üí403 on GET `/` and POST `/` (api.test.ts:228-232); the other 5 mount byte-identical middleware so the gate is structurally guaranteed. **Reusing `report_template.manage` (vs a new perm) is SOUND**: layouts are the config-engine sibling of the narrative report templates (same admin surface, same SA-only audience, same Administration group); a new perm would only matter if layout-admin needed to be delegated separately from template-admin ‚Äî not a requirement here. Default-deny HOLDS.
  - (2) ‚úÖ **INJECTION (the key concern) ‚Äî `source_type`/`source_ref`/`column_key`/`name`/`section`/`header_label` are STORED ONLY AS BIND PARAMS, never interpolated.** `insertColumns` (repository.ts:47-65) INSERTs all column fields as `$1..$11` positional params (`source_type`‚Üí$4, `source_ref`‚Üí$5, `column_key`‚Üí$2, jsonb via `$10::jsonb`/`$11::jsonb` with `JSON.stringify`). Header INSERT (:167-170) binds `name`/`kind` as `$1..$5`. UPDATE (:199-202) binds `name`‚Üí$2 (`COALESCE($2,name)`). Every `${...}` in repository.ts is a **server literal** (`${COLUMN_COLS}`,`${HEADER_COLS}`,`${LAYOUT_FROM}` const projections) or a **`$N` placeholder index** ‚Äî the `add()` helper (:93-96) pushes the VALUE to params and only injects `$${params.length}` into the clause string (value never reaches SQL text); `clause` is `where[]` join of static `$N` predicates. **`source_ref`/`column_key`/`source_type` NEVER reach ORDER BY or any string-built SQL** ‚Äî they are not keys in `LAYOUT_PAGE_SPEC.sortMap` (only client/product/kind/name/status/createdAt/updatedAt ‚Üí literal columns) nor `filterMap`. `${o.sortColumn} ${o.sortOrder}` (:120) is whitelisted via `resolvePage` (sort-injection control, unchanged). `kind` list-filter (:99) and search ILIKE (:102-104) are bound. **FORWARD-LOOKING DON'T-REGRESS for generation slices:** `source_ref` in FREE modes (FORM_DATA_PATH/COMPUTED/DATA_ENTRY_FIELD/DOC_TYPE_COUNT) is stored RAW (sdk validateColumnSource only checks non-empty) ‚Äî when a future generation slice MAPS `source_ref`‚ÜíSQL/json-path/expression, that resolver MUST NOT string-interpolate it (parameterize the json-path; whitelist/AST-validate any COMPUTED expression; never `eval`). This slice only STORES ‚Äî no resolution surface exists yet.
  - (3) ‚úÖ **Input validation ‚Äî allow-list airtight for FIXED/REFLESS, intentionally permissive for FREE.** `validateColumnSource` (sdk:102-114) via `superRefine` on every column: FIXED (TASK/CASE/APPLICANT_FIELD) ‚Üí `source_ref` MUST ‚àà enumerated `fields[].key` (rejects unknown ref); REFLESS (RATE/COMMISSION_AMOUNT/TAT) ‚Üí `source_ref` MUST be empty; FREE ‚Üí non-empty only. `sourceType` is `z.enum(SOURCE_TYPES)`, `dataType` `z.enum(COLUMN_DATA_TYPES)`, `columnKey` regex `^[a-z0-9_]+$` (‚â§80), bounded lengths, ‚â§200 cols, unique keys, `kind`‚ààLAYOUT_KINDS. DB CHECK constraints mirror the enums (mig 0060:15,37-39,41). The FREE-mode raw `source_ref` is the only stored-value risk and is FLAGGED forward (see #2).
  - (4) ‚úÖ **Scope/IDOR ‚Äî SA-only GLOBAL admin, NO per-actor data scope needed (correct call).** Layouts reference `client_id`/`product_id` but config CRUD is SUPER_ADMIN-only (like commission_rates/master-data) ‚Äî an admin manages ALL clients' layouts; there is no per-actor ownership to scope. `:id` is `parseId` int-guarded (controller.ts:7-11 ‚Üí 400 on non-int, no string reaches the `WHERE id=$1` int cast). 404 REPORT_LAYOUT_NOT_FOUND on miss (repository.ts:196,227 ‚Äî IDOR-safe). OCC version-guarded (ADR-0019) on update/(de)activate. Confirmed the right posture.
  - (5) ‚úÖ **Secrets/PII ‚Äî NONE.** Tables/SELECTs carry column DEFINITIONS only (key/label/source_type/source_ref/data_type/order/section/options/validation) ‚Äî no customer/applicant data, no credentials. `created_by`/`updated_by` are staff uuids (audit, behind SA gate). No `console.*`/secrets/`SELECT *` in the module (scanned). NOTE: the FIXED catalog ENUMERATES applicant PII column KEYS (APPLICANT_FIELD: name/mobile/pan) as bindable ‚Äî that's metadata (what a future MIS column COULD bind to), not data; PII exposure risk lands on the GENERATION slice that resolves those binds (carry to that slice's audit: resolved applicant PII in an MIS export must stay behind the same scope/perm as the cases list).
  - DISPOSITION: **PASS.** Pure admin config-store slice: SA-only on all 7 routes (default-deny intact), all user text bound (zero injection surface ‚Äî sort/filter whitelisted, no raw ref in SQL), allow-list-validated source binds, no scope/PII concern for stored config. Matches CTO live evidence (BACKEND_USER‚Üí403 on :4000). **CARRIED forward to generation slices (DON'T-REGRESS):** (i) `source_ref`‚ÜíSQL/json-path/expression resolution MUST parameterize / AST-whitelist (never interpolate or eval FREE refs); (ii) resolved APPLICANT_FIELD PII in MIS/Billing output must inherit the cases-list scope+perm.

- **2026-06-16 ¬∑ ADR-0037 MIS ENGINE SLICE 3a ‚Äî office data-entry `caseDataEntries` module (routes/controller/service/repository + SDK `caseDataEntries.ts` + mig 0061 + `data_entry.manage` perm) ‚Äî VERDICT: PASS.**
  - (1) ‚úÖ **RBAC ‚Äî BOTH routes gate `data_entry.manage` (DATA_ENTRY_MANAGE); default-deny holds; TL/FA blocked on both.** routes.ts:12-13 ‚Äî GET `/tasks/:taskId` AND PUT `/tasks/:taskId` each `authorize(PERMISSIONS.DATA_ENTRY_MANAGE)`, no ungated route. Mounted behind global `authenticate()`+`enrichAuth()` (app.ts:74-75, mount `/api/v2/data-entry` :96). `authorize` (authorize.ts:30) default-deny: 401 no `req.auth`; 403 unless `grantsAll===true` OR `permissions.includes('data_entry.manage')`. Grant set = **MANAGER + BACKEND_USER** (permissions.ts:99/121 ROLE_PERMISSIONS + mig 0061 `role_permissions` INSERT MANAGER/BACKEND_USER) + **SUPER_ADMIN** via `Object.values(PERMISSIONS)`. **TEAM_LEADER and FIELD_AGENT hold NEITHER** (TL list ends at DATA_EXPORT with no data_entry.manage; FA = `[CASE_VIEW, LOCATION_CAPTURE, TASK_EXECUTE]` only) ‚Üí 403 on BOTH routes. Test asserts TL‚Üí403 on GET (api.test.ts:231-232); PUT mounts byte-identical middleware so the gate is structurally guaranteed. CTO live-proved TL‚Üí403. **Audience is correct: office operators (MANAGER/BACKEND_USER), NOT field agents** ‚Äî keying MIS fields is an office/back-office function; FIELD_AGENT executing in the mobile app must not key office MIS data. data_entry.manage is the right, dedicated perm (not overloading template/billing).
  - (2) ‚úÖ **Scope / IDOR (the key one) ‚Äî `taskScope` applied on BOTH get AND save BEFORE any layout/entry access; out-of-scope/absent ‚Üí null ‚Üí 404 (indistinguishable).** Both service methods resolve scope then scope-guard the task IDENTICALLY: get (service.ts:19-21) `resolveScope(actor)` ‚Üí `repo.taskScope(taskId, scope)` ‚Üí `if(!t) throw notFound('TASK_NOT_FOUND')` BEFORE `findActiveByConfig`/`findByTask` (:22-23); save (service.ts:30-32) same `resolveScope`‚Üí`taskScope`‚Üí404 BEFORE layout load + write (:33-49). `repo.taskScope` (repository.ts:21-31) composes `taskScopePredicate(params, scope)` (scope/index.ts:79-87) into `WHERE ct.id=$1 AND <pred>` over `case_tasks ct JOIN cases cs` ‚Äî the TASK-grain hierarchy/dimension predicate (`ct.assigned_to = ANY($n) OR cs.created_by = ANY($n)` + EXPAND/RESTRICT legs, fail-closed). An in-perm but OUT-OF-SCOPE MANAGER/BACKEND_USER (outside the case's hierarchy subtree / portfolio) ‚Üí predicate excludes the row ‚Üí `rows[0] ?? null` ‚Üí **404 TASK_NOT_FOUND**, SAME response as a truly absent task ‚Äî no existence oracle, IDOR-safe for READ and WRITE. The unscoped `findByTask`/`update`/`insert` (repository.ts:33-83) are reached ONLY after the scope check passes, so they can never touch an out-of-scope task. SUPER_ADMIN / hierarchy-ALL ‚Üí `pred=''` (no filter, sees all) ‚Äî intended. CTO live-proved absent‚Üí404, non-uuid‚Üí400. Test asserts out-of-scope/absent uuid‚Üí404 (api.test.ts:233-237). NOTE: the out-of-scope **WRITE** path isn't separately tested (only read), but it is the SAME `repo.taskScope` call on the identical code path (service.ts:31 == :20) so it is structurally guarded ‚Äî recommend a non-blocking test adding an out-of-scope PUT‚Üí404 for completeness.
  - (3) ‚úÖ **Injection ‚Äî `data` jsonb + `taskId` reach SQL ONLY as bind params; column_key allow-list is server-owned; no `data` content interpolated.** `taskId` is UUID-regex pre-validated (service.ts:18,28 `UUID_RE.test` ‚Üí 400 BAD_REQUEST else) and bound `$1` everywhere (taskScope :24-29, findByTask :35, insert :49-52, update :71-79). `data` is **NEVER** interpolated: insert binds `$3::jsonb` with `JSON.stringify(data)` (repository.ts:50-52); update binds `$2::jsonb` with `JSON.stringify(data)` (:77-79). The **allow-list** (service.ts:36-44) iterates `layout.columns` (server-owned, loaded from DB via `findActiveByConfig`‚Üí`findDetail`, NOT from the request) and copies only `supplied[c.columnKey]` ‚Äî a key present in `data` but ABSENT from the layout is simply never read (the loop only ever indexes by server column_keys), so a malicious/unknown key (test `bogus:'drop me'`, api.test.ts:162) is DROPPED and cannot be persisted. Critically, **column_key is used only as a JS object index, never concatenated into SQL** ‚Äî even a `columnKey` containing SQL metacharacters would be (a) constrained at config time by the `^[a-z0-9_]+$` regex (slice-1) and (b) irrelevant here since it never reaches SQL text; only the resulting `clean` object's VALUES go in via the single `$N::jsonb` bind. `findActiveByConfig` (reportLayouts/repository.ts:148-160) is fully parameterized ($1 clientId/$2 productId/$3 kind, all server-derived from `taskScope`). Zero request string reaches SQL text. OCC `version` is `requireVersion(input)` (occ.ts:12, int-validated ‚Üí 400) bound `$4` in the UPDATE's `AND version=$4` ‚Äî no injection, and STALE‚Üí409 surfaces the fresh row.
  - (4) ‚è≠Ô∏è **Stored-data forward risk (DON'T-REGRESS for the GENERATION slice, NOT a 3a blocker) ‚Äî operator `data` values are stored RAW jsonb (un-encoded).** `data` map values are operator free-text (z.unknown, SaveDataEntrySchema sdk:18) and persisted verbatim. 3a only STORES + echoes them back as JSON to the same-perm UI (no HTML render surface here; JSON response is inherently encoded). **CARRY to the MIS-generation slice:** when a DATA_ENTRY_FIELD column resolves `data[key]` ‚Üí renders to Excel/CSV/MIS, that value MUST be output-encoded ‚Äî specifically CSV/Excel **formula-injection** (`=`/`+`/`-`/`@`/tab/CR leading char) must be neutralized. The platform `toCsv` export helper ALREADY neutralizes formula-injection (established in prior export audits) ‚Äî the generation slice MUST route DATA_ENTRY_FIELD values through that same sanitizer (or the xlsx equivalent), not a bespoke writer. Also any HTML/PDF render of `data[key]` must HTML-escape. Flagged forward, on the SAME line as slice-1's `source_ref`-resolution and APPLICANT_FIELD-PII carries.
  - (5) ‚úÖ **PII ‚Äî operator `data` may carry sampler/customer PII; it inherits the task scope + `data_entry.manage` gate, no broader exposure.** Read/write of `case_data_entries.data` is reachable ONLY through these two routes, both `data_entry.manage`-gated AND `taskScope`-guarded (per #1/#2) ‚Äî so a value containing PII (sampler name, customer field) is visible only to an office operator who BOTH holds the perm AND has the task in scope; identical audience to the task itself. `findByTask` runs only post-scope-check (never standalone). `created_by`/`updated_by` are staff uuids (audit). No `SELECT *`, no logging of `data`, no secrets in the module (scanned). No widening. (DPDP retention/consent for stored MIS PII is a data-lifecycle concern owned by the schema/retention track, not this slice.)
  - DISPOSITION: **PASS.** Office data-entry store slice: BOTH routes `data_entry.manage`-gated (default-deny intact; MANAGER/BACKEND_USER/SA only; TL/FA‚Üí403, CTO-proved); the task is `taskScope`-guarded on BOTH get AND save with the SAME predicate so an in-perm-but-out-of-scope MANAGER/BACKEND_USER gets 404-as-absent (IDOR-safe, no oracle, READ and WRITE); `taskId`+`data` bound only ($1, `$N::jsonb`+JSON.stringify), column_key allow-list is server-owned (layout-derived) and drops unknown keys (`bogus` test) ‚Äî zero injection, no `data` interpolation; OCC version-guarded; PII inherits the scope+perm gate (no broader exposure). Matches CTO live evidence (TL‚Üí403, absent‚Üí404, non-uuid‚Üí400). **SHOULD-FIX (non-blocking, test gap):** add an out-of-scope PUT‚Üí404 test (only the GET out-of-scope path is asserted; the write path is the same code but untested). **CARRIED forward to MIS-GENERATION slice (DON'T-REGRESS):** when DATA_ENTRY_FIELD resolves `data[key]`‚ÜíExcel/CSV/MIS, route the value through the existing formula-injection-neutralizing `toCsv`/xlsx sanitizer (operator-supplied raw values), and HTML-escape on any PDF/HTML render ‚Äî joins the slice-1 `source_ref`-resolution + APPLICANT_FIELD-PII carries.

- **2026-06-16 ¬∑ ADR-0037 MIS ENGINE SLICE 3 RE-GRAIN ‚Äî office data-entry per-TASK ‚Üí per-CASE (`caseDataEntries` module routes/controller/service/repository + new module-local `caseScopePredicate` + SDK `caseDataEntries.ts` + mig 0062 re-grains the table) ‚Äî STAGED (`git diff --cached`) ‚Äî VERDICT: PASS. No FLAG. No BLOCK.** Adversarial re-review of the grain change: `/tasks/:taskId`+`taskScope` ‚Üí `/cases/:caseId`+`caseScope`. The new scope leg is module-local (not the shared `taskScopePredicate`) ‚Äî reviewed paranoid for an IDOR/injection/oracle introduced by the swap.
  - (1) ‚úÖ **BOTH verbs scope-guard the CASE ‚Üí out-of-scope/absent ‚â° 404 (IDOR-safe, no existence oracle), READ and WRITE.** `caseScope` (repository.ts) runs `SELECT cs.id,cs.client_id,cs.product_id FROM cases cs WHERE cs.id=$1 ${pred?'AND ('+pred+')':''}` ‚Üí `rows[0] ?? null`. Service `get()` AND `save()` BOTH: `resolveScope(actor)` ‚Üí `repo.caseScope(caseId, scope)` ‚Üí `if(!c) throw AppError.notFound('CASE_NOT_FOUND')` BEFORE any layout load / `findByCase` / write (service.ts get:24-28, save:34-38). An in-perm-but-out-of-scope MANAGER/BACKEND_USER ‚Üí predicate excludes the row ‚Üí `null` ‚Üí **404 CASE_NOT_FOUND**, byte-identical to a truly-absent case ‚Üí no existence leak. The unscoped `findByCase`/`insert`/`update` are reached ONLY post-scope-pass, so they can never touch an out-of-scope case. Test asserts absent uuid‚Üí404 on GET and the SAME on PUT (`.../cases/0000‚Ä¶00ff` ‚Üí 404, test:"the PUT branch is scope-guarded the same way", caseDataEntries.api.test.ts). **NOTE the 3a SHOULD-FIX (out-of-scope WRITE untested) STILL stands** ‚Äî the test exercises absent-PUT‚Üí404 but not in-scope-perm + out-of-scope-case PUT‚Üí404; same code path as GET (service.ts save:36 == get:26), structurally guarded, non-blocking. Carry the same recommendation.
  - (2) ‚úÖ **`caseScopePredicate` is PARAMETERIZED ‚Äî `composeScopePredicate` pushes scope ids as bound `uuid[]`/typed-array placeholders; zero interpolation of scope values.** The new module-local `caseScopePredicate(params, scope)` (repository.ts) delegates to the shared `composeScopePredicate(params, scope, ph => `cs.created_by = ANY(${ph}) OR EXISTS(SELECT 1 FROM case_tasks ct WHERE ct.case_id=cs.id AND ct.assigned_to=ANY(${ph}))`)` ‚Äî the hierarchy `userIds` array is `params.push`ed ONCE and the placeholder `$N::uuid[]` is reused at BOTH `${ph}` sites (same bound array, correct). EXPAND/RESTRICT dimension legs come from the code-owned `dimensionDef` registry via `pushParam` (`= ANY(${pushParam(...)})`, all values bound ‚Äî verified dimensions.ts:50-94), RESTRICT fails CLOSED to `FALSE` on registry-skew. The predicate is then spliced as `AND (${pred})` where `pred` is composed ONLY of `$N` placeholders + server-literal column refs ‚Äî NO scope id ever reaches SQL text. This shape MIRRORS the proven `cases/repository.ts` hierarchy leg (created_by OR task-assigned) ‚Äî semantically identical case-grain visibility, just inlined module-local; not a weaker fork. SUPER_ADMIN / hierarchy-ALL ‚Üí `scope={}` ‚Üí `composeScopePredicate` returns `''` ‚Üí `pred` empty ‚Üí no `AND` clause (full visibility, intended). `findByCase`/`insert`/`update` bind `$1=caseId`, `$N::jsonb` data, `$=userId`, `$=version` ‚Äî all parameterized; `JSON.stringify(data)` bound, never concatenated.
  - (3) ‚úÖ **`:caseId` UUID-validated BEFORE the query ‚Äî no 22P02‚Üí500, no injection.** Service `get()` AND `save()` both `if(!UUID_RE.test(caseId)) throw AppError.badRequest('BAD_REQUEST',{param:'caseId'})` as the FIRST statement (service.ts:21,33) ‚Äî a non-uuid never reaches the `WHERE cs.id=$1` (uuid col) so no Postgres invalid-text-representation‚Üí500, and even if it did it's a bound param not interpolated. Test: `.../cases/not-a-uuid` ‚Üí 400. (`save` validates the body schema AFTER the uuid check but BEFORE scope ‚Äî order is fine; both are pre-DB-write 400s.)
  - (4) ‚úÖ **`data` jsonb param-bound + keys layout-filtered (no arbitrary-key write, no jsonb-path injection).** Unchanged from 3a, re-verified at case grain: insert binds `$3::jsonb`+`JSON.stringify(clean)`, update binds `$2::jsonb`+`JSON.stringify(clean)` (repository.ts) ‚Äî `data` NEVER interpolated. The allow-list (service.ts:39-46) iterates `layout.columns` (server-owned, from `findActiveByConfig(c.clientId,c.productId,'DATA_ENTRY')` where clientId/productId come from the SCOPE-VALIDATED `caseScope` row, NOT the request) and copies only `supplied[col.columnKey]` ‚Äî an unknown body key (`bogus:'drop me'`) is never indexed ‚Üí DROPPED (test asserts `entry.data` equals only the two layout keys, `bogus` absent). `columnKey` is a JS object index only, never SQL text (also `^[a-z0-9_]+$`-constrained at config time, slice-1). Required-column check (`isRequired` empty ‚Üí 400 DATA_ENTRY_REQUIRED) runs over server columns. No jsonb-path operator is built from user input ‚Äî the whole map goes in as one opaque `$N::jsonb` value.
  - (5) ‚úÖ **No mass-assignment ‚Äî closed `SaveDataEntrySchema`; `created_by`/`updated_by` from actor JWT, not body.** `SaveDataEntrySchema = z.object({ data: z.record(z.string(), z.unknown()), version: z.number().int().min(0).optional() })` (sdk/caseDataEntries.ts:18-21) ‚Äî plain z.object STRIPS unknowns, so a body carrying `caseId`/`layoutId`/`createdBy`/`version`(for insert)/`id` has those dropped, never assigned. `actor.userId` = `req.auth.userId` (controller.ts:6-9, fail-closed `if(!req.auth) throw unauthenticated()`) is passed to `repo.insert(..., actor.userId)` (bound `$4` ‚Üí both created_by AND updated_by) and `repo.update(..., actor.userId, ...)` (bound `$3`=updated_by) ‚Äî NEVER a body field. `layout.id` for insert comes from the server-loaded layout, not input. `version` is OCC: insert defaults v1 (DB), update reads expected via `requireVersion(input)` (‚Üí400 VERSION_REQUIRED if absent, occ.ts) bound to `AND version=$4`; stale‚Üí`AppError.stale(before)`‚Üí409. The mig `case_id` carries `uq_case_data_entries_case UNIQUE(case_id)` ‚Äî concurrent first-save ‚Üí 23505 ‚Üí 409 DATA_ENTRY_EXISTS (not a duplicate/overwrite). No client-settable server column.
  - (6) ‚úÖ **Perm gate on BOTH routes; role lacking `data_entry.manage` ‚Üí 403 (test-asserted).** routes.ts: GET `/cases/:caseId` AND PUT `/cases/:caseId` each `authorize(PERMISSIONS.DATA_ENTRY_MANAGE)`, no ungated route, behind global `authenticate()`+`enrichAuth()`. Grant set unchanged by the re-grain = MANAGER (permissions.ts:99) + BACKEND_USER (permissions.ts:121) + SA via `Object.values(PERMISSIONS)`; **TEAM_LEADER and FIELD_AGENT/KYC_VERIFIER hold NEITHER** ‚Üí 403. Test seeds `TL = authHeaderForRole('TEAM_LEADER')` with the comment "NO data_entry.manage" and asserts GET‚Üí403 (caseDataEntries.api.test.ts); PUT mounts byte-identical middleware (structurally guaranteed). Audience correct: office operators key the case's MIS fields; field agents do not. (Roles-parity gate covers DB‚Üîcode; mig 0062 is a TABLE re-grain only ‚Äî it does NOT touch `role_permissions`, so the 3a `data_entry.manage` seed from mig 0061 still stands; parity unaffected.)
  - (7) ‚úÖ **PII ‚Äî re-graining task‚ÜíCASE does NOT broaden exposure; the case is scope-gated IDENTICALLY to the cases module.** The new `caseScopePredicate` hierarchy leg (`cs.created_by=ANY(...) OR EXISTS task assigned_to=ANY(...)`) is the SAME case-visibility shape the `cases` module enforces ‚Äî so a data-entry value (sampler/customer field) is visible only to an operator who BOTH holds `data_entry.manage` AND can already see the case via the standard cases scope. No NEW data crosses a boundary: previously a per-task row required the task in scope; now a per-case row requires the case in scope, and case-visibility ‚äá task-visibility by design (you can see the case iff you created it or hold one of its tasks ‚Äî strictly the union the task path already implied). `findActiveByConfig` derives client/product from the scope-validated case (not the request). `created_by`/`updated_by` are staff uuids. No `SELECT *`, no logging of `data`, no secrets (scanned). No widening. (DPDP retention for stored MIS PII = data-lifecycle track, not this slice.) The MIS-GENERATION CSV/Excel formula-injection + HTML-escape carry from 3a (#4) still applies unchanged at case grain.
  - DISPOSITION: **PASS.** The per-task‚Üíper-case re-grain preserves every control: BOTH verbs scope-guard the case ‚Üí 404-as-absent (IDOR-safe, no oracle, READ + WRITE); the new module-local `caseScopePredicate` is fully parameterized through `composeScopePredicate` (scope ids bound as `$N::uuid[]`/typed arrays, single push reused across both `${ph}` sites, RESTRICT fail-closed) and is the same case-visibility shape as the proven `cases` module (not a weaker fork); `:caseId` UUID-validated before any query (no 22P02‚Üí500); `data` is one opaque `$N::jsonb`+JSON.stringify bind with a server-owned layout-key allow-list (unknown keys dropped, no jsonb-path injection); closed `SaveDataEntrySchema` + actor-JWT `created_by`/`updated_by` (no mass-assignment); BOTH routes gate `data_entry.manage` (TL‚Üí403 test-asserted); no PII broadened (case-scope ‚äá task-scope, gated identically to the cases module). Mig 0062 re-grains the table only (`uq(case_id)`, FK to cases/report_layouts) ‚Äî no role_permissions touch, parity intact. **SHOULD-FIX (non-blocking, CARRIED from 3a):** add an in-perm + out-of-scope-case **PUT**‚Üí404 test (only the absent-PUT and out-of-scope-GET paths are asserted; the in-scope-perm/out-of-scope-case WRITE path is the same code, structurally guarded, untested). **CARRIED forward (DON'T-REGRESS):** MIS-generation must route DATA_ENTRY `data[key]` through the formula-injection-neutralizing `toCsv`/xlsx sanitizer + HTML-escape on PDF/HTML render; the new module-local `caseScopePredicate` MUST stay in lockstep with the `cases` module's case-visibility shape if either changes (two copies of the hierarchy leg now exist ‚Äî drift would split list-visibility from data-entry reachability).

## 2026-06-16 ‚Äî CASE-DETAIL slice: pickup mig 0063 + per-case Pickup CRUD (`GET/PUT /data-entry/cases/:caseId/pickup`) + field-photos read (`GET /cases/:caseId/field-photos`) ‚Äî VERDICT: PASS (no BLOCK, no FLAG)

STAGED (`git diff --cached`). Two new surfaces on the case-detail page: (A) a fixed per-case office "Pickup Information" box (Zion NewDataQC) under `data_entry.manage`; (B) a read-only Field Photos card under `case.view` serving device FIELD_PHOTO attachments. Reviewed adversarially for IDOR, geo-PII leak, injection, mass-assignment, presigned-URL leak. All SQL re-read line-by-line; scope plumbing traced to `platform/scope`.

- (1) ‚úÖ **PICKUP ‚Äî BOTH verbs scope-guard the case ‚Üí out-of-scope/absent ‚â° 404 (IDOR-safe, READ + WRITE).** Service `getPickup` AND `savePickup` (caseDataEntries/service.ts) BOTH: `UUID_RE.test(caseId)` first (‚Üí400, no 22P02‚Üí500), then `resolveScope(actor)` ‚Üí `repo.caseScope(caseId, scope)` ‚Üí `if (!c) throw AppError.notFound('CASE_NOT_FOUND')` BEFORE any `pickupContext`/`findPickupByCase`/insert/update. The unscoped pickup CRUD repo fns (`pickupContext`/`findPickupByCase`/`insertPickup`/`updatePickup`, all keyed `case_id = $1` with NO inner scope leg) are reached ONLY post-`caseScope`-pass ‚Äî they can never touch an out-of-scope case. `caseScope` runs the SAME module-local `caseScopePredicate`‚Üí`composeScopePredicate` audited in the 2026-06-16 re-grain entry above (parameterized `$N::uuid[]`, RESTRICT fail-closed, same case-visibility shape as the `cases` module). **Test-PROVEN this session on live DB**: out-of-scope/absent caseId ‚Üí 404 on GET **and** PUT (`‚Ä¶/cases/0000‚Ä¶00ff/pickup` ‚Üí 404 both verbs in the request log); in-perm TL lacking `data_entry.manage` ‚Üí 403 (perm gate fires before scope). This is exactly the IDOR-safe posture I wanted to break ‚Äî both verbs guarded, no existence oracle. No IDOR.
- (2) ‚úÖ **PICKUP ‚Äî params bound, closed schema, no mass-assignment.** `SavePickupSchema = z.object({ pickupDate/reportedDate/visitDateTime: isoDateNullish, pickupTrigger/samplerName: z.string().trim().max(200).nullish(), version: z.number().int().min(0).optional() })` (sdk/caseDataEntries.ts:48-55) ‚Äî plain `z.object` STRIPS unknown keys (a body carrying `caseId`/`createdBy`/`id`/`version`-for-insert has them dropped). The service then field-maps ONLY the 5 known fields into `PickupInput` explicitly (`v.pickupDate ?? null`, ‚Ä¶) ‚Äî even if Zod ever passed an extra it would never reach SQL. `created_by`/`updated_by` come from `actor.userId` (JWT subject), bound (`$7` reused for both on insert; `$7`=updated_by on update) ‚Äî NEVER a body field. `version` is OCC (`requireVersion(input)`‚Üí400 if absent on update, bound `AND version=$8`). No client-settable server column. `.max(200)` matches the varchar(200) cap (over-long ‚Üí 400, not silent DB truncation). ISO-datetime validation (`.datetime()`) on the three timestamptz fields ‚Üí non-ISO ‚Üí 400, never a raw string into a tz col.
- (3) ‚úÖ **FIELD-PHOTOS ‚Äî `case.view` + scope EXISTS leg; cannot pull out-of-scope photos.** `GET /cases/:caseId/field-photos` gated `authorize(PERMISSIONS.CASE_VIEW)` (cases/routes.ts) ‚Äî same gate as the audited `listAttachments`. Service `listFieldPhotos` (cases/service.ts:432-436) is DOUBLE-gated: (i) `resolveScope` ‚Üí `repo.caseVisible(caseId, scope)` ‚Üí `if (!‚Ä¶ ) throw notFound('CASE_NOT_FOUND')` (the CASE must be reachable ‚Äî defense-in-depth), THEN (ii) `repo.listFieldPhotos(caseId, scope)` applies the shared `taskScopePredicate` as `AND EXISTS (SELECT 1 FROM case_tasks ct2 JOIN cases cs ‚Ä¶ WHERE ct2.id = ca.task_id AND ${pred})` (repository.ts:1352-1357). **Crucially, unlike `attachmentForAccess` there is NO `task_id IS NULL OR ‚Ä¶` escape branch** ‚Äî a FIELD_PHOTO whose `task_id` the actor can't reach is filtered out entirely. FIELD_PHOTOs always carry a `task_id` (device upload binds them to the field task, ADR-0034 / mig 0055), so the EXISTS leg always governs. Net reachability = (case in scope) ‚àß (photo's task in scope) ‚Äî strictly tighter than `case.view` alone. Tried to find a leak: a user assigned to task-B of a multi-task case who tries to see task-A's photos ‚Äî the `caseVisible` precondition lets them in (they hold a task on the case), but the per-photo EXISTS leg still requires task-A be in *their* scope; under the union-visibility model (created-the-case OR assigned-a-task) a case-creator/manager sees all, a single-task assignee sees photos on tasks they can reach. This matches the audited `listAttachments` posture exactly. No IDOR.
- (4) ‚úÖ/‚öÝÔ∏è **PII ‚Äî field-photo `geoLocation` exposure is ACCEPTABLE under `case.view` (same tier as the case), NOT a leak ‚Äî but flagged for an explicit product call.** `listFieldPhotos` returns `ca.geo_location AS "geoLocation"` ({latitude,longitude,accuracy}) alongside the photo metadata. ADVERSARIAL take: geo is location-PII (where the field agent stood when capturing). BUT ‚Äî (a) it is the *agent's own capture coordinate* embedded in the verification evidence, not a third party's; (b) it is gated identically to every other case datum (`case.view` + the SAME case-scope ‚àß task-scope reachability as the photo itself), so anyone who can see the photo can already see the case it documents; (c) the audience is the office/backend/assigned-verifier set that owns the verification ‚Äî the legitimate consumers of "was the agent actually at the address". Exposing geo to that exact audience is the *point* of geo-tagging (anti-fraud). So: **PASS ‚Äî geo at `case.view` tier is acceptable**, consistent with the watermark/geo model already shipped on the device side. **SHOULD-FIX (non-blocking, owner product-call):** if geo is ever deemed more sensitive than the rest of the case (e.g. a future external/client-portal `case.view` audience), the geo field should be split behind a narrower perm than the photo metadata; today the audience is internal staff only, so no split is needed. Recorded so a future audience-widening doesn't silently carry geo with it.
- (5) ‚úÖ **PRESIGNED-URL ‚Äî image bytes never returned inline; served via the existing scope-guarded short-lived URL.** `listFieldPhotos` returns ONLY metadata (id/taskId/unitName/photoType/originalName/geoLocation/createdAt) ‚Äî NO `storage_key`, NO bytes, NO URL. The image is fetched lazily through the existing `GET /cases/:id/attachments/:attachmentId/url` route (cases/routes.ts:53, gated `case.view`), which calls `attachmentForAccess(caseId, attachmentId, scope)` ‚Äî bound to `ca.id=$1 AND ca.case_id=$2 AND deleted_at IS NULL` + the scope task-leg, ‚Üí null ‚Üí 404 (IDOR-safe), then mints `getStorage().signedUrl(storageKey)` with `expiresIn: env.S3_SIGNED_URL_TTL_S` (storage/index.ts:104-107) ‚Äî a configurable short TTL, scope RE-CHECKED at mint time. Serving a FIELD_PHOTO via this kind-agnostic route is still scope-safe: the route never trusts `kind`, it re-applies the case_id+task-scope guard, so there's no way to mint a URL for a photo on an out-of-scope task. The presigned URL is the only thing the client ever sees of object storage; it expires; no long-lived/leakable handle. No leak.
- DISPOSITION: **PASS.** No BLOCK, no FLAG. Pickup: BOTH verbs scope-guard the case ‚Üí 404-as-absent (IDOR-safe READ+WRITE, test-proven live), closed `SavePickupSchema` + actor-JWT `created_by`/`updated_by` (no mass-assignment), all params bound (no interpolation), UNIQUE(case_id) serializes racing first-saves (23505‚Üí409 PICKUP_EXISTS), OCC version guarded (400/409), `:caseId` UUID-checked pre-query, `.max(200)`/ISO-datetime validation matches the column types, `data_entry.manage` gate (TL‚Üí403 test-proven). Field-photos: `case.view` + DOUBLE guard (`caseVisible` precondition ‚àß per-photo `taskScopePredicate` EXISTS leg with NO null-escape) = strictly tighter than the audited `listAttachments`, metadata-only response, images via the scope-re-checked short-lived presigned route; geo-PII at `case.view` tier is acceptable (agent's own evidence coordinate, internal-staff audience, gated identically to the case). **SHOULD-FIX (non-blocking):** (i) add a direct field-photos test (out-of-scope task photo NOT returned for an in-case single-task assignee; out-of-scope case ‚Üí 404) ‚Äî the read is structurally identical to the proven `listAttachments` but has no dedicated negative test; (ii) carry the in-perm/out-of-scope-case **PUT** pickup‚Üí404 test from the 3a/re-grain SHOULD-FIX (same code path, structurally guarded, untested). **DON'T-REGRESS:** the field-photos read MUST keep the no-`task_id IS NULL`-escape EXISTS leg (FIELD_PHOTOs are always task-bound; a future null-escape would leak task-less photos case-wide); if geo's audience ever widens beyond internal staff, split geo behind a narrower perm than the photo metadata.

## 2026-06-16 ‚Äî FIELD_REPORT engine SLICE 1 (ADR-0039): render an admin-authored Handlebars template against a task's device form_data + case/applicant context (`GET /api/v2/cases/:id/tasks/:taskId/field-report`; new `modules/fieldReports/{repository,render,service,controller}.ts` + route on `cases/routes.ts:49`) ‚Äî VERDICT: PASS (no BLOCK, no FLAG)

UNCOMMITTED. New read-only render endpoint. Reviewed adversarially for IDOR/cross-case isolation, SQL injection, server-side template injection (SSTI) + prototype-pollution via the admin `templateBody`, json-path traversal, and PII/DPDP. All SQL re-read line-by-line; render path traced through Handlebars runtime options.

- (1) ‚úÖ **RBAC default-deny + scope ‚Üí out-of-scope/absent/cross-case ‚â° 404 (IDOR-safe, no existence oracle).** Route gated `authorize(PERMISSIONS.CASE_VIEW)` (cases/routes.ts:51) ‚Äî same gate as every other case read (attachments/field-photos/verdict-history), behind the global authenticate+enrichAuth. Service (service.ts:18-23): `UUID_RE.test(caseId)` AND `UUID_RE.test(taskId)` FIRST (‚Üí400 BAD_REQUEST, no 22P02‚Üí500), then `resolveScope(actor)` ‚Üí `repo.loadContext(caseId, taskId, scope)` ‚Üí `if (!ctx) throw notFound('TASK_NOT_FOUND')` BEFORE any layout load / render. `loadContext` (repository.ts:44-99) keys the read `WHERE ct.id = $1 AND ct.case_id = $2 ${pred?'AND ('+pred+')':''}` with `params=[taskId, caseId]` ‚Äî so **cross-case isolation is enforced**: a real taskId under a *different* caseId fails `ct.case_id = $2` ‚Üí 0 rows ‚Üí `rows[0]?.ctx ?? null` ‚Üí 404, byte-identical to absent. An in-perm-but-out-of-scope MANAGER/BACKEND_USER/FIELD_AGENT ‚Üí `caseScopePredicate` excludes the row ‚Üí null ‚Üí 404. No 403, no leak, no oracle. IDOR-safe on BOTH the task identity AND the case binding.
- (2) ‚úÖ **`caseScopePredicate` is the proven shared shape, fully parameterized ‚Äî alias-disambiguated correctly.** The module-local `caseScopePredicate` (repository.ts:25-33) delegates to the shared `composeScopePredicate(params, scope, ph => `cs.created_by = ANY(${ph}) OR EXISTS (SELECT 1 FROM case_tasks ct2 WHERE ct2.case_id = cs.id AND ct2.assigned_to = ANY(${ph}))`)` ‚Äî the SAME case-visibility shape as `cases/repository.ts:187` (created-the-case OR assigned-a-task), audited PASS in the 2026-06-16 re-grain + case-detail entries. **Alias check (the subtle bit):** the OUTER query aliases `case_tasks ct` (repository.ts:89), so the EXISTS subquery uses `ct2` to avoid shadowing the outer row ‚Äî correct disambiguation (the cases-module copy uses `ct` because its outer FROM is `cases cs` with no `ct`). Scope ids are `params.push`ed as bound `$N::uuid[]` (composeScopePredicate:51-52), reused at both `${ph}` sites; EXPAND/RESTRICT legs come from the code-owned dimension registry (all `= ANY($N)` bound), RESTRICT fails CLOSED to FALSE on registry skew. SUPER_ADMIN / hierarchy-ALL ‚Üí scope empty ‚Üí `pred=''` ‚Üí no AND clause (full visibility, intended). NO scope value reaches SQL text.
- (3) ‚úÖ **SQL injection ‚Äî every value bound; the ONLY request-derived strings are UUID-regex-gated before the query; `verificationType`/`source_ref` never reach SQL text.** `loadContext` binds `$1=taskId` (uuid-regex-validated), `$2=caseId` (uuid-regex-validated) + the scope placeholders ‚Äî no `${}` of any request data. The `json_build_object` KEYS (taskId/clientId/.../applicant.pan/calling_code) are **server-side string literals** in the query source, NOT user input ‚Äî they label the output JSON; none is request-derived. `findActiveByConfig` (reportLayouts/repository.ts:152-169) binds `$1=clientId`, `$2=productId`, `$3=kind`, and ‚Äî critically ‚Äî `verificationType` is `params.push`ed and matched as `AND verification_type = $N` (line 161-162), NOT interpolated; and that `verificationType` value originates from `vu.code` (a DB column read in loadContext, line 51), never from the request. The `source_ref` (FORM_DATA_PATH/TASK_FIELD/...) NEVER touches SQL at all ‚Äî it is resolved in JS (render.ts, see #4). Zero request string reaches SQL text anywhere in the slice.
- (4) ‚úÖ **Json-path / catalog-ref resolution is plain property access in JS ‚Äî NO eval, NO interpolation, NO jsonb-path operator built from input.** `walkPath` (render.ts:23-31) splits `source_ref` on `.` and does `cur = (cur as Record)[seg]` with a `typeof !== 'object'` guard each hop ‚Äî pure bracket indexing into the already-loaded `formData` object, never `eval`/`Function`/template-string, never a Postgres jsonb path. `resolveColumnValue` (render.ts:35-49) switches on `sourceType` and indexes the fixed in-memory `ctx.task[ref]`/`ctx.case[ref]`/`ctx.applicant[ref]` (server-loaded objects) by the catalog ref; an unknown ref just yields `undefined`‚Üí`''`. `formData` came back as one `$N`-free jsonb column (`ct.form_data`) inside the server-built `json_build_object` ‚Äî it is data, not SQL. The catalog `source_ref` is config-time constrained: FIXED sources validate `ref ‚àà catalog.fields` (sdk/reportLayouts.ts:115-117); FORM_DATA_PATH is FREE but `.max(200)` (sdk:182) and only ever used as a JS dot-path. No traversal-to-SQL, no path injection.
- (5) ‚úÖ **TEMPLATE INJECTION (SSTI) + prototype pollution ‚Äî output-encoded, proto-blocked, isolated instance; residual risk is SUPER_ADMIN-only and LOW.** `renderNarrative` (render.ts:73-86): (a) **output-encoding** ‚Äî uses `Handlebars` default `{{var}}` which **HTML-escapes** every value (`& < > " ' \``); a malicious `form_data` value (device-supplied, the only untrusted DATA here) is escaped, so even though slice-1's S2 carry says the FE renders `narrative` ‚Äî see #6 ‚Äî the rendered string already has HTML metachars neutralized. (b) **prototype access BLOCKED** ‚Äî `compiled(data, { allowProtoPropertiesByDefault: false, allowProtoMethodsByDefault: false })` (render.ts:81-84) disables Handlebars' proto-property/method access (the documented Handlebars RCE vector, e.g. `{{constructor.constructor ...}}` / `lookup`-to-proto), and the context `data` is a plain object built by `buildContext` (own enumerable keys only). (c) **isolated instance** ‚Äî `Handlebars.create()` (render.ts:13) gives a private registry; only one custom helper `eq` (pure `a===b` comparison, no I/O, no proto walk) is registered ‚Äî no `log`/file/require/exec helper, no `helperMissing` override that could reach globals. (d) **template SOURCE is admin-authored** ‚Äî `templateBody` is settable ONLY via the report-layout create/update path gated by the layout-manage perm (SUPER_ADMIN tier); a field agent / backend user CANNOT author a template. **Residual:** a malicious *template author* is by definition a SUPER_ADMIN who already holds every permission ‚Äî SSTI by that actor grants nothing they lack; the proto guard + escaped output still contain a careless template. `templateBody` capped `.max(20_000)` (sdk:265) bounds render cost (no unbounded-recursion DoS vector via a giant body). LOW residual, accepted.
- (6) ‚úÖ **XSS / S2 carry ‚Äî response is `res.json(...)`; `narrative` is HTML-escaped server-side; the FE render surface is the only place to re-confirm.** Controller does `res.json(await svc.render(...))` (controller.ts:17) ‚Äî `application/json`, inherently encoded on the wire, no HTML render server-side. The `FieldReportView` returns ONLY `{taskId, verificationType, layoutId, layoutName, narrative}` ‚Äî the raw render context (form_data, applicant PII fields) is NOT echoed; only the admin-template-shaped, HTML-escaped `narrative` string. `cleanWhitespace` (render.ts:64-69) only collapses spaces/newlines ‚Äî it does NOT decode entities, so the escaping survives. **S2 (carried, FE concern):** if the FE injects `narrative` via `dangerouslySetInnerHTML`/`v-html`, the Handlebars HTML-escape already neutralizes device-supplied metachars, but the FE SHOULD still render it as text (it is a plain narrative). No server-side XSS vector here; FE render path is the residual to confirm in the FE slice.
- (7) ‚úÖ/‚öÝÔ∏è **PII/DPDP ‚Äî APPLICANT_FIELD (name/mobile/pan/calling_code) + case backend_contact_number inherit `case.view` + case-scope; internal-staff audience, ACCEPTABLE, not a leak ‚Äî flagged for the same audience-widening watch as field-photos geo.** The `applicant` json block (repository.ts:81-87) exposes `ca.name/mobile/pan/applicant_type/calling_code` and the `case` block exposes `cs.backend_contact_number` (repository.ts:75) ‚Äî these are customer/applicant PII (mobile + PAN are DPDP-sensitive identifiers). ADVERSARIAL take: PAN is a strong identifier. BUT ‚Äî (a) they surface ONLY through the admin template's chosen columns AND only inside the rendered narrative (not as a raw context dump); (b) gated identically to the case itself (`case.view` + the SAME case-scope reachability), so anyone who can render the report can already see the applicant on the case-detail page (`CASE_VIEW_SELECT` already exposes primary_name/primary_mobile/primary_pan ‚Äî audited prior); (c) the audience is internal staff (office/backend/assigned verifier/field agent on the case) ‚Äî the legitimate consumers of the verification narrative. So **PASS ‚Äî applicant PII at `case.view` tier is acceptable, no broadened exposure vs the existing case-detail read.** **SHOULD-FIX (non-blocking, owner product-call):** if `case.view` ever extends to an external/client-portal audience, the applicant PAN/mobile in the narrative must be re-evaluated (and likely masked) ‚Äî today internal-staff only, so no masking needed. Same audience-widening watch recorded for field-photos geo (2026-06-16 case-detail entry).
- DISPOSITION: **PASS.** No BLOCK, no FLAG. Render endpoint: `case.view`-gated + scope-guarded with the proven shared case-visibility predicate (alias-disambiguated `ct2`), keyed `ct.id=$1 AND ct.case_id=$2 [+scope]` ‚Üí out-of-scope/absent/**cross-case** all collapse to 404 (IDOR-safe, no oracle); UUIDs regex-validated pre-query (no 22P02‚Üí500); every SQL value bound, `verificationType` bound + DB-sourced (`vu.code`), `json_build_object` keys are server literals, `source_ref` resolved purely in JS via `walkPath` bracket-indexing (no eval/no SQL/no jsonb-path); Handlebars default HTML-escapes data values + `allowProtoPropertiesByDefault:false`/`allowProtoMethodsByDefault:false` on an isolated `Handlebars.create()` instance with one pure `eq` helper (SSTI/proto-pollution contained; residual is SUPER_ADMIN-author-only = LOW); response is metadata + escaped narrative only (no raw-context echo); applicant PII inherits case.view+scope (internal-staff audience, no broadening). **SHOULD-FIX (non-blocking):** (i) add negative tests ‚Äî cross-case taskId (real task under wrong caseId)‚Üí404, out-of-scope-case‚Üí404, non-uuid‚Üí400, malicious `templateBody` with `{{constructor‚Ä¶}}`/proto-walk‚Üírenders inert (proves the proto guard), device `form_data` value with `<script>`‚ÜíHTML-escaped in narrative; (ii) the FE field-report card MUST render `narrative` as TEXT (not raw HTML) ‚Äî confirm in the FE slice. **DON'T-REGRESS:** keep `allowProtoPropertiesByDefault:false`+`allowProtoMethodsByDefault:false` on every render call and NEVER register a Handlebars helper that does I/O / reaches globals / walks proto; the module-local `caseScopePredicate` MUST stay in lockstep with the cases-module case-visibility shape (third copy of the hierarchy leg now exists ‚Äî drift would split report reachability from case visibility); if `case.view` audience ever widens beyond internal staff, mask applicant PAN/mobile (+ backend_contact_number) in the narrative.

- **2026-06-16 ¬∑ Slice S2a ‚Äî `FieldReportView.sections` (RAW device-submitted fields surfaced to FE; `fieldReports/sections.ts` + service + CaseDetailPage). VERDICT: PASS.** This slice surfaces the agent's RAW submitted `form_data` values (UNTRUSTED, device-supplied) ‚Äî the prior narrative was Handlebars-HTML-escaped server-side, but `sections` values are RAW strings, so the output-encoding burden moves to the FE. Resolves the S1 SHOULD-FIX-(ii) FE-render confirmation for the raw fields too.
  - (1) ‚úÖ **XSS / output-encoding ‚Äî FE renders `sections` AND `narrative` as React TEXT CHILDREN (auto-escaped), NO `dangerouslySetInnerHTML`.** Grepped `dangerouslySetInnerHTML` across `CaseDetailPage.tsx` ‚Üí NONE (whole file). Field values flow `report.sections[].fields[]` ‚Üí `<Meta label={f.label} value={f.value}>` (CaseDetailPage.tsx:1532) ‚Üí `<div>{value}</div>` / `<div>{label}</div>` (Meta, :1670-1671) ‚Äî JSX `{value}` is a text child, React auto-escapes; a device value like `<script>` / `<img onerror>` renders inert as literal text. Section titles `{section.title}` (:1527) and narrative `<p ‚Ä¶>{report.narrative}</p>` (:1505) are likewise text children. `whitespace-pre-wrap` is CSS only (no HTML parse). **No XSS sink in the slice.** Server side: `res.json(...)`, JSON-encoded on the wire, no HTML render. ‚úÖ
  - (2) ‚úÖ **No new data source / no sensitive leak beyond what `case.view` already grants.** `buildSections(ctx.formData)` (service.ts:27) reads ONLY `ctx.formData` ‚Äî the SAME already-loaded, scope-guarded blob the render path consumes; NO new query, NO new column, NO new join. `sections.ts` explicitly SKIPS bulky/system keys (`photos|attachments|attachmentids|geolocation|metadata|formdata`, SKIP_KEYS :16) and DROPS nested objects (toValue returns null on objects, :39) ‚Äî so it surfaces only the agent's flat keyed answers + `verificationOutcome`, strictly a SUBSET of the form_data already gated behind `case.view`+case-scope. Geolocation is deliberately NOT surfaced (consistent with the field-photos geo audience-watch). No PII broadening vs the existing case-detail read. ‚úÖ
  - (3) ‚úÖ **Scope guard NOT bypassed ‚Äî sections inherit S1's IDOR-safe 404.** `sections` are built AFTER `repo.loadContext(caseId,taskId,scope)` returns a non-null `ctx` (the unchanged S1 path: cross-case/out-of-scope/absent ‚Üí null ‚Üí 404 BEFORE buildSections is ever reached). `buildSections` takes no caseId/taskId/scope and issues no query ‚Äî it cannot reach a row the scope predicate excluded. Endpoint still `case.view` + UUID-regex-gated (unchanged). ‚úÖ
  - (4) ‚úÖ **No ReDoS in the `toLabel` regexes on attacker-controlled keys.** Device-controlled `form_data` KEYS reach `toLabel(key)` (sections.ts:19) and slug‚Üí`toLabel(slug)` (:68). The three regexes are all LINEAR / backtracking-free: `/_/g` (literal), `/([a-z0-9])([A-Z])/g` and `/([A-Z]+)([A-Z][a-z])/g` ‚Äî `[A-Z]+` is a single bounded quantifier with disjoint following classes (`[A-Z][a-z]`), no nested/overlapping quantifier, no catastrophic-backtracking shape (no `(a+)+`/`(a|a)*`). `.split(/\s+/)` is linear. Worst case is O(n) in key length; keys are bounded by the device blob size. No ReDoS. (Belt-and-suspenders: a per-key length cap would bound cost further but is not needed.) ‚úÖ
  - DISPOSITION: **PASS.** No BLOCK, no FLAG. Raw device values surfaced but FE renders them as auto-escaped React text (no dangerouslySetInnerHTML anywhere in CaseDetailPage); `buildSections` reads only the already-scope-loaded `ctx.formData` (no new source/column/join, skips geo+bulky keys), built after the S1 404 scope-gate so no bypass; `toLabel` regexes are linear (no ReDoS). **DON'T-REGRESS:** keep the field-report FE rendering `sections`/`narrative` as TEXT children ‚Äî NEVER pipe a device-submitted `sections` value (or the narrative) through `dangerouslySetInnerHTML`; keep `buildSections` sourced ONLY from the scope-loaded `ctx.formData` (never re-query by id inside it); keep the SKIP_KEYS geo/photo/metadata exclusions so the raw view can't leak geolocation or grow past the case.view audience; if `toLabel` ever gains a backreference/nested-quantifier regex, re-check for ReDoS.

- **2026-06-16 ¬∑ ADR-0039 SLICE S3a ‚Äî FIELD_REPORT render flipped to PLAIN TEXT (`noEscape:true`) + new grammar-helper library (`helpers.ts`) + SKIP_KEYS widened ‚Äî `git diff HEAD` ‚Äî VERDICT: PASS. No FLAG. No BLOCK.** This is the security-critical re-review of the change that REMOVES Handlebars HTML-escaping (the thing S1 partly leaned on). New model: **plain-text-at-engine + escape-at-consumer** ‚Äî engine emits the raw value verbatim (must match v1 System A literal output, e.g. `shows the name "X"`, not `&quot;`), and XSS-safety moves to the rendering sink. Reviewed paranoid for an XSS/injection hole opened by dropping the engine-level encode.
  - (1) ‚úÖ **OUTPUT-ENCODING CHAIN INTACT ‚Äî sole consumer is a React TEXT node, auto-escaped at the DOM layer.** Producer = `service.ts:52 renderNarrative(...)` ‚Üí JSON on `GET /cases/:id/tasks/:taskId/field-report` (cases/routes.ts:48-52, `authorize(CASE_VIEW)` read-only). Only web consumer = `CaseDetailPage.tsx:1545` `<p className="whitespace-pre-wrap text-sm text-foreground">{report.narrative}</p>` ‚Äî a JSX text child, NOT `dangerouslySetInnerHTML`. `grep -rn '.narrative' acs-web-v2/src` = 3 hits, all in that one #6 card; `grep dangerouslySetInnerHTML ... narrative` = none. So a device-submitted `<script>x</script>` lands in the DOM as inert text (React escapes `<`/`>`/`&`/`"` at render). **render.test.ts:108 asserts the engine itself returns `Note: <script>x</script>` verbatim** (entities NOT introduced) ‚Äî the model is intentional and tested. NO PDF/Word/HTML/email sink consumes `narrative` today (`grep -rni narrative acs-api-v2/src` = only render/repo/service/route/controller). XSS-safe.
  - (2) ‚úÖ **plain-text-at-engine + escape-at-consumer is the CORRECT model** and matches v1 System A (plain-text/regex `TemplateReportService`, no escaping; v1's PDF was a SEPARATE HTML engine). The render.ts comment (render.ts:69-71) records the contract correctly.
  - üö® **DON'T-REGRESS (S5 ‚Äî HARD GATE):** the narrative is now RAW untrusted device text. **Any S5 PDF/Word/HTML/email renderer MUST output-encode `narrative` (and any raw `sections` value) for ITS sink context** ‚Äî HTML-escape before an HTML/PDF-from-HTML template, XML-escape for .docx runs. Do NOT drop the raw narrative into an HTML string sink or `dangerouslySetInnerHTML`/`innerHTML`. The engine deliberately no longer escapes; the encode is the sink's job. A new sink that interpolates `narrative` into markup without encoding = stored XSS / content injection ‚Äî BLOCK-level. (Extends the 2026-06-16 prior entry's text-children DON'T-REGRESS to cover the now-removed engine escape.)
  - (3) ‚úÖ **Template injection still bounded.** `template_body` stays admin-authored (SUPER_ADMIN / `report_template.manage`). `noEscape` only changes value output-encoding ‚Äî it does NOT enable proto access: `hb.compile(...,{noEscape,strict:false})` + run-time `allowProtoPropertiesByDefault:false`/`allowProtoMethodsByDefault:false` retained (render.ts:74-78); `walkPath` unchanged (plain property access, no eval/interp). The new helpers (helpers.ts) are **pure string transforms** ‚Äî none call `require`/`eval`/`Function`/I/O/timers or walk the prototype chain. `str()` coerces `null`/objects‚Üí`''` (so the Handlebars trailing `options` object stringifies to `''`, the optional-arg-safety trick), `Number()` paths guard via `isFinite`/`isNaN`. `default` (`defaultHelper`) and `eq` are pure (`eq` only branches `options.fn`/`inverse`). Safe.
  - (4) ‚úÖ **No ReDoS.** All new regexes are linear / no nested or overlapping quantifiers under a quantifier: `pluralize` `^(\d+(?:\.\d+)?)\s+(year|month|day|week)s?$` (anchored, `\d+`/`\s+` non-overlapping, fixed alternation), `date` `^\d{4}-\d{2}-\d{2}$` + `^(\d{4}-\d{2}-\d{2})` (fixed counts), `ownershipType` `^(Are|Is)\s+` (anchored), the various `^sighted`/`^not sighted` literal prefixes. Bounded on attacker-controlled values.
  - (5) ‚úÖ **SKIP_KEYS extension only WIDENS what `buildSections` hides** (+formtype/submissionid/submittedat/submittedby/verification/verificationimages) ‚Äî strictly reduces the raw-field surface, introduces no new exposure; still sourced only from scope-loaded `ctx.formData`.
  - GATE: targeted suite green ‚Äî helpers.test.ts 14 ‚úì, render.test.ts 7 ‚úì (incl. the noEscape/raw-`<script>` parity assertion), sections.test.ts 5 ‚úì (3 api tests skipped by design). Browser-verified per brief: #6 renders literal quotes, hasEntities=false, 0 console errors. `pnpm verify` green modulo the documented auth-lockout rotating flake (passes isolated).

- **2026-06-17 ¬∑ S4 Slice A ‚Äî field-photo on-view reverse-geocode endpoint + migration 0065 (`GET /cases/:id/field-photos/:attachmentId/address`; `reverse_geocoded_address` col + freeze trigger + geo CHECK + `reverse_geocode_dlq`) ‚Äî `git diff bb0e1d1` ‚Äî VERDICT: PASS. No FLAG. No BLOCK.** New endpoint reverse-geocodes ONE field photo's GPS via Google (server-side) and persists a frozen address. Audited adversarially across all 5 brief dimensions; all controls hold.
  - (1) ‚úÖ **RBAC + scope (IDOR) ‚Äî out-of-scope / cross-case / unknown attachmentId all collapse to 404, no 403 oracle.** Route gated `authorize(PERMISSIONS.CASE_VIEW)` (routes.ts:50) ‚Äî same gate as `GET /:id/field-photos` and every other case read; behind global authenticate. Service (service.ts:445-460): `resolveScope(actor)` ‚Üí `repo.fieldPhotoForGeocode(caseId, attachmentId, scope)` ‚Üí `if (!row) throw notFound('FIELD_PHOTO_NOT_FOUND')` BEFORE any geocode. Repo WHERE (repository.ts:1431) keys `ca.id = $1 AND ca.case_id = $2 AND ca.kind = 'FIELD_PHOTO' AND ca.deleted_at IS NULL ${taskLeg}` with `params=[attachmentId, caseId]`. **Cross-case isolation enforced** by `ca.case_id = $2` ‚Äî a real attachmentId under a *different* caseId fails the bind ‚Üí 0 rows ‚Üí `rows[0] ?? null` ‚Üí 404, byte-identical to absent. The scope leg (repository.ts:1418-1426) uses `taskScopePredicate` and is wired correctly for the photo grain: `AND (ca.task_id IS NULL OR EXISTS (SELECT 1 FROM case_tasks ct JOIN cases cs ON cs.id=ct.case_id WHERE ct.id=ca.task_id AND ${pred}))` ‚Äî an out-of-scope MGR/BE/FE whose `taskScopePredicate` excludes the owning task ‚Üí EXISTS false ‚Üí row excluded ‚Üí null ‚Üí 404. RESTRICT legs fail CLOSED to FALSE on registry skew (composeScopePredicate:62-64); SUPER_ADMIN/hierarchy-ALL ‚Üí `pred=''` ‚Üí no leg (full visibility, intended). No 403, no existence oracle. Integration test asserts unknown attachmentId ‚Üí 404 (cases.api.test.ts:2250-2256). ‚úÖ
  - (2) ‚úÖ **`kind='FIELD_PHOTO'` hard-pins the surface ‚Äî OFFICE_REF docs unreachable.** Both the read (`fieldPhotoForGeocode`, repository.ts:1431) and the write-through (`setFieldPhotoReverseGeocodedAddress`, repository.ts:1442) carry `AND kind = 'FIELD_PHOTO'`. An office reference document (kind=OFFICE_REF) can never be resolved or have an address written here even with a valid uuid ‚Äî reverse-geocode is a field-photo-only concern (ADR-0040). ‚úÖ
  - (3) ‚úÖ **PII / DPDP ‚Äî GPS coord + resolved street address inherit `case.view` + case+task scope; NO key leakage to client; coords stay server-side, not in logs/URLs beyond the existing geocode seam.** The lat/lng (device-supplied, stored at upload in `geo_location`) and the Google `formatted_address` are personal data, gated identically to the case (only users who can see the case + are in task scope reach the row). **Server key never leaves the server:** the Google call is built in `platform/geocode/index.ts:createGoogleGeocoder` (`?latlng=${lat},${lng}&key=${encodeURIComponent(apiKey)}`) ‚Äî server-side `fetch`, the key read from `env.GOOGLE_GEOCODING_API_KEY` (ADR-0040 server-only). The device/client never sees the key; the API response to the browser is only `{address, cached}` (service.ts:455-459 / `ReverseGeocodeResult`) ‚Äî coords are NOT echoed, the URL-with-key is NEVER returned. Diff scan: zero `console.*`, zero `GOOGLE_`/`apiKey`/`secret` strings in the diff. The only log on the geocode path is `logger.warn('reverse geocode failed', { error: <message> })` (index.ts) ‚Äî logs the error *message* only, NOT the URL, NOT the key, NOT the coords. No new PII-in-logs/URL surface beyond the pre-existing seam. ‚úÖ
  - (4) ‚úÖ **Injection ‚Äî every value bound; the only request-derived strings are UUID-gated pre-query.** `caseId`/`attachmentId` come via `parseUuidParam` (controller.ts:9-13): `UUID_RE.test(v)` else 400 BAD_REQUEST (no 22P02‚Üí500), then bound as `$1`/`$2`. lat/lng are read from the `geo_location` jsonb as numbers and only ever passed to `geocodeService.reverse` (typed `number`, range-validated `|lat|<=90 |lng|<=180`, NaN-rejected ‚Üí `INVALID_COORDINATES`) ‚Äî never interpolated into SQL. The address write binds `$2=address` (repository.ts:1440-1443). `kind='FIELD_PHOTO'` is a server literal. NO `${}` of request data in any SQL; the only interpolated fragment is `${taskLeg}`/`${pred}`, both server-composed from the code-owned dimension registry with all scope ids `params.push`ed as bound `$N::uuid[]`. The migration's geo CHECK uses `jsonb ?`/`jsonb_typeof` operators (no dynamic SQL). ‚úÖ
  - (5) ‚úÖ **Evidence integrity ‚Äî address immutable at the DB (freeze trigger), app write is NULL-guarded, NO overwrite path exists.** Migration 0065 `BEFORE UPDATE` trigger `case_attachments_freeze_geocoded_address()` (0065:33-50) RAISEs if `OLD.reverse_geocoded_address IS NOT NULL AND NEW IS DISTINCT FROM OLD` ‚Äî exactly one NULL‚Üíaddress transition is permitted; any later rewrite (address‚Üídifferent OR address‚ÜíNULL) is blocked at the DB regardless of caller. The app write `setFieldPhotoReverseGeocodedAddress` (repository.ts:1438-1448) additionally guards `WHERE ‚Ä¶ reverse_geocoded_address IS NULL` (no-op on an already-set row) then re-reads the current value, so a concurrent race returns the frozen winner rather than the loser's value (service returns that read-back, service.ts:457). The geocode_cache itself is write-once (`ON CONFLICT (lat,lng) DO NOTHING`, geocode/repository.ts:17-20). **Grepped: `reverse_geocoded_address` is SET only at repository.ts:1442** ‚Äî no other UPDATE path touches it; the trigger backstops even a future stray write. Test proves it: first view persists `12 MG ROAD‚Ä¶`; a later geocoder returning `SOMEWHERE ELSE` does NOT change the frozen value (cached early-return, cases.api.test.ts:2207-2227). ‚úÖ
  - (6) ‚úÖ **DoS / abuse ‚Äî bounded; no unbounded amplification.** Per unresolved photo, one view triggers at most ONE Google call, and only after a cache miss: cache-first via `geocode_cache` keyed on 6-dp rounded coords (geocodeService.reverse: `getCached(rlat,rlng)` hit ‚Üí early return, no Google call). A frozen/cached address short-circuits in the service BEFORE the geocoder (service.ts:450 `if (row.address) return ‚Ä¶cached:true`). No-coords ‚Üí returns null WITHOUT calling Google (service.ts:453-454; test cases.api.test.ts:2236-2247 asserts the geocoder is never invoked). The Google call has a hard 5s `AbortController` timeout + null-degrade (index.ts `GEOCODE_TIMEOUT_MS=5000`); failures are not cached (self-heal) and not retried inline (BullMQ/DLQ owns retries). Amplification ceiling = (unresolved field photos a viewer can see) √ó 1, and each resolved photo permanently caches ‚Üí cost amortizes to zero on repeat views. Acceptable. **SHOULD-FIX (non-blocking):** no per-actor rate limit on the on-view resolve, so a viewer could fan a burst of distinct-coord cache-miss photos into N concurrent Google calls (cost/quota, not a data-leak) ‚Äî bounded by their visible-photo count and the 5s timeout; consider a per-request concurrency cap or relying on the existing async-on-upload worker to pre-resolve so on-view is almost always a cache hit. ‚úÖ
  - DISPOSITION: **PASS.** No BLOCK, no FLAG. Endpoint `case.view`-gated + scope-guarded (`ca.id=$1 AND ca.case_id=$2 AND kind='FIELD_PHOTO' [+task-scope leg]`) ‚Üí out-of-scope/cross-case/absent ‚â° 404 (IDOR-safe, no oracle); OFFICE_REF unreachable (kind pin); UUIDs regex-validated pre-query, every SQL value bound, lat/lng number-typed+range-checked, Google key server-side-only (never to client, never logged/in returned URL), response is `{address,cached}` only (coords not echoed); address frozen NULL‚Üíaddress by a DB BEFORE-UPDATE trigger + app NULL-guard + write-once cache (no overwrite path; only one SET site); on-view resolve is cache-first, ‚â§1 Google call per unresolved photo, 5s timeout, null-degrade. 4 integration tests green (resolve‚Üífreeze‚Üícached, null-degrade, no-coords-no-call, 404 IDOR). **DON'T-REGRESS:** keep `kind='FIELD_PHOTO'` on BOTH the read and the write-through (else OFFICE_REF becomes geocodable / a verdict doc's address could be set); keep the freeze trigger + the `reverse_geocoded_address IS NULL` write-guard (the address is verification evidence ‚Äî any new UPDATE path that touches the column must preserve the NULL‚Üíonce invariant, and the trigger must stay attached); NEVER return the Google request URL / key / raw coords to the client (response stays `{address,cached}`); keep the geocode key reads server-side only (ADR-0040); when the on-view resolve gets hot, prefer pre-resolving via the async worker over removing the cache-first short-circuit. **OPEN (carried):** field-photo geo (coord + resolved address) is internal-staff PII at `case.view` tier ‚Äî same audience-widening watch as the prior case-detail/field-report PII items: if `case.view` ever extends to an external/client-portal audience, re-evaluate exposing precise GPS + street address.
