## 2026-06-17 ‚Äî async reverse-geocode + DLQ ops endpoints (S4 Slice B) ‚Äî PASS
> ‚öÝÔ∏è CTO-conducted (Security seat) ‚Äî panel subagent dispatch 529-Overloaded (platform outage). Re-spawn to ratify.

New: system async geocode queue/worker + `GET /api/v2/geocode/dlq` + `POST /api/v2/geocode/dlq/replay` (both authorize(SYSTEM_VIEW)); on-upload enqueue internal.
1. **AuthZ ‚Äî PASS:** both DLQ endpoints SYSTEM_VIEW (page.system, SA/ops); LIVE-verified FIELD_AGENT‚Üí403, SA‚Üí200. No unauth path.
2. **No new IDOR ‚Äî PASS:** processor is a SYSTEM job keyed by server-derived attachmentId; resolves a photo's OWN stored coords + writes only that photo's address; cannot cross records. enqueue only ever called with server ids (verification-tasks upload after insert + DLQ replay over server rows) ‚Äî never a client-supplied id.
3. **PII ‚Äî PASS:** DLQ stores attachment_id+lat/lng+error, gated SYSTEM_VIEW; Google key server-side only; not logged beyond attachmentId+error msg.
4. **Injection ‚Äî PASS:** DLQ SQL parameterized; replay iterates server rows; no request-data interpolation.
5. **Evidence integrity ‚Äî PASS:** async write is the same NULL-guarded freeze-safe path as Slice A; BEFORE-UPDATE trigger blocks any rewrite; worker cannot overwrite a frozen address.
6. **DoS ‚Äî PASS:** enqueue bounded by an authed agent's own ‚â§10 photos/upload; replay SA-only.
**PASS.** Carry (from Slice A, unchanged): field-photo geo PII at case.view tier ‚Äî re-eval if case.view widens to external/client audience. OPEN: re-spawn post-outage.

## 2026-06-17 ‚Äî CASE_REPORT assembly engine + `/preview` endpoint (S5 Slice 1, ADR-0041) ‚Äî PASS

New: `apps/api/src/modules/caseReports/{repository,service,controller}.ts` + `GET /api/v2/cases/:id/report/preview` (cases/routes.ts:63) + mig `0066_case_report_layouts.sql` + SDK `packages/sdk/src/caseReports.ts`. Returns the Zod-typed `CaseReportContext` JSON the slice 2/4/5 renderers will run against.

1. **RBAC + IDOR ‚Äî PASS.** Route gated `authorize(PERMISSIONS.CASE_VIEW)` (routes.ts:63) ‚Äî same gate as `GET /cases/:id`; default-deny preserved. Controller (controller.ts:7-9) throws `AppError.unauthenticated()` when `req.auth` is missing ‚Äî no anonymous path. Service calls `caseRepository.findById(caseId, scope)` (service.ts:29) ‚Üí out-of-scope returns null ‚Üí 404 `CASE_NOT_FOUND` (service.ts:30); IDOR-safe via the existing `caseScopePredicate` (cases/repository.ts:493-499, "out-of-scope case resolves to null"). UUID regex `^[0-9a-f]{8}-[0-9a-f]{4}-[0-9a-f]{4}-[0-9a-f]{4}-[0-9a-f]{12}$/i` (service.ts:10, :26) rejects malformed ids before DB.
2. **Scope on photos ‚Äî PASS.** `caseReportRepository.listPhotosForReport` (repository.ts:25) uses `taskScopePredicate(params, scope)` via an `EXISTS(SELECT 1 FROM case_tasks ct JOIN cases cs ‚Ä¶ WHERE ct.id=ca.task_id AND <pred>)` leg (repository.ts:29-33). Out-of-scope photos silently disappear (not 403/404) ‚Äî same shape as cases.repository.listFieldPhotos. SUPER_ADMIN / no-cap actors ‚Üí empty pred ‚Üí no leg ‚Üí all photos visible (correct).
3. **Injection ‚Äî PASS.** All values parameter-bound: `[caseId]` then `taskScopePredicate` appends to the same `params` array (repository.ts:26-29). `userName`/`caseTrigger` use bound `$1` (repository.ts:49, :57). No `ORDER BY` interpolation (`ORDER BY ca.created_at ASC` is a literal, repository.ts:41). No `${request}` anywhere in SQL strings.
4. **PII surface ‚Äî PASS (no new exposure).** Context exposes customerName/customerPhone/panNumber/applicants[].{name,mobile,pan,applicantType}/photo geo (lat/lng/accuracy/reverseGeocodedAddress) ‚Äî all ALREADY surfaced under `case.view` by `GET /cases/:id` (cases/repository.ts CASE_VIEW_SELECT + applicants + tasks + field-photos endpoints, Slice A address freeze). No new column added; same audience (case.view holders). Standing carry from Slice A unchanged.
5. **Presigned URL ‚Äî PASS (no new sink).** `getStorage().signedUrl(row.storageKey)` (service.ts:43) is the **existing** primitive used by `attachmentUrl` (cases/service.ts:519). Default TTL is the storage provider's; not freshly leaked here. Storage key is server-internal; only the signed URL leaves (repository.ts comment 4-6 explicit).
6. **Output-encoding ‚Äî PASS for Slice 1.** Returns JSON; `res.json` escapes by JSON serialization rules. No HTML construction in this slice ‚Äî narrative/sections pass through unchanged (correct: encoding is the renderer's job per ADR-0041 ¬ß7, lint gate over `{{{raw}}}` lands in Slice 2). No `{{{` triple-stash anywhere in the slice.
7. **DPDP / deleted_at ‚Äî PASS.** `WHERE ca.case_id=$1 AND ca.kind='FIELD_PHOTO' AND ca.deleted_at IS NULL` (repository.ts:40) ‚Äî erased photos never leak. `kind='FIELD_PHOTO'` discriminator prevents pulling DOCUMENT/SIGNATURE evidence into the report (correct narrow surface).
8. **Mig 0066 ‚Äî PASS.** No new table, no new permission, only `ALTER report_layouts ADD COLUMN IF NOT EXISTS page_size/page_orientation` + widened `kind` CHECK + replacement `chk_report_layouts_shape` CHECK (mig:11-40). Fail-closed: CASE_REPORT row without `template_body`/valid `page_size`/`page_orientation` is rejected by the DB (mig:29-33); cannot insert a Designer-saved layout that the renderer would blank-render. The existing `uq_report_layouts_active` partial-unique already collapses CASE_REPORT to one active per (client, product) via `COALESCE(verification_type,'')` (mig:42-44). Forward-only, idempotent, BEGIN/COMMIT wrapped.
9. **Authn ‚Äî PASS.** `actor(req)` throws `AppError.unauthenticated()` on missing `req.auth` (controller.ts:7); same as every other case route.

**SHOULD-FIX (non-blocking):** `caseTrigger` runs a separate `SELECT trigger FROM case_tasks WHERE case_id=$1 ORDER BY created_at ASC LIMIT 1` (repository.ts:55-60) ‚Äî could be pulled from `detail.tasks[0]` to avoid an extra round-trip. Performance, not security. Flag for Perf auditor.

**Confirmations:** Single-layer result column reads (`case_tasks.verification_outcome` via `detail.tasks[].verificationOutcome`, `cases.verification_outcome` via `detail.verificationOutcome`) ‚Äî no FE-mutable column read (service.ts:72, 139). Per-task `narrative`/`sections` come from `fieldReportService.render` which is itself `case.view`-gated. `getStorage().signedUrl` runs per photo serially (`await` in loop, service.ts:43) ‚Äî Perf concern not security.

**OPEN (carried):** standing rule reaffirmed for slices 2/4/5 ‚Äî PDF renderer MUST set Handlebars `noEscape:false`, lint gate `{{{` on template_body at save, docx via `TextRun` only, xlsx via `escapeFormulaCell`. The plain-text passthrough in Slice 1 is correct ONLY IF every renderer encodes at its sink boundary.

**VERDICT: PASS.** No BLOCK. Carry from prior slices: field-photo geo PII at case.view tier ‚Äî re-eval if case.view widens to external audience.

## 2026-06-17 ‚Äî CASE_REPORT HTML render engine + `GET /:id/report.html` (S5 Slice 2a, ADR-0041) ‚Äî PASS ¬∑ OUTPUT-ENCODING INVARIANT MET

FIRST HTML sink for plain-text FIELD_REPORT narratives + case data. Central question ‚Äî **can any user-controlled value reach rendered HTML un-escaped? NO.** Audited every sink; output-encoding (ADR-0041 ¬ß2/¬ß7 BLOCK-level) is **MET**.

1. **Auto-escape ON ‚Äî PASS.** `Handlebars.create()` (render.ts:19); `hb.compile(body, { strict:false })` (render.ts:171) ‚Äî NO `noEscape:true` (contrast the FIELD_REPORT engine). `{{var}}` HTML-escapes by engine default. Compile call passes `allowProtoProperties/MethodsByDefault:false` (render.ts:173-174) ‚Äî prototype-access defence-in-depth.
2. **`nl2br` helper ‚Äî PASS.** `Handlebars.escapeExpression(...)` FIRST, THEN `.replace(/\r?\n/g,'<br>')`, then `SafeString` (render.ts:30-31). Escape precedes any markup ‚Üí a narrative `<script>`/literal `<br>` becomes `&lt;script&gt;`/`&lt;br&gt;`; only the engine-inserted `<br>` is real markup. Cannot inject. Test asserts `line1<br>&lt;script&gt;alert(3)&lt;/script&gt;` (render.test.ts:113).
3. **`badge` helper ‚Äî PASS.** `<span class="badge">${escapeExpression(s)}</span>` (render.ts:163). Input lands in the TEXT node only; the class attr is a static literal (no interpolation) ‚Üí no attribute injection.
4. **DEFAULT template ‚Äî PASS.** Zero `{{{` triple-stash (grep + test render.test.ts:135-137). Every value is `{{ }}` / `orDash` / `fmtDate` / `nl2br` / `badge`. Photo `<img src="{{url}}">` (render.ts:137) is `{{ }}`-escaped ‚Üí breakout `x" onerror=‚Ä¶` ‚Üí `x&quot; onerror‚Ä¶`; test render.test.ts:117-123 asserts `&quot;` present, `onerror="alert(4)"` absent. Name/narrative/section XSS test render.test.ts:97-115 (`=`‚Üí`&#x3D;` too). **All 5 render tests PASS (verified: `vitest run render.test.ts` ‚Üí 5 passed).**
5. **Admin-layout path ‚Äî PASS + confirmed INERT until Slice 3.** `renderCaseReportHtml(ctx, layoutBody)` compiles an admin body the SAME way (autoescape ON) ‚Äî even a `{{{`-bearing admin body escapes its `{{ }}` values; only a literal triple-stash would raise raw, and the `{{{`-reject lint gate lands in Slice 3. **Gate timing is FINE because the create path cannot insert a CASE_REPORT body today:** `CreateReportLayoutSchema.superRefine(refineFieldReport)` (sdk/reportLayouts.ts:271-283) rejects any non-FIELD_REPORT kind carrying `templateBody` ‚Üí 400 "templateBody is only for FIELD_REPORT" (reportLayouts.ts:262-267). A CASE_REPORT `template_body` can therefore only arrive via direct SQL. Schema also yields no page_size/page_orientation, so a bodyless CASE_REPORT row ‚Üí `layoutBody:null` (service.ts:120-129,183) ‚Üí built-in default. Admin sink is inert through the API until Slice 3 ships create/update + the lint gate.
6. **RBAC / scope ‚Äî PASS.** `GET /:id/report.html` gated `authorize(PERMISSIONS.CASE_VIEW)` (cases/routes.ts:65) ‚Äî same gate as `/preview` and `GET /:id`. Reuses the Slice-1 `assemble()` (service.ts:34) ‚Üí `caseRepository.findById(caseId, scope)` ‚Üí out-of-scope null ‚Üí 404 IDOR-safe; UUID-gated before DB (service.ts:46). Controller throws `unauthenticated()` on missing auth (controller.ts:7).
7. **FE blob path ‚Äî PASS.** `apiBlob` fetches with bearer token; `URL.createObjectURL(blob)` ‚Üí `blob:` opaque/null origin (no cookie/same-origin DOM access); `window.open(url,'_blank','noopener')` (CaseDetailPage.tsx:1673-1675) ‚Äî no `window.opener` handle, no reverse-tabnab. No `dangerouslySetInnerHTML`/`innerHTML` ‚Äî server HTML never injected into the app DOM; renders in its own document. Acceptable.
8. **Content-Type ‚Äî PASS.** `res.type('html').send(html)` (controller.ts:29) ‚Üí text/html on an escaped payload (the only safe combination, satisfied by the engine).

**SHOULD-FIX (non-blocking, defence-in-depth):** the `report.html` response sets no `X-Content-Type-Options: nosniff` / restrictive CSP header. Not exploitable today (payload is correctly escaped + Content-Type is text/html + opens in a null-origin blob, not the app origin), but when Slice 2b/Designer widen the surface a `nosniff` + `Content-Security-Policy: default-src 'none'; img-src https:` on this endpoint would harden it. Flag to Principal/SRE for the header pass; NOT a Slice-2a blocker.

**DISPOSITION: PASS ‚Äî output-encoding invariant MET.** No user-controlled value can reach the rendered HTML un-escaped: auto-escape ON, no triple-stash in the default, both SafeString helpers escape-before-markup, attribute sinks escaped, admin raw-body path inert until the Slice-3 lint gate. No BLOCK, no FLAG. Carry: Slice 3 MUST land the `{{{`-reject lint gate on `template_body` save BEFORE any CASE_REPORT create/update API path is enabled.

## 2026-06-17 ‚Äî async CASE_REPORT PDF job + `POST /:id/report` enqueue + Puppeteer `htmlToPdf` (S5 Slice 2b, ADR-0041) ‚Äî PASS ¬∑ SSRF CLEARED ¬∑ `--no-sandbox` ACCEPTED

NEW: `platform/pdf/index.ts` (Puppeteer wrapper), `modules/caseReports/job.ts` (processor). MODIFIED: `caseReports/{service,controller}.ts` (enqueue gate + nosniff), `cases/routes.ts:67`, `platform/jobs/index.ts` (CASE_REPORT type). REUSED unchanged: `modules/jobs/service.ts` resultUrl (own-job-only presigned download). Mig 0067 widens `chk_jobs_type`. ADR shifted from synchronous streaming (¬ß6) to async job + presigned artifact ‚Äî audited the new shape.

1. **RBAC + scope (IDOR) ‚Äî PASS.** `POST /:id/report` gated `authorize(PERMISSIONS.CASE_VIEW)` (routes.ts:67) ‚Äî same gate as `/preview` + `report.html`; default-deny preserved. `enqueueReport` (service.ts:56-62): UUID-gates `caseId` ‚Üí `resolveScope(actor)` ‚Üí `caseRepository.caseVisible(caseId, scope)` (repository.ts:1212) ‚Üí out-of-scope ‚áí 404 `CASE_NOT_FOUND` (service.ts:59) ‚Äî fail-fast at enqueue, IDOR-safe (user gets 404 not a FAILED job). The WORKER re-resolves the SAME scope via `assemble()‚ÜífindById(scope)` (job.ts:29 ‚Üí service.ts:72-75) ‚Üí defence-in-depth: a tampered payload still 404s in the worker. Confirmed no per-task scope hole ‚Äî photos go through `listPhotosForReport` (slice-1 taskScopePredicate).
2. **Actor in payload ‚Äî SAFE (not user-supplied).** `actor` is built ONLY from `req.auth` in the controller (`controller.ts:7-9`, `{ role: req.auth.role, userId: req.auth.userId }`) and threaded service‚Üí`CaseReportJobPayload`‚Üíworker (service.ts:60, job.ts:26). Grepped the enqueue path: NO read of `req.body`/`req.query`/`req.params` for role or userId. The actor is server-authoritative; a client cannot inject a privileged role or another user's id into the job.
3. **Output-encoding (inherited from 2a) ‚Äî PASS, UNCHANGED.** `job.ts:32` calls `renderCaseReportHtml(context, layoutBody)` ‚Äî the SAME auto-escaped engine confirmed MET in the 2a entry. `pdf/index.ts` adds ZERO interpolation: `htmlToPdf(html)` only calls `page.setContent(html, {waitUntil:'load'})` (index.ts:89) + `page.pdf(...)` ‚Äî no template, no string concatenation, the only dynamic inputs to `page.pdf` are the whitelisted `PAPER[pageSize]` enum + boolean `landscape`. XSS posture is byte-identical to 2a. No new sink.
4. **SSRF ‚Äî CLEARED (no BLOCK).** `setContent(...waitUntil:'load')` DOES make Chromium fetch resources during render. The ONLY network sink in the template is `<img src="{{url}}">` (render.ts:141). `{{url}}` = `storage.signedUrl(row.storageKey)` (service.ts:89) ‚Üí `getSignedUrl(client, GetObjectCommand{Bucket, Key})` (storage/index.ts:104-108): the host is the FIXED configured S3/MinIO endpoint+bucket; `Key` = `row.storageKey`, a server-assigned object path from the field-photo upload pipeline ‚Äî NOT request input. **No user-controlled value becomes a Chromium-fetched URL.** Cross-checked the two free-text geo fields: `reverseGeocodedAddress` (render.ts:144) and `address` (render.ts:129) render as `{{ }}`-escaped TEXT nodes only ‚Äî never an `href`/`src`. An attacker-supplied `<img src=http://169.254.169.254/...>` inside a narrative is HTML-escaped by the 2a invariant ‚Üí inert text, not a fetched tag. SSRF surface = none beyond our own object store.
5. **`--no-sandbox` ‚Äî ACCEPTED HERE (FLAG to SRE for container hardening).** `pdf/index.ts:35` launches with `--no-sandbox --disable-setuid-sandbox --disable-dev-shm-usage` ‚Äî standard container flags that DO disable Chromium's process sandbox. Risk model: the sandbox protects the host from a Chromium RCE driven by hostile *content*. Here the content is OUR OWN server-rendered, output-encoded static HTML (`setContent` of a fixed string, no remote document/URL navigation), and the only remote fetch is our own presigned object-store images (item 4). With no attacker-controlled markup, script, or navigation reaching Chromium, the residual exploit path is a zero-day in Chromium's image decoder triggered by a malicious stored *photo byte stream* ‚Äî narrow, and the worker runs as an unprivileged process. ACCEPTABLE for this trusted-input renderer. Defence-in-depth FLAG (non-blocking) to Reliability/SRE: run the worker container as non-root with a seccomp profile (e.g. Chrome's seccomp json) so a hypothetical decoder escape stays jailed even without the Chromium sandbox.
6. **Artifact access ‚Äî PASS.** Stored at `case-reports/${actor.userId}/${jobId}.pdf` (job.ts:41) ‚Äî userId-prefixed key (defence-in-depth). Downloaded via `jobs.resultUrl(userId, id)` ‚Üí `jobRepository.getOwned(id, userId)` = `WHERE id=$1 AND created_by=$2` (repository.ts:67-72) ‚Üí another user's job ‚áí null ‚áí 404. User A CANNOT fetch user B's report job. The presigned URL itself is unguessable + TTL-bound (`S3_SIGNED_URL_TTL_S`). Cross-user artifact access: impossible.
7. **SQL ‚Äî PASS.** Mig 0067 only `DROP/ADD CONSTRAINT chk_jobs_type CHECK (type IN (‚Ä¶'CASE_REPORT'))` (BEGIN/COMMIT, forward-only) ‚Äî no injection surface. Enqueue inserts via `jobRepository.insert` ‚Üí `INSERT INTO jobs (type, payload, created_by) VALUES ($1, $2::jsonb, $3)` (repository.ts:22-26) ‚Äî fully parameterized; payload is `JSON.stringify`'d to jsonb. No raw interpolation anywhere on the path.
8. **nosniff (2a carry RESOLVED) ‚Äî PASS.** `report.html` now sets `res.setHeader('X-Content-Type-Options', 'nosniff')` (controller.ts:31) before `res.type('html').send` ‚Äî the 2a SHOULD-FIX is closed.

**FLAG (non-blocking, PII retention ‚Äî ADR-0021):** the generated PDF carries the full case.view PII tier (customer/applicant name¬∑mobile¬∑PAN, photo geo) and now PERSISTS in object storage at `case-reports/{userId}/{jobId}.pdf` with no cleanup. Retention/purge is deferred (ADR-0021). A DPDP erasure of a case must eventually purge its generated reports too, else PII outlives the source. Owner: whoever lands the ADR-0021 retention sweep. Not a Slice-2b blocker.

**DISPOSITION: PASS.** No BLOCK. No IDOR in download (own-job-only `getOwned`), no cross-user artifact access (userId-keyed + owner-scoped result-url), no output-encoding regression (zero new interpolation; 2a engine reused), and **no SSRF** ‚Äî the sole Chromium-fetched URL is our own server-signed object-store image; no user-controlled value reaches a fetchable URL. `--no-sandbox` accepted for this trusted-input-only renderer (SRE container-hardening FLAG). PII-retention FLAG to ADR-0021 owner. **SSRF VERDICT: CLEARED ‚Äî no user-controlled value can become a Chromium-fetched URL.**

## 2026-06-17 ‚Äî CASE_REPORT Designer: create/update API opens to CASE_REPORT + `{{{` lint gate (S5 Slice 3, ADR-0041) ‚Äî üî¥ BLOCK ¬∑ OUTPUT-ENCODING GATE INCOMPLETE (`{{&` evades it)

This slice discharges the standing carry ("the `{{{` lint gate must land at Slice 3 BEFORE any CASE_REPORT create/update API path is enabled") and opens `CreateReportLayoutSchema`/`UpdateReportLayoutSchema` to CASE_REPORT bodies. The gate as built is **server-authoritative and correctly placed, but its regex is INCOMPLETE** ‚Äî it bans triple-stash `{{{` but NOT Handlebars' ampersand raw form `{{& }}`, which is an identical un-escaped output sink. **This re-opens the stored-XSS hole the gate exists to close.**

1. **üî¥ BLOCK ‚Äî the lint gate misses `{{& }}` (Handlebars' OTHER raw-output form).** `TRIPLE_STASH_RE = /\{\{\{/` (sdk/reportLayouts.ts:234) applied via `templateBodySchema.refine` (reportLayouts.ts:235-242) to BOTH Create (`templateBody: templateBodySchema.nullish()`, reportLayouts.ts:300) and Update (`templateBody: templateBodySchema.optional()`, reportLayouts.ts:316). The regex catches `{{{x}}}` but NOT `{{& x}}` / `{{&x}}`. **Empirically confirmed** against the pinned `handlebars@4.7.9` (the version `render.ts` uses): with `ctx.x='<script>alert(1)</script>'`, `hb.compile('{{x}}')` ‚Üí `&lt;script&gt;‚Ä¶` (escaped, safe) but `hb.compile('{{& x}}')` AND `hb.compile('{{&x}}')` BOTH ‚Üí `<script>alert(1)</script>` (RAW, identical to `{{{x}}}`). And `/\{\{\{/.test('{{& x}}')` === **false** ‚Üí the gate passes it. So an admin can author `{{& case.customerName}}` (or `{{& narrative}}`, any user-controlled context value) and the un-escaped value flows straight into the rendered HTML ‚Üí into Puppeteer `setContent` (Slice 2b) ‚Üí into the PDF. The renderer's auto-escape (`noEscape:false`, render.ts:64) does **NOT** save this: `{{&` is a template-LEVEL escape-opt-out, evaluated regardless of the engine-level escape setting (same as `{{{`). The lint gate is therefore the ONLY control standing between an admin-authored body and a raw-output sink ‚Äî and it has a hole. **FIX: widen the gate to also reject the ampersand form, e.g. `/\{\{\{|\{\{\s*&/` (or `/\{\{[{&]/` after collapsing optional whitespace), and add a `{{& userField}}` rejection test to BOTH `reportLayouts.test.ts` and the api test.** This is a one-line regex change but it is a BLOCK because without it the slice's stated security objective (no raw-output sink over user-controlled case data) is not met.

2. **Gate placement / server-authority ‚Äî PASS (this part is right).** The gate is a Zod `.refine` on the shared `templateBodySchema`, wired into BOTH write schemas; the service calls `CreateReportLayoutSchema.parse` (service.ts:101) and `UpdateReportLayoutSchema.parse` (service.ts:106) ‚Üí ZodError ‚áí 400. A crafted request bypassing the FE still hits the schema ‚Üí cannot smuggle a banned body. The FE mirror `hasTripleStash = /\{\{\{/.test(templateBody)` (ReportLayoutsPage.tsx:145) only disables Save + shows a warning (tsx:463-465) ‚Äî UX-only, correctly NOT the authority. **NOTE:** the FE mirror shares the SAME incomplete regex, so once the server regex is widened, mirror tsx:145 must be widened identically (else FE lets the user Save a body the server then 400s ‚Äî cosmetic, but fix together).

3. **Other raw-output / evasion vectors ‚Äî assessed, no further hole beyond item 1.** Handlebars raw output is reachable ONLY via `{{{...}}}` and `{{& ...}}` (and `{{{{raw-block}}}}`, which starts with `{{{` so it IS caught). Helper-emitted SafeString is not template-authorable (the helper set ‚Äî `eq/nl2br/orDash/fmtDate/badge`, render.ts:26-57 ‚Äî is fixed in code; `nl2br`/`badge` escape-before-markup, audited PASS in the 2a entry). Partials/`registerHelper` are not exposed to template authors. So `{{&` is the single missing case; closing it makes the gate complete.

4. **RBAC ‚Äî PASS, CASE_REPORT gated identically.** All report-layout write routes mount `report_template.manage` (SUPER_ADMIN-only; routes.ts:7 comment + verified perm is SUPER_ADMIN-exclusive). CASE_REPORT create/update is NOT specially exempted ‚Äî same gate as DATA_ENTRY/MIS/FIELD_REPORT. Default-deny intact; no new route, no weakened gate.

5. **Page-geometry persistence (`page_size`/`page_orientation`) ‚Äî PASS, no injection.** Both are `z.enum(REPORT_PAGE_SIZES)` / `z.enum(REPORT_PAGE_ORIENTATIONS)` (reportLayouts.ts:302-303,317-318) ‚Üí only `'A4'|'LETTER'|'LEGAL'` / `'portrait'|'landscape'` survive parse (api test asserts `pageSize:'A3'`‚Üí400, `pageOrientation:'sideways'`‚Üí400). Persisted as bound params: INSERT `$7,$8` (repository.ts:181-192), UPDATE `COALESCE($5,‚Ä¶)/COALESCE($6,‚Ä¶)` (repository.ts:242-253) ‚Äî never interpolated. The whole insert/update path is fully parameterized (`$1..$N`, options/validation `::jsonb` via `JSON.stringify`). No injection surface.

6. **`refineLayoutShape` coherence ‚Äî PASS (no new sink).** CASE_REPORT requires templateBody+pageSize+pageOrientation, forbids verificationType+columns (reportLayouts.ts:268-274); mirrors the DB `chk_report_layouts_shape`. `DEFAULT_CASE_REPORT_TEMPLATE` (caseReports.ts:195-298) + the variable catalog moved to the SDK ‚Äî grepped: zero `{{{` AND zero `{{&` in the default body (every value is `{{ }}`/`orDash`/`fmtDate`/`nl2br`/`badge`). The shipped default is clean; the BLOCK is purely the gate's failure to stop a MALICIOUS admin body using `{{&`.

**DISPOSITION: üî¥ BLOCK.** The output-encoding gate is **placed correctly and is server-authoritative**, but **INCOMPLETE**: `TRIPLE_STASH_RE = /\{\{\{/` (sdk/reportLayouts.ts:234) does not reject Handlebars' `{{& }}` ampersand form, which produces byte-identical un-escaped output (empirically confirmed on handlebars@4.7.9). An admin under `report_template.manage` can author `{{& case.customerName}}` to re-open the stored-XSS sink over user-controlled case data ‚Äî the exact threat the gate is meant to close, and auto-escape-ON does not mitigate it (template-level opt-out). **Required fix before merge:** widen the regex to `/\{\{[{&]/` (or equivalent) in BOTH `templateBodySchema` (sdk:234) and the FE mirror (ReportLayoutsPage.tsx:145), and add a `{{& userField}}`-reject test to `reportLayouts.test.ts` + the api test (create AND update). Once the ampersand form is banned, the gate is COMPLETE (item 3: no other author-reachable raw-output path remains). Everything else in the slice ‚Äî RBAC parity, page-geometry enum‚Üíparameterized persistence, server-authoritative `.parse`, clean shipped default ‚Äî is PASS.

## 2026-06-17 ‚Äî RE-CHECK of S5 Slice 3 output-encoding gate fix (ADR-0041) ‚Äî üî¥ STILL-BLOCKED ¬∑ `{{~` whitespace-control prefix EVADES the widened gate

Re-audit of the applied fix against the original BLOCK (2026-06-17, S5 Slice 3, above). The fix lands as prescribed: `RAW_OUTPUT_RE = /\{\{[{&]/` (sdk/reportLayouts.ts:235) now bans BOTH `{{{` and `{{&`, via `templateBodySchema.refine` (reportLayouts.ts:241-244) wired into BOTH `CreateReportLayoutSchema` (templateBody at reportLayouts.ts:302) and `UpdateReportLayoutSchema` (reportLayouts.ts:318) ‚Äî server-authoritative. The FE mirror is widened identically: `hasRawOutput = /\{\{[{&]/.test(templateBody)` (ReportLayoutsPage.tsx:146), UX-only (gates `canSave` at tsx:274 + inline error at tsx:466-472). Tests assert `{{{`, `{{&`, `{{&x`-reject on create AND update + `{{ }}`-accept (reportLayouts.test.ts:150-169; api test reportLayouts.api.test.ts:193-205). **The ORIGINAL hole (`{{&`) is CLOSED.** But the prior entry's item 3 claim ‚Äî "no other author-reachable raw-output path remains" ‚Äî is **FALSE**.

1. **üî¥ STILL-BLOCKED ‚Äî Handlebars whitespace-control prefix `{{~` produces raw output and EVADES `/\{\{[{&]/`.** Handlebars allows a `~` (whitespace-strip) immediately after `{{`, *before* the `{`/`&` raw marker. The regex requires the char after `{{` to be `{` or `&`; with `~` in between it does NOT match. **Empirically confirmed** against the same pinned `handlebars@4.7.9` the renderer uses, with `ctx.x='<b>RAW</b>'`:
   - `{{~& x}}` ‚Üí renders `<b>RAW</b>` (RAW); `/\{\{[{&]/.test('{{~& x}}')` === **false** ‚Üí gate PASSES it.
   - `{{~{x}}}` ‚Üí renders `<b>RAW</b>` (RAW); regex === **false** ‚Üí PASSES.
   - `{{~&x}}` (no space) ‚Üí renders `<b>RAW</b>` (RAW); regex === **false** ‚Üí PASSES.
   - (`{{ ~& x}}` and `{{&~ x}}` are Handlebars Parse errors ‚Üí not exploitable; `~` must be the FIRST char and must precede the raw marker.)
   So an admin under `report_template.manage` can author `{{~& case.customerName}}` (or `{{~{narrative}}}`) and the un-escaped, user-controlled case value flows into the rendered HTML ‚Üí Puppeteer `setContent` ‚Üí PDF. This is the SAME stored-XSS sink the gate exists to close; the widened `/\{\{[{&]/` does not cover it. Both the server gate (sdk:235) AND the FE mirror (tsx:146) share this hole.

2. **FIX: allow the optional `~` between `{{` and the raw marker ‚Äî `RAW_OUTPUT_RE = /\{\{~?[{&]/`.** Verified on handlebars@4.7.9: `/\{\{~?[{&]/` catches all five raw forms (`{{{`, `{{&`, `{{&x`, `{{~&`, `{{~{`, `{{~&x`) while still ACCEPTING normal escaped output and block helpers (`{{ x }}`‚Üífalse, `{{normal}}`‚Üífalse, `{{#each xs}}`‚Üífalse). Apply identically to `templateBodySchema` (sdk/reportLayouts.ts:235) AND the FE mirror (ReportLayoutsPage.tsx:146). Add `{{~& userField}}` + `{{~{userField}}}` reject tests (create AND update) to `reportLayouts.test.ts` and `reportLayouts.api.test.ts`. Update the doc comment (reportLayouts.ts:229-234) to note the `~` variant.

3. **No further evasion beyond the `~` prefix.** Re-swept the Handlebars raw surface: raw output is reachable only via `{{{...}}}`, `{{& ...}}`, the `{{{{raw-block}}}}` form (starts `{{{` ‚Üí caught), and the `~`-prefixed variants of these (item 1). The trailing `~` (`{{x~}}`) is whitespace-only, not raw. Helper-emitted SafeString remains non-authorable (fixed `eq/nl2br/orDash/fmtDate/badge` set in code; no `registerHelper`/partials exposed to authors). `/\{\{~?[{&]/` closes every author-reachable raw path.

**DISPOSITION: üî¥ STILL-BLOCKED.** The fix correctly closes the original `{{&` hole and is server-authoritative with mirrored FE + create/update tests ‚Äî but it is STILL INCOMPLETE: Handlebars' `{{~` whitespace-control prefix yields byte-identical raw output and slips past `/\{\{[{&]/` (empirically confirmed on handlebars@4.7.9: `{{~& case.customerName}}` renders un-escaped). Surviving evasion input: **`{{~& case.customerName}}`** (also `{{~{narrative}}}`, `{{~&x}}`). **Required fix before merge:** change the regex to **`/\{\{~?[{&]/`** in BOTH `templateBodySchema` (sdk/reportLayouts.ts:235) and the FE mirror (ReportLayoutsPage.tsx:146), and add `{{~&`/`{{~{` reject tests (create AND update) to both test files. With that, the gate is COMPLETE (item 3).

## 2026-06-17 ‚Äî FINAL RE-CHECK of S5 Slice 3 output-encoding gate (ADR-0041) ‚Äî ‚úÖ RESOLVED ¬∑ `/\{\{~?[{&]/` closes every author-reachable raw-output path

Third pass, against the two prior BLOCKs (`{{&` missed ‚Üí widened to `/\{\{[{&]/`; then `{{~&`/`{{~{` missed ‚Üí widened to `/\{\{~?[{&]/`). The prescribed fix is now applied and verified server-authoritative + FE-mirrored + tested.

1. ‚úÖ **Gate as built.** `RAW_OUTPUT_RE = /\{\{~?[{&]/` (sdk/reportLayouts.ts:237) wired via `templateBodySchema.refine` (reportLayouts.ts:243-246) into BOTH `CreateReportLayoutSchema` (templateBody, reportLayouts.ts:304) and `UpdateReportLayoutSchema` (reportLayouts.ts:321) ‚Äî server-authoritative `.parse`. FE mirror identical: `hasRawOutput = /\{\{~?[{&]/.test(templateBody)` (ReportLayoutsPage.tsx:147), gating `canSave` (tsx:275) + inline error (tsx:467-472) ‚Äî UX layer only. Doc comment (reportLayouts.ts:229-236) updated to call out the optional `~`.

2. ‚úÖ **Tests assert the `~` variants.** `reportLayouts.test.ts:150-178`: rejects `{{{`, `{{&`, `{{&x`, `{{~&`, `{{~{` on create AND `{{{`/`{{&`/`{{~&` on update; accepts normal `{{ }}`, block helpers, and the ESCAPED `{{~case.customerName}}`. API test `reportLayouts.api.test.ts:193-205`: `{{{ }}}`/`{{& }}`/`{{~& }}` ‚Üí 400 on create + `{{{ }}}`/`{{& }}` ‚Üí 400 on update.

3. ‚úÖ **Adversarial sweep ‚Äî empirically tested EVERY raw form against the regex AND the live engine** (`node` in apps/api, handlebars@4.7.9, ctx `x='<script>...'`):
   - `{{{x}}}`, `{{~{x}}}`, `{{&x}}`, `{{& x}}`, `{{~& x}}` ‚Üí all render RAW, all `caught=true`. ‚úÖ
   - `{{{{raw}}}}` raw-block opener ‚Üí starts `{{{` ‚Üí matches `\{\{~?{` ‚Üí `caught=true`. ‚úÖ
   - **SPACE-before-marker (the flagged case): `{{ & x}}`, `{{  &x}}`, `{{~ & x}}`, tab/newline-before-`&` ‚Üí all are Handlebars PARSE ERRORS, NOT raw output.** Handlebars requires the `&`/`{` mutator immediately adjacent to `{{` (optionally after a single `~`); any whitespace in between fails to compile ‚Üí cannot reach the renderer. So `{{ & x}}` being `caught=false` is HARMLESS ‚Äî it is not an author-reachable raw sink. ‚úÖ
   - `{{x}}`, `{{~x}}` (escaped) ‚Üí render HTML-ESCAPED, `caught=false` ‚Äî correctly ALLOWED. ‚úÖ
   - `{{> partial}}` ‚Üí not raw output + no partials registered (compile throws "could not be found"); `{{! }}`/`{{!-- --}}` comments ‚Üí no output. Not sinks. ‚úÖ
   - Helper-emitted SafeString (`eq/nl2br/orDash/fmtDate/badge`) remains non-authorable (fixed code set, no `registerHelper`/partials exposed to authors).

   No author-reachable raw-output form slips `/\{\{~?[{&]/`, and no escaped/block form is falsely rejected.

**DISPOSITION: ‚úÖ RESOLVED.** The output-encoding gate is server-authoritative (`.parse` on create + update), FE-mirrored, and test-covered. `/\{\{~?[{&]/` catches all three real raw forms (`{{{`, `{{&`, `{{{{`) and their `~`-prefixed variants; the only uncaught marker-with-space cases (`{{ & x}}` etc.) are Handlebars parse errors that never render, so they are not a sink. The stored-XSS hole this gate exists to close is CLOSED. No surviving evasion input. The standing Slice-3 BLOCK is cleared.

## 2026-06-17 ‚Äî CASE_REPORT Word/.docx renderer + the CASE_REPORT job `format` param (S5 Slice 4, ADR-0041) ‚Äî ‚úÖ PASS ¬∑ NO SSRF ¬∑ OUTPUT-ENCODING STRUCTURAL ¬∑ NO BLOCK

NEW: `modules/caseReports/docx.ts` (programmatic `docx` builder; `TextRun` for all text, `ImageRun` from `fetchImage(photo.url)` over the network). CHANGED: `job.ts` (format branch pdf|docx, MIME map, `.${format}` key/filename), `service.ts` (`enqueueReport(caseId, format, actor)`), `controller.ts` (`reportFormat(req)` parses/validates `?format=` against `CASE_REPORT_FORMATS`, defaults pdf, 400 on bad). SDK `caseReports.ts` (`CASE_REPORT_FORMATS = ['pdf','docx']`, `CaseReportFormat`) + `client.ts` (`generateReport(caseId, format='pdf')`). Tests: `__tests__/docx.test.ts` (2 ‚Äî verified PASS) + api test (`format=docx`‚Üí`.docx` artifact; `format=exe`‚Üí400).

1. **Output-encoding via docx ‚Äî PASS (structural, not a gate).** docx.ts builds the document PROGRAMMATICALLY from the typed `CaseReportContext` ‚Äî there is NO HTML/Handlebars parse, NO template, NO raw-XML construction. Grepped docx.ts for `{{{`, `SafeString`, `innerHTML`, `String.raw`, `new XML`, backtick-`<w:`, literal `<w:t` ‚Üí **NONE**. EVERY text value reaches the document only through `new TextRun({ text })` (the K/V table `kvRow`, `headerCell`/`cell`, `narrativeParagraphs`, headings, caption, footer ‚Äî all `TextRun`-wrapped; docx.ts:46,48,71,75,99,105,109,145,156,161,167,231). The `docx` package's OOXML serializer entity-encodes text-run content. **Empirically confirmed** against the installed `docx` build: `TextRun({text:'<script>alert(1)</script> & "quote"'})` ‚Üí `word/document.xml` contains `<w:t xml:space="preserve">&lt;script&gt;alert(1)&lt;/script&gt; &amp; &quot;quote&quot;</w:t>` ‚Äî `<`‚Üí`&lt;`, `&`‚Üí`&amp;`, `"`‚Üí`&quot;`; the raw `<script>` tag NEVER appears as live markup. So the plain-text FIELD_REPORT narrative + case fields CANNOT inject ‚Äî this is a genuine STRUCTURAL defense (the TextRun-only construction has no markup-interpretation path to bypass), unlike the Slice-3 Handlebars gate which had to enumerate raw forms. The docx.test assertion `buf.includes('<script>alert(1)</script>') === false` (docx.test.ts:92) is SOUND on two independent grounds: (a) the OOXML serializer entity-encodes the text run, and (b) document.xml is DEFLATE-compressed inside the .docx zip, so the literal substring would not survive even before encoding. The assertion would genuinely fail only if a raw-markup path existed ‚Äî none does. (Note docx.test ASCII-only; full-XML-decode is covered by the empirical probe above.) **No path concatenates a context string into raw XML.**

2. **SSRF on the image fetch ‚Äî CLEARED (re-assessed; SAME posture as the 2b Puppeteer img fetch).** `fetchImage(photo.url)` does `fetch(url)` server-side (docx.ts:84). Traced `photo.url`: the assembly engine sets `photo.url = await storage.signedUrl(row.storageKey)` (service.ts:90) ‚Üí `getSignedUrl(client, GetObjectCommand{ Bucket, Key: key })` (storage/index.ts:104-108) ‚Äî host = the FIXED configured S3/MinIO endpoint+bucket; `Key = row.storageKey`. `storageKey` is **server-assigned at upload**: `attachments/${caseId}/${randomUUID()}.${kind.ext}` (cases/service.ts:498) where `caseId` is a validated UUID, the filename is `randomUUID()`, and `kind.ext` comes from a server-side MIME whitelist ‚Äî the **client never supplies the storage key**. So the URL passed to `fetch()` is entirely server-generated, fixed-host, NOT user-controlled. Cross-checked: NO request input (`req.body`/`req.query`/`req.params`) reaches `photo.url`; the only user-influenced photo fields (`reverseGeocodedAddress`, lat/lng) land in the caption `TextRun` (docx.ts:139-140) ‚Äî escaped text, never a URL. **No user-controlled value reaches `fetch()`.** This is byte-identical to the 2b SSRF clearance (the sole network sink is our own server-signed object-store image). SSRF surface = none beyond our own object store.

3. **fetch hardening ‚Äî PASS (acceptable; one defence-in-depth note).** `fetchImage` wraps `fetch` in a 15s `AbortController` timeout (docx.ts:82-85) + try/catch ‚Üí `null` (docx.ts:90-92) ‚Üí the report degrades to caption-only (never fails the whole job). On `!res.ok` ‚Üí null (docx.ts:86). Redirect handling: `fetch` follows redirects by default; since the URL is our own presigned object-store GET, a malicious redirect would require compromising MinIO/S3 itself ‚Äî out of this threat model. ACCEPTABLE. Defence-in-depth NOTE (non-blocking, matches the spirit of the 2b SRE flag): could pin `fetch(url, { redirect: 'manual' })` to harden against a future object-store-side open-redirect; not required while the host is our own fixed endpoint. No content-length/size cap on the fetched buffer (a hostile stored photo byte stream could be large) ‚Äî DoS-tier, not SSRF; flag to Perf/SRE.

4. **`format` param validation ‚Äî PASS (no injection into the storage key).** `reportFormat(req)` (controller.ts:14-20): `undefined`‚Üí`'pdf'`; a string in `CASE_REPORT_FORMATS` (`['pdf','docx']`) is returned; ANYTHING ELSE ‚Üí 400 `BAD_REQUEST {param:'format'}`. So only the validated enum reaches `enqueueReport` ‚Üí the payload ‚Üí the worker. In job.ts the format keys (a) the storage extension `case-reports/${actor.userId}/${ctx.jobId}.${format}` (job.ts:50), (b) the filename `.${format}` (job.ts:55), and (c) the `MIME` lookup (job.ts:29-32, indexed by the enum) ‚Äî all keyed by the VALIDATED enum, NEVER raw-interpolated user input. A bad/`../`/path-traversal format string (e.g. `?format=../../etc`) is rejected at the controller BEFORE enqueue, so it can never reach the storageKey. api test asserts `format=exe`‚Üí400 (api test:391). **No format-param injection into the storage key.**

5. **RBAC / scope ‚Äî PASS (docx inherits the pdf gate exactly).** There is ONE route `POST /:id/report` gated `authorize(PERMISSIONS.CASE_VIEW)` (cases/routes.ts:67); `?format=` is just a query param, so docx and pdf share the identical gate. `enqueueReport` (service.ts:57-63): UUID-gate ‚Üí `resolveScope(actor)` ‚Üí `caseRepository.caseVisible(caseId, scope)` ‚Üí out-of-scope ‚áí 404 `CASE_NOT_FOUND` (IDOR-safe at enqueue); the WORKER re-resolves the SAME scope via `assemble()‚ÜífindById(scope)` (job.ts:38). Actor is server-built from `req.auth` only (controller.ts:8-11) ‚Äî NOT user-supplied (same as 2b item 2). api test asserts non-uuid‚Üí400, out-of-scope/unknown‚Üí404 (api test:387-394). Default-deny preserved; no docx-specific exemption.

6. **PII ‚Äî PASS (no NEW surface).** The .docx carries the same `case.view`-tier PII as the PDF (customer/applicant name¬∑mobile¬∑PAN, photo geo) and PERSISTS at `case-reports/${actor.userId}/${jobId}.docx` (job.ts:50, userId-prefixed key, own-job-only `getOwned` download ‚Äî same as 2b). Same DPDP-retention carry as the PDF (ADR-0021 purge owner) ‚Äî no NEW PII column, audience, or storage surface introduced by the docx format.

**DISPOSITION: ‚úÖ PASS ‚Äî no BLOCK, no FLAG (beyond two pre-existing carries: ADR-0021 retention purge of generated reports now extends to .docx artifacts; optional `redirect:'manual'` + fetch size-cap defence-in-depth to SRE/Perf).** Output-encoding is STRUCTURAL via TextRun-only construction (no markup parse, no raw-XML path ‚Äî empirically verified the OOXML serializer entity-encodes); the format param is enum-validated before it can touch the storage key; RBAC/scope/actor are inherited unchanged from the shared `enqueueReport`/route. **SSRF VERDICT: CLEARED ‚Äî the sole `fetch()` target is our own server-signed object-store image (`storage.signedUrl(server-assigned storageKey)`); no user-controlled value reaches `fetch()`, identical posture to the 2b Puppeteer img fetch.**

## 2026-06-17 ‚Äî CASE_REPORT Excel/.xlsx renderer + xlsx format branch (S5 Slice 5, ADR-0041) ‚Äî ‚úÖ PASS ¬∑ FORMULA-GUARD COMPLETE ¬∑ NO SSRF ¬∑ NO RAW-XML ¬∑ NO BLOCK

NEW: `modules/caseReports/xlsx.ts` (exceljs 3-sheet workbook + `csvSafe` formula guard) + `__tests__/xlsx.test.ts` (3 ‚Äî verified PASS, `--coverage=false`). CHANGED: `job.ts` (xlsx render branch job.ts:46-47 + MIME `application/vnd‚Ä¶spreadsheetml.sheet` job.ts:33), SDK `caseReports.ts` (`CASE_REPORT_FORMATS = ['pdf','docx','xlsx']` caseReports.ts:12), FE Excel button (CaseDetailPage.tsx:1732-1738 ‚Üí `generate.mutate('xlsx')`). The spreadsheet is a DATA export ‚Äî photos are LISTED/linked, NOT embedded.

1. **üü¢ Formula-injection guard ‚Äî COMPLETE.** `csvSafe(value)` (xlsx.ts:29-32): `/^[=+\-@\t\r]/.test(s) ? `'${s}` : s` ‚Äî prefixes a single quote when the cell starts with `=`/`+`/`-`/`@`/TAB/CR so Excel/Sheets treat it as literal text, never a formula. **Empirically verified the regex == the accepted OWASP lead set** (`= + - @` plus TAB 0x09 / CR 0x0D ‚Äî the two whitespace chars Excel TRIMS then re-evaluates): all 4 chars + `\t=`/`\r=` guarded; LF `\n=` correctly NOT guarded (Excel doesn't trim LF to a lead); ` =x` (leading space) correctly NOT guarded (a leading space already prevents formula eval); mid-string `a=1+1` untouched. No other dangerous lead char exists for the Excel/Sheets engines ‚Äî the 4-char + TAB/CR set is complete.
2. **üü¢ Cell walk ‚Äî EVERY case-controlled string is csvSafe-guarded (no unguarded sink).** Walked all 3 sheets:
   - **Sheet 1 Case Summary:** col-1 keys are STATIC literals (xlsx.ts:43-66, safe); col-2 values ALL routed through `csvSafe(v)` (the single `for‚Ä¶summary.addRow([k, csvSafe(v)])` xlsx.ts:67) ‚Äî covers customerName, customerPhone, panNumber, applicantType, status, verificationOutcome, resultRemark, generatedByName, and the numeric totals (`String(...)`, harmless, still guarded).
   - **Sheet 2 Per-Task:** `taskNumber, unitName, applicantName, address, outcome, remark` ALL `csvSafe(...)` (xlsx.ts:87-92); `completedAt`‚Üí`fmtDate` (ISO `YYYY-MM-DD`, xlsx.ts:93); `photos.length`‚Üínumber.
   - **Sheet 3 Photo Manifest:** `taskNumber, photoType, reverseGeocodedAddress, url` ALL `csvSafe(...)` (xlsx.ts:116,117,121,125); `captureTime`‚Üí`fmtDate` (xlsx.ts:122).
   **No user/case-controlled string is written WITHOUT csvSafe.** Header label rows are static literals (xlsx.ts:41,83,111).
3. **üü¢ Numeric cells are NUMBERS, not formula-injectable strings ‚Äî PASS.** `latitude/longitude/accuracy` are `number | null` in the context type (sdk caseReports.ts:44-46) and written as `p.latitude ?? ''` / `p.longitude ?? ''` / `p.accuracy ?? ''` (xlsx.ts:118-120) ‚Äî a number stays a numeric cell (or `''` empty when null); never coerced to a String, so there is no leading `=`/`+`/`-` to guard. Correct to leave them unguarded.
4. **üü¢ The URL cell ‚Äî TEXT, not a HYPERLINK formula ‚Äî PASS.** `photo.url` (the presigned object-store URL) is written via `csvSafe(p.url)` as a PLAIN-TEXT cell (xlsx.ts:125), NOT an Excel `HYPERLINK()` formula (a formula cell would re-open the injection surface; the inline comment xlsx.ts:123-124 calls this out explicitly). Grepped xlsx.ts for `HYPERLINK`/`formula:`/`.value = {` ‚Äî NONE; no cell is constructed as a formula object. The URL is the SAME time-limited presigned link the tray download + the docx/pdf `<img src>` already use (`storage.signedUrl(server-assigned storageKey)`); it expires (TTL-bound) and the storage key is server-internal. Leaking it into a downloadable spreadsheet is the same exposure as the 2b/4 image src ‚Äî ACCEPTABLE, noted, not a blocker.
5. **üü¢ No markup/raw-XML sink ‚Äî PASS.** exceljs writes cell values through its value API, which XML-encodes content into the OOXML sheet parts ‚Äî there is NO raw-XML construction in xlsx.ts. Grepped for `String.raw`, `innerHTML`, `new XML`, `writeXml`, literal `<w:`/`<x:`/backtick-`<`, formula objects ‚Üí NONE (the only `x:` grep hits are `xlsx`/`ctx` substrings, not XML). No string is concatenated into a sheet XML part.
6. **üü¢ SSRF ‚Äî NONE (no network surface at all) ‚Äî PASS.** Unlike the 2b Puppeteer (`setContent`‚Üífetch) and 4 docx (`fetchImage`) renderers, the xlsx path does NOT fetch images ‚Äî it LISTS the URL as text. Grepped xlsx.ts for `fetch`/`axios`/`XMLHttp`/`http`/`require(` ‚Üí NONE. **Zero network sink ‚Üí zero SSRF surface.** This is the safest of the three renderers.
7. **üü¢ RBAC / scope / actor / format-validation ‚Äî PASS (inherited unchanged from the shared enqueue).** One route `POST /:id/report` gated `authorize(PERMISSIONS.CASE_VIEW)` (cases/routes.ts:67); `?format=` parsed by `reportFormat(req)` (controller.ts:14-19) against `CASE_REPORT_FORMATS` ‚Üí only `'pdf'|'docx'|'xlsx'` survive; anything else ‚Üí 400 `BAD_REQUEST {param:'format'}` (controller.ts:19). The validated enum keys the storage extension/filename/MIME (job.ts:33,54,59) ‚Äî never raw-interpolated. `enqueueReport` UUID-gates ‚Üí `resolveScope` ‚Üí `caseVisible` ‚Üí out-of-scope 404 (IDOR-safe); worker re-resolves the same scope via `assemble()` (job.ts:40). Actor is server-built from `req.auth` only ‚Äî not user-supplied. No xlsx-specific exemption.
8. **üü¢ PII ‚Äî PASS (no NEW surface; one carried note).** The .xlsx carries the same `case.view`-tier PII as the pdf/docx (customer/applicant name¬∑phone¬∑PAN, photo GPS + frozen address) and PERSISTS at `case-reports/${actor.userId}/${jobId}.xlsx` (job.ts:54, userId-prefixed, own-job-only `getOwned` download). The Photo Manifest sheet now lists GPS + address in a SORTABLE/FILTERABLE spreadsheet (easier bulk-exfiltration than a PDF), but every value is ALREADY authorized under `case.view` ‚Äî no new column, audience, or storage surface. Same DPDP-retention carry as pdf/docx (ADR-0021 purge owner now also covers .xlsx artifacts). NOTE, not a blocker.

**DISPOSITION: ‚úÖ PASS ‚Äî no BLOCK, no new FLAG (beyond the carried ADR-0021 retention-purge extension to .xlsx artifacts).** The spreadsheet-specific sink (formula injection) is FULLY guarded: `csvSafe` is applied to every free-text case-controlled cell across all 3 sheets, its `/^[=+\-@\t\r]/` regex matches the complete OWASP lead set (empirically verified), numeric cells are genuine numbers (not formula-injectable), the URL is a TEXT cell (NOT a HYPERLINK formula), there is no raw-XML path (exceljs XML-encodes), and ‚Äî uniquely among the three renderers ‚Äî there is NO `fetch()`, so NO SSRF surface. RBAC/scope/actor/format-validation inherited unchanged from the shared `enqueueReport`/route. All 3 tests PASS.
